File Summary
================================================================

Purpose:
--------
This file contains a packed representation of the entire repository's contents.
It is designed to be easily consumable by AI systems for analysis, code review,
or other automated processes.

File Format:
------------
The content is organized as follows:
1. This summary section
2. Repository information
3. Directory structure
4. Repository files (if enabled)
5. Multiple file entries, each consisting of:
  a. A separator line (================)
  b. The file path (File: path/to/file)
  c. Another separator line
  d. The full contents of the file
  e. A blank line

Usage Guidelines:
-----------------
- This file should be treated as read-only. Any changes should be made to the
  original repository files, not this packed version.
- When processing this file, use the file path to distinguish
  between different files in the repository.
- Be aware that this file may contain sensitive information. Handle it with
  the same level of security as you would the original repository.

Notes:
------
- Some files may have been excluded based on .gitignore rules and Repomix's configuration
- Binary files are not included in this packed representation. Please refer to the Repository Structure section for a complete list of file paths, including binary files
- Files matching patterns in .gitignore are excluded
- Files matching default ignore patterns are excluded
- Code comments have been removed from supported file types
- Empty lines have been removed from all files
- Line numbers have been added to the beginning of each line
- Content has been formatted for parsing in plain style
- Files are sorted by Git change count (files with more changes are at the bottom)

  3:     const allElements = [];
  4:     function processElement(el, parent = null, depth = 0) {
  5:       const tagNameUpper = el.tagName.toUpperCase();
  6:       if (tagNameUpper === 'HTML' || tagNameUpper === 'BODY') {
  7:         const children = [];
  8:         for (let child of el.children) {
  9:           const childData = processElement(child, el, depth);
 10:           if (childData) {
 11:             children.push(childData);
 12:           }
 13:         }
 14:         return children.length > 0 ? { tag: 'BODY', children: children } : null;
 15:       }
 16:       const style = window.getComputedStyle(el);
 17:       const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
 18:       const isImportant = ['IMG', 'SVG', 'CANVAS', 'VIDEO', 'IFRAME', 'TABLE', 'TR', 'TD', 'TH', 'H1', 'H2', 'H3', 'H4', 'H5', 'H6'].includes(tagNameUpper);
 19:       let hasValidSize = rect.height > 0 && rect.width > 0;
 20:       if (!hasValidSize && (tagNameUpper === 'SVG' || tagNameUpper === 'CANVAS')) {
 21:         const attrWidth = el.getAttribute('width');
 22:         const attrHeight = el.getAttribute('height');
 23:         const viewBox = el.getAttribute('viewBox');
 24:         if (attrWidth && attrHeight) {
 25:           const width = parseFloat(attrWidth);
 26:           const height = parseFloat(attrHeight);
 27:           if (width > 0 && height > 0) {
 28:             hasValidSize = true;
 29:           }
 30:         } else if (viewBox) {
 31:           const viewBoxValues = viewBox.split(/[\s,]+/).map(v => parseFloat(v));
 32:           if (viewBoxValues.length >= 4 && viewBoxValues[2] > 0 && viewBoxValues[3] > 0) {
 33:             hasValidSize = true;
 34:           }
 35:         }
 36:       }
 37:       if (style.display === 'none' || (!hasValidSize && !isImportant)) {
 38:         return null;
 39:       }
 40:       let directText = '';
 41:       for (let node of el.childNodes) {
 42:         if (node.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE) {
 43:           const text = node.textContent.trim();
 44:           if (text) {
 45:             directText += text + ' ';
 46:           }
 47:         }
 48:       }
 49:       directText = directText.trim();
 50:       // 先处理子元素，再决定是否记录当前元素
 51:       const children = [];
 52:       for (let child of el.children) {
 53:         const childData = processElement(child, el, depth + 1);
 54:         if (childData) {
 55:           children.push(childData);
 56:         }
 57:       }
 58:       // 检查是否有有意义的子元素
 59:       const hasImportantChildren = children.length > 0;
 60:       // 判断是否需要记录此元素（isImportant 已在前面定义）
 61:       const hasDirectText = directText.length > 0;
 62:       // 安全地获取 className：对于 SVG 元素，className 可能是 SVGAnimatedString，需要使用 .baseVal
 63:       let classNameStr = '';
 64:       if (el.className) {
 65:         if (typeof el.className === 'string') {
 66:           classNameStr = el.className;
 67:         } else if (el.className.baseVal !== undefined) {
 68:           classNameStr = el.className.baseVal;
 69:         } else {
 70:           classNameStr = String(el.className);
 71:         }
 72:       }
 73:       const hasClassName = classNameStr.trim().length > 0;
 74:       const shouldRecord = isImportant || (hasDirectText && !hasImportantChildren) || (!hasDirectText && hasImportantChildren && hasClassName);
 75:       if (!shouldRecord && !hasImportantChildren) {
 76:         return null;
 77:       }
 78:       let actualBottom = rect.bottom;
 79:       if (tagNameUpper === 'IMG') {
 80:         const objectFit = style.objectFit;
 81:         if (objectFit === 'cover' && el.naturalWidth && el.naturalHeight && rect.width && rect.height) {
 82:           const containerRatio = rect.width / rect.height;
 83:           const imageRatio = el.naturalWidth / el.naturalHeight;
 84:           if (imageRatio !== containerRatio && imageRatio < containerRatio) {
 85:             const actualHeight = rect.width / imageRatio;
 86:             actualBottom = rect.top + actualHeight;
 87:           }
 88:         }
 89:       }
 90:       let parentClassNameStr = '';
 91:       if (parent && parent.className) {
 92:         if (typeof parent.className === 'string') {
 93:           parentClassNameStr = parent.className;
 94:         } else if (parent.className.baseVal !== undefined) {
 95:           parentClassNameStr = parent.className.baseVal;
 96:         } else {
 97:           parentClassNameStr = String(parent.className);
 98:         }
 99:       }
100:       const parentInfo = parent ? (parentClassNameStr || parent.id || parent.tagName) : null;
101:       const elementData = {
102:         tag: el.tagName,
103:         top: Math.round(rect.top),
104:         bottom: Math.round(rect.bottom),
105:         actualBottom: tagNameUpper === 'IMG' ? Math.round(actualBottom) : Math.round(rect.bottom),
106:         height: Math.round(rect.height),
107:         width: Math.round(rect.width),
108:         className: classNameStr,
109:         id: el.id || '',
110:         directText: directText || (tagNameUpper === 'IMG' ? (el.alt || 'no alt') : ''),
111:         depth: depth,
112:         parent: parentInfo,
113:         children: children
114:       };
115:       allElements.push(elementData);
116:       return elementData;
117:     }
118:     const root = processElement(document.body);
119:     // 如果root是BODY包装器，返回其第一个子节点作为实际根，否则返回root
120:     if (root && root.tag === 'BODY' && root.children && root.children.length > 0) {
121:       if (root.children.length === 1) {
122:         return root.children[0];
123:       } else {
124:         return { tag: 'ROOT', children: root.children };
125:       }
126:     }
127:     return root;
128:   }
129:   function flattenTree(node, result = []) {
130:     if (!node) return result;
131:     result.push(node);
132:     for (let child of node.children) {
133:       flattenTree(child, result);
134:     }
135:     return result;
136:   }
137:   const tree = buildElementTree();
138:   const flatElements = flattenTree(tree);
139:   const bodyRect = document.body.getBoundingClientRect();
140:   const htmlRect = document.documentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
141:   return {
142:     elements: flatElements,
143:     tree: tree,
144:     bodyHeight: Math.round(bodyRect.height),
145:     htmlHeight: Math.round(htmlRect.height),
146:     viewportHeight: window.innerHeight
147:   };
148: }

 49:     const parts = jsxLoc.split(":");
 50:     const filePath = parts[0] || "";
 51:     const line = Number.parseInt(parts[1] || "0", 10);

 55: function isValidUrl(url) {
 56:     if (!url)
 57:         return false;
 58:     try {
 59:         new URL(url);
 60:         return true;
 61:     }
 62:     catch {
 63:         return url.startsWith("/") || url.startsWith(".");
 64:     }
 65: }
 66: function isSameUrl(url1, url2) {
 67:     return url1 === url2;
 68: }
 69: function findTextInCode(text, code) {
 70:     const results = [];
 71:     let index = 0;
 72:     while (index < code.length) {
 73:         const found = code.indexOf(text, index);
 74:         if (found === -1)
 75:             break;
 76:         results.push({ start: found, end: found + text.length });
 77:         index = found + 1;
 78:     }
 79:     return results;
 80: }
 81: function formatStyleObject(styles) {
 82:     return Object.entries(styles)
 83:         .map(([key, value]) => {
 84:         const needsQuotes = /[\s,]/.test(value) || !value.match(/^[a-zA-Z0-9#.%-]+$/);
 85:         if (needsQuotes) {
 86:             const escapedValue = value.replace(/\\/g, "\\\\").replace(/'/g, "\\'");
 87:             return `${key}: '${escapedValue}'`;
 88:         }
 89:         else {
 90:             // Simple values without quotes (e.g., numeric values for certain properties)
 91:             return `${key}: '${value}'`;
 92:         }
 93:     })
 94:         .join(", ");
 95: }
 96: async function applyComponentChanges(ast, code, magic, source, changes) {
 97:     const updated = {
 98:         src: false,
 99:         href: false,
100:         text: false,
101:         class: false,
102:         style: false,
103:         deleted: false,
104:     };
105:     if (!code)
106:         return updated;
107:     const traverse = (await Promise.resolve().then(() => __importStar(require("@babel/traverse")))).default;
108:     traverse(ast, {
109:         JSXElement({ node }) {
110:             const opening = node.openingElement;
111:             // Match by line number only if column is not provided (0), otherwise match both
112:             const lineMatches = opening.loc?.start.line === source.line;
113:             const columnMatches = source.column === 0 || opening.loc?.start.column === source.column - 1;
114:             if (lineMatches && columnMatches) {
115:                 if (changes.deleted) {
116:                     updated.deleted = applyDeleteChange(magic, node, code);
117:                 }
118:                 if (changes.src) {
119:                     updated.src = applySrcChange(magic, changes.src, node);
120:                 }
121:                 if (changes.href) {
122:                     updated.href = applyHrefChange(magic, changes.href, node);
123:                 }
124:                 if (changes.className) {
125:                     updated.class = applyClassChange(magic, changes.className, node);
126:                 }
127:                 if (changes.textContent) {
128:                     updated.text = applyTextChange(magic, changes.textContent, node, code);
129:                 }
130:                 if (changes.style) {
131:                     updated.style = applyStyleChange(magic, changes.style, node);
132:                 }
133:             }
134:         },
135:     });
136:     return updated;
137: }
138: function applyDeleteChange(magic, node, code) {
139:     if (node.start === null ||
140:         node.end === null ||
141:         node.start === undefined ||
142:         node.end === undefined) {
143:         return false;
144:     }
145:     // Find the start position, including any leading whitespace on the same line
146:     let start = node.start;
147:     let end = node.end;
148:     // Look backwards to find the start of the line or first non-whitespace
149:     while (start > 0 && code[start - 1] !== "\n") {
150:         const char = code[start - 1];
151:         if (char === " " || char === "\t") {
152:             start--;
153:         }
154:         else {
155:             break;
156:         }
157:     }
158:     // If we're at a newline, include it in the deletion
159:     if (start > 0 && code[start - 1] === "\n") {
160:         start--;
161:     }
162:     while (end < code.length && (code[end] === " " || code[end] === "\t")) {
163:         end++;
164:     }
165:     if (end < code.length && code[end] === "\n") {
166:         end++;
167:     }
168:     magic.remove(start, end);
169:     return true;
170: }
171: function applySrcChange(magic, change, node) {
172:     const { original, modified } = change;
173:     if (!isValidUrl(modified) || isSameUrl(original, modified)) {
174:         return false;
175:     }
176:     const src = node.openingElement.attributes.find((attr) => attr.type === "JSXAttribute" && attr.name.name === "src");
177:     if (src?.type === "JSXAttribute") {
178:         if (src.value?.type === "StringLiteral" && src.value.start && src.value.end) {
179:             magic.update(src.value.start, src.value.end, `"${modified}"`);
180:             return true;
181:         }
182:         else if (
183:         src.value?.type === "JSXExpressionContainer" &&
184:             src.value.expression?.type === "StringLiteral" &&
185:             src.value.expression?.start &&
186:             src.value.expression?.end) {
187:             magic.update(src.value.expression.start, src.value.expression.end, `"${modified}"`);
188:             return true;
189:         }
190:     }
191:     return false;
192: }
193: function applyHrefChange(magic, change, node) {
194:     const { original, modified } = change;
195:     if (!isValidUrl(modified) || isSameUrl(original, modified)) {
196:         return false;
197:     }
198:     const href = node.openingElement.attributes.find((attr) => attr.type === "JSXAttribute" && attr.name.name === "href");
199:     if (href?.type === "JSXAttribute") {
200:         if (href.value?.type === "StringLiteral" && href.value.start && href.value.end) {
201:             magic.update(href.value.start, href.value.end, `"${modified}"`);
202:             return true;
203:         }
204:         else if (
205:         href.value?.type === "JSXExpressionContainer" &&
206:             href.value.expression?.type === "StringLiteral" &&
207:             href.value.expression?.start &&
208:             href.value.expression?.end) {
209:             magic.update(href.value.expression.start, href.value.expression.end, `"${modified}"`);
210:             return true;
211:         }
212:     }
213:     return false;
214: }
215: function applyTextChange(magic, change, node, code) {
216:     const original = change.original.trim();
217:     const modified = change.modified.trim();
218:     if (!original)
219:         return false;
220:     const slice = code.slice(node.start ?? 0, node.end ?? 0);
221:     if (findTextInCode(original, slice).length !== 1)
222:         return false;
223:     for (const child of node.children) {
224:         if (child.type === "JSXText") {
225:             const found = findTextInCode(original, child.value);
226:             if (found.length === 1 && child.start) {
227:                 magic.update(child.start + found[0].start, child.start + found[0].end, modified);
228:                 return true;
229:             }
230:         }
231:         else if (
232:         child.type === "JSXExpressionContainer" &&
233:             child.expression?.type === "StringLiteral") {
234:             const found = findTextInCode(original, child.expression.value);
235:             if (found.length === 1 && child.expression.start) {
236:                 magic.update(child.expression.start + found[0].start, child.expression.start + found[0].end, `"${modified.replace(/\n/g, " ")}"`);
237:                 return true;
238:             }
239:         }
240:     }
241:     return false;
242: }
243: function applyClassChange(magic, change, node) {
244:     const { modified } = change;
245:     if (!modified)
246:         return false;
247:     const className = node.openingElement.attributes.find((attr) => attr.type === "JSXAttribute" && attr.name.name === "className");
248:     if (className?.type === "JSXAttribute") {
249:         if (
250:         className.value?.type === "StringLiteral" &&
251:             className.value.start &&
252:             className.value.end) {
253:             magic.update(className.value.start, className.value.end, `"${modified}"`);
254:             return true;
255:         }
256:         else if (
257:         className.value?.type === "JSXExpressionContainer" &&
258:             className.value.expression?.type === "StringLiteral" &&
259:             className.value.expression.start &&
260:             className.value.expression.end) {
261:             magic.update(className.value.expression.start, className.value.expression.end, `"${modified}"`);
262:             return true;
263:         }
264:     }
265:     return false;
266: }
267: function applyStyleChange(magic, styleChanges, node) {
268:     const style = node.openingElement.attributes.find((attr) => attr.type === "JSXAttribute" && attr.name.name === "style");
269:     const newStyles = {};
270:     for (const [property, change] of Object.entries(styleChanges)) {
271:         if (change && change.modified) {
272:             newStyles[property] = change.modified;
273:         }
274:     }
275:     if (Object.keys(newStyles).length === 0) {
276:         return false;
277:     }
278:     if (style?.type === "JSXAttribute") {
279:         if (style.value?.type === "JSXExpressionContainer" &&
280:             style.value.expression?.type === "ObjectExpression" &&
281:             style.value.expression.properties) {
282:             const existingStyles = {};
283:             for (const prop of style.value.expression.properties) {
284:                 if (prop.type === "ObjectProperty" && prop.key?.type === "Identifier") {
285:                     existingStyles[prop.key.name] = prop;
286:                 }
287:             }
288:             let updatedCount = 0;
289:             for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(newStyles)) {
290:                 const existingProp = existingStyles[key];
291:                 if (existingProp && existingProp.value?.start && existingProp.value?.end) {
292:                     const escapedValue = value.replace(/\\/g, "\\\\").replace(/'/g, "\\'");
293:                     magic.update(existingProp.value.start, existingProp.value.end, `'${escapedValue}'`);
294:                     updatedCount++;
295:                     delete existingStyles[key]; // Mark as updated
296:                 }
297:             }
298:             // If we have properties that weren't in the existing object, append them
299:             const newProps = Object.entries(newStyles).filter(([key]) => !existingStyles[key] && newStyles[key]);
300:             if (newProps.length > 0 && style.value.expression.properties.length > 0) {
301:                 const lastProp = style.value.expression.properties[style.value.expression.properties.length - 1];
302:                 if (lastProp.end) {
303:                     const newPropsString = newProps
304:                         .map(([key, value]) => {
305:                         const escapedValue = value.replace(/\\/g, "\\\\").replace(/'/g, "\\'");
306:                         return `${key}: '${escapedValue}'`;
307:                     })
308:                         .join(", ");
309:                     magic.appendLeft(lastProp.end, `, ${newPropsString}`);
310:                     updatedCount += newProps.length;
311:                 }
312:             }
313:             else if (newProps.length > 0 && style.value.expression.properties.length === 0) {
314:                 // Empty style object, insert properties
315:                 const start = style.value.expression.start;
316:                 const end = style.value.expression.end;
317:                 if (start && end) {
318:                     const styleString = formatStyleObject(newStyles);
319:                     magic.update(start, end, `{${styleString}}`);
320:                     return true;
321:                 }
322:             }
323:             return updatedCount > 0;
324:         }
325:         else if (style.value?.start && style.value?.end) {
326:             // Style exists but is not an object expression, replace it
327:             const styleString = formatStyleObject(newStyles);
328:             magic.update(style.value.start, style.value.end, `{{${styleString}}}`);
329:             return true;
330:         }
331:     }
332:     else {
333:         // No style attribute exists - add one
334:         const attributes = node.openingElement.attributes;
335:         const styleString = formatStyleObject(newStyles);
336:         if (attributes.length > 0) {
337:             const lastAttr = attributes[attributes.length - 1];
338:             if (lastAttr.end) {
339:                 magic.appendLeft(lastAttr.end, ` style={{${styleString}}}`);
340:                 return true;
341:             }
342:         }
343:         else {
344:             // No attributes, insert after element name
345:             const nameEnd = node.openingElement.name.end;
346:             if (nameEnd) {
347:                 magic.appendLeft(nameEnd, ` style={{${styleString}}}`);
348:                 return true;
349:             }
350:         }
351:     }
352:     return false;
353: }
354: async function readStdin() {
355:     return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
356:         let data = "";
357:         process.stdin.setEncoding("utf8");
358:         process.stdin.on("data", (chunk) => {
359:             data += chunk;
360:         });
361:         process.stdin.on("end", () => {
362:             resolve(data);
363:         });
364:         process.stdin.on("error", reject);
365:     });
366: }
367: if (require.main === module) {
368:     (async () => {
369:         try {
370:             const input = JSON.parse(await readStdin());
371:             const { code, edits } = input;
372:             if (!code || !Array.isArray(edits)) {
373:                 console.error(JSON.stringify({ error: "Invalid input: code and edits are required" }));
374:                 process.exit(1);
375:             }
376:             const { parse } = await Promise.resolve().then(() => __importStar(require("@babel/parser")));
377:             const ast = parse(code, { sourceType: "module", plugins: ["jsx", "typescript"] });
378:             const magic = new magic_string_1.default(code);
379:             const results = [];
380:             for (const edit of edits) {
381:                 const { line } = parseJsxLoc(edit.element?.jsxLoc || "");
382:                 const updated = await applyComponentChanges(ast, code, magic, { line, column: 0 }, edit.changes || {});
383:                 results.push(updated);
384:             }
385:             const modifiedContent = magic.toString();
386:             const hasChanges = modifiedContent !== code;
387:             console.log(JSON.stringify({ modifiedContent, hasChanges }));
388:         }
389:         catch (error) {
390:             console.error(JSON.stringify({ error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error) }));
391:             process.exit(1);
392:         }
393:     })();
394: }

File: manus-archive-master/runtime_app_data/js/checkElementsBelowHeight.js
================
 1: (checkHeight) => {
 2:   const allElements = document.body.getElementsByTagName('*');
 3:   for (let el of allElements) {
 4:     if (el.tagName === 'HTML' || el.tagName === 'BODY') {
 5:       continue;
 6:     }
 7:     const style = window.getComputedStyle(el);
 8:     const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
 9:     if (style.display !== 'none' &&
10:         style.visibility !== 'hidden' &&
11:         rect.height > 0 &&
12:         rect.width > 0 &&
13:         rect.bottom >= checkHeight) {
14:       const hasDirectText = el.childNodes && Array.from(el.childNodes).some(node =>
15:         node.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE && node.textContent.trim().length > 0
16:       );
17:       const isContentElement = ['H1', 'H2', 'H3', 'H4', 'H5', 'H6', 'P', 'SPAN', 'STRONG', 'EM', 'I', 'B'].includes(el.tagName);
18:       const isImportantElement = ['IMG', 'SVG', 'CANVAS', 'VIDEO', 'IFRAME', 'TABLE', 'TR', 'TD', 'TH'].includes(el.tagName);
19:       let elementBottom = rect.bottom;
20:       if (el.tagName === 'IMG') {
21:         const objectFit = style.objectFit;
22:         if (objectFit === 'cover' && el.naturalWidth && el.naturalHeight && rect.width && rect.height) {
23:           const containerRatio = rect.width / rect.height;
24:           const imageRatio = el.naturalWidth / el.naturalHeight;
25:           if (imageRatio !== containerRatio && imageRatio < containerRatio) {
26:             const actualHeight = rect.width / imageRatio;
27:             elementBottom = rect.top + actualHeight;
28:           }
29:         }
30:       }
31:       if ((hasDirectText || isContentElement || isImportantElement) && elementBottom >= checkHeight) {
32:         return true;
33:       }
34:     }
35:   }
36:   return false;
37: }

  1: ({
  2:   startIndex,
  3:   clickFlagAttr,
  4:   clickIdAttr,
  5: }) => {
  6:   const elements = [];
  7:   let index = startIndex;
  8:   const interactiveTags = new Set(['a', 'button', 'input', 'select', 'textarea', 'summary', 'option', 'canvas']);
  9:   const interactiveRoles = new Set([
 10:     'button',
 11:     'tab',
 12:     'link',
 13:     'checkbox',
 14:     'menuitem',
 15:     'menuitemcheckbox',
 16:     'menuitemradio',
 17:     'radio',
 18:   ]);
 19:   const normalizeText = (value, limit = 120) => {
 20:     if (!value) {
 21:       return '';
 22:     }
 23:     const trimmed = value.replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
 24:     if (!trimmed) {
 25:       return '';
 26:     }
 27:     if (trimmed.length > limit) {
 28:       return `${trimmed.slice(0, limit)}...`;
 29:     }
 30:     return trimmed;
 31:   };
 32:   const buildDescription = (el, tagName, text, inputType) => {
 33:     const hints = [];
 34:     const idValue = normalizeText(el.id, 60);
 35:     if (idValue) {
 36:       hints.push(`id:"${idValue}"`);
 37:     }
 38:     const ariaLabel = normalizeText(el.getAttribute('aria-label') || el.title || '', 80);
 39:     if (ariaLabel) {
 40:       hints.push(`hint:"${ariaLabel}"`);
 41:     }
 42:     const placeholder = normalizeText(el.getAttribute('placeholder') || '', 80);
 43:     if (placeholder) {
 44:       hints.push(`placeholder:"${placeholder}"`);
 45:     }
 46:     const role = normalizeText(el.getAttribute('role') || '', 40);
 47:     if (role) {
 48:       hints.push(`role:"${role}"`);
 49:     }
 50:     if (inputType) {
 51:       hints.push(`type:"${inputType}"`);
 52:     }
 53:     const hintText = hints.length ? `{${hints.join(',')}}` : '{}';
 54:     if (text) {
 55:       return `${tagName} ${hintText} ${text}`.trim();
 56:     }
 57:     return `${tagName} ${hintText}`.trim();
 58:   };
 59:   const getPrimaryText = (el, tagName, inputType) => {
 60:     if (el instanceof HTMLInputElement || el instanceof HTMLTextAreaElement) {
 61:       if (el.value) {
 62:         return normalizeText(el.value);
 63:       }
 64:       if (el.placeholder) {
 65:         return normalizeText(el.placeholder);
 66:       }
 67:     }
 68:     if (tagName === 'option' && el instanceof HTMLOptionElement) {
 69:       return normalizeText(el.innerText || el.textContent || '');
 70:     }
 71:     if (tagName === 'select' && el instanceof HTMLSelectElement) {
 72:       const options = Array.from(el.options || []).slice(0, 5);
 73:       const optionTexts = options
 74:         .map((opt, idx) => {
 75:           const val = normalizeText(opt.textContent || '');
 76:           if (!val) {
 77:             return null;
 78:           }
 79:           return `option#${idx}:${val}`;
 80:         })
 81:         .filter(Boolean);
 82:       if (optionTexts.length) {
 83:         return optionTexts.join(', ');
 84:       }
 85:     }
 86:     const text = normalizeText(el.innerText || el.textContent || '');
 87:     if (text) {
 88:       return text;
 89:     }
 90:     if (inputType === 'submit' || inputType === 'button') {
 91:       return normalizeText(el.value || 'submit');
 92:     }
 93:     return '';
 94:   };
 95:   const isProbablyClickable = (el, tagName) => {
 96:     if (el.hasAttribute(clickFlagAttr)) {
 97:       return true;
 98:     }
 99:     if (interactiveTags.has(tagName)) {
100:       return true;
101:     }
102:     const role = (el.getAttribute('role') || '')
103:       .split(' ')
104:       .map((r) => r.trim().toLowerCase());
105:     if (role.some((r) => interactiveRoles.has(r))) {
106:       return true;
107:     }
108:     const contentEditable = el.getAttribute('contenteditable');
109:     if (contentEditable && contentEditable.toLowerCase() !== 'false') {
110:       return true;
111:     }
112:     return false;
113:   };
114:   const isVisible = (el, rect) => {
115:     if (!rect || rect.width <= 1 || rect.height <= 1) {
116:       return false;
117:     }
118:     const style = window.getComputedStyle(el);
119:     if (style.display === 'none' || style.visibility === 'hidden' || style.visibility === 'collapse') {
120:       return false;
121:     }
122:     if (style.pointerEvents === 'none') {
123:       return false;
124:     }
125:     const opacity = Number.parseFloat(style.opacity || '1');
126:     if (!Number.isNaN(opacity) && opacity <= 0) {
127:       return false;
128:     }
129:     return true;
130:   };
131:   const seen = new Set();
132:   const traverse = (root) => {
133:     const walker = document.createTreeWalker(root, NodeFilter.SHOW_ELEMENT);
134:     let node = walker.nextNode();
135:     while (node) {
136:       if (node instanceof HTMLElement && !seen.has(node)) {
137:         seen.add(node);
138:         const tagName = node.tagName.toLowerCase();
139:         if (isProbablyClickable(node, tagName)) {
140:           const rect = node.getBoundingClientRect();
141:           if (isVisible(node, rect)) {
142:             const inputTypeRaw = tagName === 'input' ? node.getAttribute('type') || 'text' : null;
143:             const inputType = inputTypeRaw ? inputTypeRaw.toLowerCase() : null;
144:             const text = getPrimaryText(node, tagName, inputType);
145:             const description = buildDescription(node, tagName, text, inputType);
146:             node.setAttribute(clickIdAttr, String(index));
147:             elements.push({
148:               index,
149:               x: rect.x,
150:               y: rect.y,
151:               width: rect.width,
152:               height: rect.height,
153:               tag: tagName,
154:               inputType,
155:               description,
156:             });
157:             index += 1;
158:           }
159:         }
160:         if (node.shadowRoot) {
161:           traverse(node.shadowRoot);
162:         }
163:       }
164:       node = walker.nextNode();
165:     }
166:   };
167:   traverse(document);
168:   return {
169:     elements,
170:     nextIndex: index,
171:     viewport: {
172:       width: window.innerWidth || (document.documentElement ? document.documentElement.clientWidth : null),
173:       height: window.innerHeight || (document.documentElement ? document.documentElement.clientHeight : null),
174:       devicePixelRatio: window.devicePixelRatio || 1,
175:     },
176:   };
177: }

================
File: manus-archive-master/runtime_app_data/js/findElementByClickId.js
================
 1: (index) => {
 2:   const attr = 'data-manus_click_id';
 3:   const target = String(index);
 4:   const visited = new Set();
 5:   const MAX_DEPTH = 10;
 6:   const walk = (root, depth = 0) => {
 7:     if (!root || depth > MAX_DEPTH) {
 8:       return null;
 9:     }
10:     const walker = document.createTreeWalker(root, NodeFilter.SHOW_ELEMENT);
11:     let node = walker.nextNode();
12:     while (node) {
13:       if (node instanceof Element && node.getAttribute(attr) === target) {
14:         return node;
15:       }
16:       if (node instanceof Element && node.shadowRoot) {
17:         const found = walk(node.shadowRoot, depth + 1);
18:         if (found) {
19:           return found;
20:         }
21:       }
22:       node = walker.nextNode();
23:     }
24:     return null;
25:   };
26:   const searchFrames = (doc, depth = 0) => {
27:     if (!doc || depth > MAX_DEPTH) {
28:       return null;
29:     }
30:     const foundInDoc = walk(doc, depth);
31:     if (foundInDoc) {
32:       return foundInDoc;
33:     }
34:     const frames = doc.querySelectorAll('iframe, frame');
35:     for (const frame of frames) {
36:       if (!(frame instanceof HTMLIFrameElement || frame instanceof HTMLFrameElement)) {
37:         continue;
38:       }
39:       if (visited.has(frame)) {
40:         continue;
41:       }
42:       visited.add(frame);
43:       try {
44:         const childDoc = frame.contentDocument;
45:         const found = searchFrames(childDoc, depth + 1);
46:         if (found) {
47:           return found;
48:         }
49:       } catch (error) {
50:         continue;
51:       }
52:     }
53:     return null;
54:   };
55:   return searchFrames(document, 0);
56: };

File: manus-archive-master/runtime_app_data/js/nestedScroll.js

  1: async ({
  2:   direction = 'down',
  3:   toEdge = false,
  4:   pixelDelta,
  5:   targetPoint,
  6:   preferLargest = false,
  7:   minViewportRatio = 0,
  8: } = {}) => {
  9:   const validDirections = ['up', 'down', 'left', 'right'];
 10:   if (!validDirections.includes(direction)) {
 11:     return { scrolled: false, reason: 'invalid-direction' };
 12:   }
 13:   const axis = direction === 'left' || direction === 'right' ? 'x' : 'y';
 14:   const dir = direction === 'up' || direction === 'left' ? -1 : 1;
 15:   const isScrollable = (el) => {
 16:     if (!el || !(el instanceof Element)) return false;
 17:     if (el.clientHeight === 0 || el.clientWidth === 0) return false;
 18:     const style = getComputedStyle(el);
 19:     if (style.display === 'none' || style.visibility === 'hidden') return false;
 20:     const scrollableSpace = axis === 'y' ? el.scrollHeight - el.clientHeight : el.scrollWidth - el.clientWidth;
 21:     return scrollableSpace > 1 && Number.isFinite(scrollableSpace);
 22:   };
 23:   const describeElement = (el) => {
 24:     const tag = el.tagName ? el.tagName.toLowerCase() : 'element';
 25:     const idPart = el.id ? `#${el.id}` : '';
 26:     const classList = (el.className || '').toString().trim().split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 2);
 27:     const classPart = classList.length ? `.${classList.join('.')}` : '';
 28:     const ariaLabel = el.getAttribute ? el.getAttribute('aria-label') : null;
 29:     const ariaPart = ariaLabel ? `[aria-label="${ariaLabel.slice(0, 40)}"]` : '';
 30:     return `${tag}${idPart}${classPart}${ariaPart}`;
 31:   };
 32:   const buildPath = (el) => {
 33:     const parts = [];
 34:     let current = el;
 35:     let safety = 0;
 36:     while (current && safety < 8) {
 37:       if (!(current instanceof Element)) break;
 38:       parts.unshift(describeElement(current));
 39:       const root = current.getRootNode ? current.getRootNode() : null;
 40:       if (root && typeof ShadowRoot !== 'undefined' && root instanceof ShadowRoot && root.host && current !== root.host) {
 41:         current = root.host;
 42:       } else {
 43:         current = current.parentElement;
 44:       }
 45:       safety += 1;
 46:     }
 47:     return parts.join(' > ');
 48:   };
 49:   const dedupe = (arr) => {
 50:     const seen = new Set();
 51:     return arr.filter((el) => {
 52:       if (!el || seen.has(el)) return false;
 53:       seen.add(el);
 54:       return true;
 55:     });
 56:   };
 57:   const readPosition = (el) => {
 58:     if (!el) return 0;
 59:     if (el === document.body || el === document.documentElement) {
 60:       const winPos = axis === 'y' ? window.scrollY : window.scrollX;
 61:       if (typeof winPos === 'number' && Number.isFinite(winPos)) return winPos;
 62:     }
 63:     const val = axis === 'y' ? el.scrollTop : el.scrollLeft;
 64:     if (typeof val === 'number' && Number.isFinite(val)) return val;
 65:     return 0;
 66:   };
 67:   const waitForScrollSettle = async (el, before) => {
 68:     const immediate = readPosition(el);
 69:     if (Math.abs(immediate - before) > 1) return immediate;
 70:     await new Promise((resolve) => requestAnimationFrame(resolve));
 71:     const afterFrame = readPosition(el);
 72:     if (Math.abs(afterFrame - before) > 1) return afterFrame;
 73:     await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 50));
 74:     return readPosition(el);
 75:   };
 76:   const getChainFromPoint = () => {
 77:     if (!Array.isArray(targetPoint) || targetPoint.length !== 2) return [];
 78:     const [px, py] = targetPoint;
 79:     const start = document.elementFromPoint(px, py);
 80:     if (!start) return [];
 81:     const chain = [];
 82:     let current = start;
 83:     let safety = 0;
 84:     while (current && safety < 50) {
 85:       if (current instanceof Element) chain.push(current);
 86:       const root = current.getRootNode ? current.getRootNode() : null;
 87:       if (root && typeof ShadowRoot !== 'undefined' && root instanceof ShadowRoot && root.host && current !== root.host) {
 88:         current = root.host;
 89:       } else {
 90:         current = current.parentElement;
 91:       }
 92:       safety += 1;
 93:     }
 94:     return chain;
 95:   };
 96:   const pickLargestScrollable = () => {
 97:     if (!preferLargest) return null;
 98:     const minWidth = Math.max(window.innerWidth * minViewportRatio, 0);
 99:     const minHeight = Math.max(window.innerHeight * minViewportRatio, 0);
100:     const base = [
101:       document.scrollingElement,
102:       document.documentElement,
103:       document.body,
104:     ].filter(Boolean);
105:     const all = dedupe([...base, ...Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('*'))]);
106:     const scored = all
107:       .filter((el) => {
108:         if (!isScrollable(el)) return false;
109:         const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
110:         if (minViewportRatio > 0) {
111:           if (rect.width < minWidth || rect.height < minHeight) return false;
112:         }
113:         return true;
114:       })
115:       .map((el) => {
116:         const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
117:         const scrollableSpace = Math.max(
118:           axis === 'y' ? el.scrollHeight - el.clientHeight : el.scrollWidth - el.clientWidth,
119:           0,
120:         );
121:         const area = Math.max(el.clientWidth, 1) * Math.max(el.clientHeight, 1);
122:         return {
123:           el,
124:           capacity: scrollableSpace * area,
125:         };
126:       })
127:       .sort((a, b) => b.capacity - a.capacity);
128:     return scored.length > 0 ? scored[0].el : null;
129:   };
130:   const resolveTarget = () => {
131:     if (preferLargest) return pickLargestScrollable();
132:     const chain = getChainFromPoint();
133:     for (const el of chain) {
134:       if (isScrollable(el)) return el;
135:     }
136:     return pickLargestScrollable();
137:   };
138:   const target = resolveTarget();
139:   if (!target || !isScrollable(target)) {
140:     const reason = preferLargest && minViewportRatio > 0 ? 'no-large-container' : 'no-scrollable-target';
141:     return { scrolled: false, reason };
142:   }
143:   const before = readPosition(target);
144:   const maxOffset = axis === 'y'
145:     ? Math.max(target.scrollHeight - target.clientHeight, 0)
146:     : Math.max(target.scrollWidth - target.clientWidth, 0);
147:   const boundaryBefore = dir < 0 ? before <= 1 : before >= maxOffset - 1;
148:   let step = axis === 'y' ? target.clientHeight : target.clientWidth;
149:   if (!(typeof step === 'number' && Number.isFinite(step) && step > 0)) {
150:     const fallback = typeof pixelDelta === 'number' && Number.isFinite(pixelDelta) ? pixelDelta : 0;
151:     step = fallback > 0 ? fallback : Math.max(120, Math.round((axis === 'y' ? window.innerHeight : window.innerWidth) * 0.6));
152:   }
153:   const targetPos = toEdge
154:     ? (dir < 0 ? 0 : maxOffset)
155:     : Math.min(Math.max(before + dir * step, 0), maxOffset);
156:   if (axis === 'y') {
157:     if (typeof target.scrollTo === 'function') {
158:       target.scrollTo({ top: targetPos, behavior: 'auto' });
159:     } else {
160:       target.scrollTop = targetPos;
161:     }
162:   } else if (typeof target.scrollTo === 'function') {
163:     target.scrollTo({ left: targetPos, behavior: 'auto' });
164:   } else {
165:     target.scrollLeft = targetPos;
166:   }
167:   const after = await waitForScrollSettle(target, before);
168:   const moved = Math.abs(after - before) > 1;
169:   const atBoundary = dir < 0 ? after <= 1 : after >= maxOffset - 1;
170:   return {
171:     scrolled: moved,
172:     targetDescription: describeElement(target),
173:     path: buildPath(target),
174:     before,
175:     after,
176:     atBoundary,
177:     boundaryBefore,
178:     maxOffset,
179:   };
180: };

 1: async ({ direction, toEdge, delta }) => {

 3:   const dir = direction === 'up' || direction === 'left' ? -1 : 1;
 4:   const root = document.scrollingElement || document.documentElement || document.body;
 5:   if (!root) return { ok: false, reason: 'no-root' };
 6:   const readPosition = (el) => {

 9:       const winPos = axis === 'y' ? window.scrollY : window.scrollX;

13:     if (typeof val === 'number' && Number.isFinite(val)) return val;
14:     return 0;
15:   };
16:   const waitForScrollSettle = async (el, beforePos) => {

18:     if (Math.abs(immediate - beforePos) > 1) return immediate;

20:     const afterFrame = readPosition(el);

32:     : (typeof root.clientWidth === 'number' && root.clientWidth > 0 ? root.clientWidth : window.innerWidth);

41:     } else {

43:     }
44:   } else if (typeof root.scrollTo === 'function') {

54:   if (root === document.body) targetDescription = 'body';

37:       () => base62chars[Math.floor(Math.random() * 62)]
38:     ).join('')
39:     return timestamp + randomPart
40:   }
41:   const actionId = genActionId()
42:   const timeoutMs = timeout * 1000
43:   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
44:     const onMessage = (event) => {
45:       const res = event.data
46:       // console.log('runExtensionAction: received message', res)
47:       if (res.type === '__agentActionResult__' && res.actionId === actionId) {
48:         window.removeEventListener('message', onMessage)
49:         clearTimeout(timeoutId)
50:         if (res.error) {
51:           resolve([res.error, null])
52:         } else {
53:           resolve([null, res])
54:         }
55:       }
56:     }
57:     const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
58:       window.removeEventListener('message', onMessage)
59:       resolve(['Operation timed out', null])
60:     }, timeoutMs)
61:     window.addEventListener('message', onMessage)
62:     if (origin === 'null') {
63:       postMessageFunc({
64:         type: '__agentAction__',
65:         actionId,
66:         action,
67:         ...data
68:       })
69:     } else {
70:       postMessageFunc({
71:         type: '__agentAction__',
72:         actionId,
73:         action,
74:         ...data
75:       }, origin)
76:     }
77:   })
78: }

================
File: manus-archive-master/runtime_app_data/js/scrollAtPoint.js
================
  1: async ({
  2:   x,
  3:   y,
  4:   direction = 'down',
  5:   toEdge = false,
  6:   pixelDelta,
  7: } = {}) => {
  8:   const validDirections = ['up', 'down', 'left', 'right'];
  9:   if (!validDirections.includes(direction)) {
 10:     return { scrolled: false, reason: 'invalid-direction' };
 11:   }
 12:   const axis = direction === 'left' || direction === 'right' ? 'x' : 'y';
 13:   const dir = direction === 'up' || direction === 'left' ? -1 : 1;
 14:   const stepFallback = Math.max(
 15:     120,
 16:     Math.round((axis === 'y' ? window.innerHeight : window.innerWidth) * 0.6),
 17:   );
 18:   const delta = typeof pixelDelta === 'number' && Number.isFinite(pixelDelta) && pixelDelta > 0
 19:     ? pixelDelta
 20:     : stepFallback;
 21:   const targetEl = document.elementFromPoint(x, y);
 22:   if (!targetEl) {
 23:     return { scrolled: false, reason: 'no-target' };
 24:   }
 25:   const isScrollable = (el) => {
 26:     if (!el || !(el instanceof Element)) return false;
 27:     if (el.clientHeight === 0 || el.clientWidth === 0) return false;
 28:     const style = getComputedStyle(el);
 29:     if (style.display === 'none' || style.visibility === 'hidden') return false;
 30:     const scrollableSpace = axis === 'y' ? el.scrollHeight - el.clientHeight : el.scrollWidth - el.clientWidth;
 31:     return scrollableSpace > 1 && Number.isFinite(scrollableSpace);
 32:   };
 33:   const describeElement = (el) => {
 34:     const tag = el.tagName ? el.tagName.toLowerCase() : 'element';
 35:     const idPart = el.id ? `#${el.id}` : '';
 36:     const classList = (el.className || '').toString().trim().split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean).slice(0, 2);
 37:     const classPart = classList.length ? `.${classList.join('.')}` : '';
 38:     const ariaLabel = el.getAttribute ? el.getAttribute('aria-label') : null;
 39:     const ariaPart = ariaLabel ? `[aria-label="${ariaLabel.slice(0, 40)}"]` : '';
 40:     return `${tag}${idPart}${classPart}${ariaPart}`;
 41:   };
 42:   const buildPath = (el) => {
 43:     const parts = [];
 44:     let current = el;
 45:     let safety = 0;
 46:     while (current && safety < 8) {
 47:       if (!(current instanceof Element)) break;
 48:       parts.unshift(describeElement(current));
 49:       const root = current.getRootNode ? current.getRootNode() : null;
 50:       if (root && typeof ShadowRoot !== 'undefined' && root instanceof ShadowRoot && root.host && current !== root.host) {
 51:         current = root.host;
 52:       } else {
 53:         current = current.parentElement;
 54:       }
 55:       safety += 1;
 56:     }
 57:     return parts.join(' > ');
 58:   };
 59:   const readPosition = (el) => {
 60:     if (!el) return 0;
 61:     if (el === document.body || el === document.documentElement) {
 62:       const winPos = axis === 'y' ? window.scrollY : window.scrollX;
 63:       if (typeof winPos === 'number' && Number.isFinite(winPos)) return winPos;
 64:     }
 65:     const val = axis === 'y' ? el.scrollTop : el.scrollLeft;
 66:     if (typeof val === 'number' && Number.isFinite(val)) return val;
 67:     return 0;
 68:   };
 69:   const waitForScrollSettle = async (el, before) => {
 70:     const immediate = readPosition(el);
 71:     if (Math.abs(immediate - before) > 1) return immediate;
 72:     await new Promise((resolve) => requestAnimationFrame(resolve));
 73:     const afterFrame = readPosition(el);
 74:     if (Math.abs(afterFrame - before) > 1) return afterFrame;
 75:     await new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 50));
 76:     return readPosition(el);
 77:   };
 78:   let current = targetEl;
 79:   let safety = 0;
 80:   while (current && safety < 80) {
 81:     if (!isScrollable(current)) {
 82:       const root = current.getRootNode ? current.getRootNode() : null;
 83:       if (root && typeof ShadowRoot !== 'undefined' && root instanceof ShadowRoot && root.host && current !== root.host) {
 84:         current = root.host;
 85:       } else {
 86:         current = current.parentElement;
 87:       }
 88:       safety += 1;
 89:       continue;
 90:     }
 91:     const before = readPosition(current);
 92:     const maxOffset = axis === 'y'
 93:       ? Math.max(current.scrollHeight - current.clientHeight, 0)
 94:       : Math.max(current.scrollWidth - current.clientWidth, 0);
 95:     const boundaryBefore = dir < 0 ? before <= 1 : before >= maxOffset - 1;
 96:     const target = toEdge
 97:       ? (dir < 0 ? 0 : maxOffset)
 98:       : Math.min(Math.max(before + dir * delta, 0), maxOffset);
 99:     try {
100:       if (axis === 'y') {
101:         if (typeof current.scrollTo === 'function') {
102:           current.scrollTo({ top: target, behavior: 'auto' });
103:         } else {
104:           current.scrollTop = target;
105:         }
106:       } else if (typeof current.scrollTo === 'function') {
107:         current.scrollTo({ left: target, behavior: 'auto' });
108:       } else {
109:         current.scrollLeft = target;
110:       }
111:     } catch (e) {
112:       return { scrolled: false, reason: 'scroll-failed', error: e.message };
113:     }
114:     const after = await waitForScrollSettle(current, before);
115:     const moved = Math.abs(after - before) > 1;
116:     const atBoundary = dir < 0 ? after <= 1 : after >= maxOffset - 1;
117:     return {
118:       scrolled: moved,
119:       targetDescription: describeElement(current),
120:       path: buildPath(current),
121:       before,
122:       after,
123:       atBoundary,
124:       boundaryBefore,
125:       maxOffset,
126:     };
127:   }
128:   return { scrolled: false, reason: 'no-scrollable-at-point' };
129: };

 3:   if (!el) return;
 4:   if (axis === 'x') {
 5:     if (typeof el.scrollTo === 'function') {
 6:       el.scrollTo({ left: el.scrollLeft + deltaValue, behavior: 'auto' });
 7:     } else {
 8:       window.scrollBy(deltaValue, 0);
 9:     }
10:     return;
11:   }
12:   if (typeof el.scrollTo === 'function') {

14:   } else {
15:     window.scrollBy(0, deltaValue);
16:   }

 1: (target) => {
 2:   if (!target || !target.getBoundingClientRect) {
 3:     return { has_canvas: false, intersects_target: false };
 4:   }
 5:   const rect = target.getBoundingClientRect();
 6:   const centerX = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
 7:   const centerY = rect.top + rect.height / 2;
 8:   const canvases = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('canvas'));
 9:   let intersects = false;
10:   for (const canvas of canvases) {
11:     const canvasRect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
12:     if (
13:       centerX >= canvasRect.left &&
14:       centerX <= canvasRect.right &&
15:       centerY >= canvasRect.top &&
16:       centerY <= canvasRect.bottom
17:     ) {
18:       intersects = true;
19:       break;
20:     }
21:   }
22:   return { has_canvas: canvases.length > 0, intersects_target: intersects };

143:     async def get_status(self, interaction_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
144:         """
145:         Get the status of a research task.
146:         Returns:
147:             Dict with 'status' and optionally 'result' or 'error'
148:         """
149:         client = await self._get_client()
150:         try:
151:             response = await client.get(
152:                 f"{self.BASE_URL}/{interaction_id}",

154:                 timeout=30.0
155:             )
156:             if response.status_code != 200:
157:                 return {"status": "error", "error": f"API error: {response.status_code}"}
158:             data = response.json()

162:                 if outputs:

164:                     return {"status": "completed", "result": text, "raw": data}

172:     async def wait_for_completion(
173:         self,
174:         interaction_id: str,
175:         timeout: Optional[int] = None,
176:         poll_interval: Optional[int] = None,
177:         progress_callback: Optional[Callable[[int, float, str], None]] = None
178:     ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
179:         timeout = timeout or self.timeout
180:         poll_interval = poll_interval or self.poll_interval
181:         start_time = asyncio.get_event_loop().time()
182:         poll_count = 0
183:         while True:
184:             elapsed = asyncio.get_event_loop().time() - start_time
185:             if elapsed > timeout:
186:                 self.history.update_status(interaction_id, "timeout")
187:                 return {"status": "timeout", "error": f"Research timed out after {timeout}s"}

189:             poll_count += 1
190:             if progress_callback:
191:                 progress_callback(poll_count, elapsed, result.get("status", "unknown"))
192:             if result["status"] == "completed":
193:                 self.history.update_status(interaction_id, "completed")
194:                 return result
195:             elif result["status"] in ["failed", "error"]:
196:                 self.history.update_status(interaction_id, "failed")
197:                 return result
198:             await asyncio.sleep(poll_interval)
199:     async def stream_research(
200:         self,
201:         query: str,
202:         format_spec: Optional[str] = None
203:     ) -> AsyncIterator[Dict[str, Any]]:
204:         prompt = self._build_prompt(query, format_spec)
205:         client = await self._get_client()
206:         try:
207:             async with client.stream(
208:                 "POST",
209:                 f"{self.BASE_URL}?alt=sse",
210:                 headers={
211:                     "Content-Type": "application/json",
212:                     "x-goog-api-key": str(self.api_key)
213:                 },
214:                 json={
215:                     "input": prompt,
216:                     "agent": self.AGENT,
217:                     "background": True,
218:                     "stream": True,
219:                     "agent_config": {
220:                         "type": "deep-research",
221:                         "thinking_summaries": "auto"
222:                     }
223:                 },
224:                 timeout=None
225:             ) as response:
226:                 interaction_id = None
227:                 buffer = ""
228:                 async for chunk in response.aiter_text():
229:                     buffer += chunk
230:                     # Parse SSE events
231:                     while "\n\n" in buffer:
232:                         event_str, buffer = buffer.split("\n\n", 1)
233:                         if not event_str.strip():
234:                             continue
235:                         data_line = None
236:                         for line in event_str.split("\n"):
237:                             if line.startswith("data: "):
238:                                 data_line = line[6:]
239:                                 break
240:                         if not data_line:
241:                             continue
242:                         try:
243:                             event = json.loads(data_line)
244:                         except json.JSONDecodeError:
245:                             continue
246:                         event_type = event.get("event_type", "")
247:                         if event_type == "interaction.start":
248:                             interaction_id = event.get("interaction", {}).get("id")
249:                             if interaction_id:
250:                                 self.history.add_interaction(interaction_id, query, "streaming")
251:                             yield {"type": "start", "interaction_id": interaction_id}
252:                         elif event_type == "content.delta":
253:                             delta = event.get("delta", {})
254:                             delta_type = delta.get("type")
255:                             if delta_type == "text":
256:                                 yield {"type": "text", "content": delta.get("text", "")}
257:                             elif delta_type == "thought_summary":
258:                                 content = delta.get("content", {})
259:                                 yield {"type": "thought", "content": content.get("text", "")}
260:                         elif event_type == "interaction.complete":
261:                             if interaction_id:
262:                                 self.history.update_status(interaction_id, "completed")
263:                             yield {"type": "complete"}
264:                         elif event_type == "error":
265:                             if interaction_id:
266:                                 self.history.update_status(interaction_id, "failed")
267:                             yield {"type": "error", "error": event.get("error", "Unknown error")}
268:         except httpx.HTTPError as e:
269:             yield {"type": "error", "error": str(e)}
270:     def parse_result(self, text: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
271:         if not text:
272:             return None
273:         try:
274:             return json.loads(text)
275:         except json.JSONDecodeError:
276:             pass
277:         json_match = re.search(r'```(?:json)?\s*(\{.*?\})\s*```', text, re.DOTALL)
278:         if json_match:
279:             try:
280:                 return json.loads(json_match.group(1))
281:             except json.JSONDecodeError:
282:                 pass
283:         # Try finding JSON object pattern
284:         json_match = re.search(r'\{[^{}]*"[^"]+"\s*:[^{}]*\}', text, re.DOTALL)
285:         if json_match:
286:             try:
287:                 return json.loads(json_match.group(0))
288:             except json.JSONDecodeError:
289:                 pass
290:         return None
291: def print_progress(poll_count: int, elapsed: float, status: str):
292:     """Print progress update during polling."""
293:     mins = int(elapsed // 60)
294:     secs = int(elapsed % 60)
295:     print(f"\r[{mins:02d}:{secs:02d}] Poll
296: async def cmd_research(args):
297:     client = DeepResearchClient()
298:     try:
299:         if args.stream:
300:             print(f"Starting streaming research...\n")
301:             full_text = ""
302:             async for event in client.stream_research(args.query, args.format):
303:                 if event["type"] == "start":

309:                     full_text += event["content"]
310:                 elif event["type"] == "complete":
311:                     print("\n\n[Research Complete]")
312:                 elif event["type"] == "error":
313:                     print(f"\n[Error] {event['error']}", file=sys.stderr)
314:                     return 1
315:             # Output JSON if requested
316:             if args.json and full_text:
317:                 parsed = client.parse_result(full_text)
318:                 if parsed:
319:                     print("\n\n--- Parsed JSON ---")
320:                     print(json.dumps(parsed, indent=2))
321:         else:
322:             # Polling mode
323:             previous_id = args.continue_from if hasattr(args, 'continue_from') else None
324:             print(f"Starting research task...")
325:             interaction_id = await client.start_research(
326:                 args.query,
327:                 args.format,
328:                 previous_id
329:             )
330:             print(f"Interaction ID: {interaction_id}")
331:             print(f"Estimated time: 2-10 minutes\n")
332:             if args.no_wait:
333:                 print(f"Research started. Check status with: --status {interaction_id}")
334:                 return 0
335:             print("Waiting for completion (Ctrl+C to cancel)...")
336:             result = await client.wait_for_completion(
337:                 interaction_id,
338:                 progress_callback=print_progress
339:             )
340:             print()  # New line after progress
341:             if result["status"] == "completed":
342:                 text = result.get("result", "")
343:                 if args.json:
344:                     parsed = client.parse_result(text)
345:                     if parsed:
346:                         print(json.dumps(parsed, indent=2))
347:                     else:
348:                         print(json.dumps({"text": text}, indent=2))
349:                 elif args.raw:
350:                     print(json.dumps(result.get("raw", {}), indent=2))
351:                 else:
352:                     print("\n--- Research Result ---\n")
353:                     print(text)
354:                 return 0
355:             else:
356:                 print(f"\nResearch failed: {result.get('error', 'Unknown error')}")
357:                 return 1
358:     except DeepResearchError as e:
359:         print(f"Error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
360:         return 1
361:     except KeyboardInterrupt:
362:         print("\n\nCancelled by user.")
363:         return 130
364:     finally:
365:         await client.close()
366: async def cmd_status(args):
367:     """Check status of a research task."""
368:     client = DeepResearchClient()
369:     try:
370:         result = await client.get_status(args.interaction_id)
371:         if args.json:
372:             print(json.dumps(result, indent=2))
373:         else:
374:             print(f"Status: {result['status']}")
375:             if result["status"] == "completed":
376:                 text = result.get("result", "")
377:                 if text:
378:                     print(f"\n--- Result Preview ---\n{text[:500]}...")
379:             elif result["status"] in ["failed", "error"]:
380:                 print(f"Error: {result.get('error', 'Unknown')}")
381:         return 0 if result["status"] != "error" else 1
382:     except DeepResearchError as e:
383:         print(f"Error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
384:         return 1
385:     finally:
386:         await client.close()
387: async def cmd_wait(args):
388:     """Wait for a research task to complete."""
389:     client = DeepResearchClient()
390:     try:
391:         print(f"Waiting for {args.interaction_id}...")
392:         result = await client.wait_for_completion(
393:             args.interaction_id,
394:             progress_callback=print_progress
395:         )
396:         print()
397:         if result["status"] == "completed":
398:             text = result.get("result", "")
399:             if args.json:
400:                 parsed = client.parse_result(text)
401:                 if parsed:
402:                     print(json.dumps(parsed, indent=2))
403:                 else:
404:                     print(json.dumps({"text": text}, indent=2))
405:             else:
406:                 print("\n--- Research Result ---\n")
407:                 print(text)
408:             return 0
409:         else:
410:             print(f"Research failed: {result.get('error', 'Unknown error')}")
411:             return 1
412:     except DeepResearchError as e:
413:         print(f"Error: {e}", file=sys.stderr)
414:         return 1
415:     except KeyboardInterrupt:
416:         print("\n\nCancelled by user.")
417:         return 130
418:     finally:
419:         await client.close()
420: async def cmd_list(args):
421:     """List recent research tasks."""
422:     history = HistoryManager()
423:     interactions = history.get_recent(args.limit)
424:     if not interactions:
425:         print("No research history found.")
426:         return 0
427:     if args.json:
428:         print(json.dumps(interactions, indent=2))
429:     else:
430:         print(f"Recent research tasks (last {len(interactions)}):\n")
431:         for item in interactions:
432:             status_icon = {
433:                 "completed": "[ok]",
434:                 "failed": "[!!]",
435:                 "started": "[..]",
436:                 "streaming": "[>>]",
437:                 "timeout": "[to]"
438:             }.get(item.get("status", ""), "[??]")
439:             print(f"{status_icon} {item['id'][:12]}...")
440:             print(f"    Query: {item['query'][:60]}{'...' if len(item['query']) > 60 else ''}")
441:             print(f"    Started: {item.get('started_at', 'N/A')}")
442:             if item.get("completed_at"):
443:                 print(f"    Completed: {item['completed_at']}")
444:             print()
445:     return 0
446: def main():
447:     parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
448:         description="Gemini Deep Research - Autonomous multi-step research agent",
449:         formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter,
450:         epilog="""
451: Examples:
452:   # Start a research task and wait for results
453:   %(prog)s --query "Research the history of Kubernetes"
454:   # With structured output format
455:   %(prog)s --query "Compare Python web frameworks" \\
456:     --format "1. Executive Summary\\n2. Comparison Table\\n3. Recommendations"
457:   # Stream progress in real-time
458:   %(prog)s --query "Analyze EV battery market" --stream
459:   # Start without waiting
460:   %(prog)s --query "Research topic" --no-wait
461:   # Check status of running research
462:   %(prog)s --status abc123
463:   # Continue from previous research
464:   %(prog)s --query "Elaborate on point 2" --continue abc123
465:   # List recent research
466:   %(prog)s --list
467: Note: Research tasks typically take 2-10 minutes and cost $2-5 per task.
468: """
469:     )
470:     cmd_group = parser.add_mutually_exclusive_group(required=True)
471:     cmd_group.add_argument("--query", "-q", help="Research query to execute")
472:     cmd_group.add_argument("--status", "-s", dest="interaction_id", metavar="ID",
473:                           help="Check status of a research task")
474:     cmd_group.add_argument("--wait", "-w", dest="wait_id", metavar="ID",
475:                           help="Wait for a research task to complete")
476:     cmd_group.add_argument("--list", "-l", action="store_true",
477:                           help="List recent research tasks")
478:     parser.add_argument("--format", "-f", metavar="SPEC",
479:                        help="Output format specification")
480:     parser.add_argument("--continue", dest="continue_from", metavar="ID",
481:                        help="Continue from previous research interaction")
482:     parser.add_argument("--stream", action="store_true",
483:                        help="Stream progress in real-time")
484:     parser.add_argument("--no-wait", action="store_true",
485:                        help="Start research without waiting for completion")
486:     parser.add_argument("--json", "-j", action="store_true",
487:                        help="Output results as JSON")
488:     parser.add_argument("--raw", "-r", action="store_true",
489:                        help="Output raw API response")
490:     parser.add_argument("--limit", type=int, default=10,
491:                        help="Number of recent tasks to show (default: 10)")
492:     args = parser.parse_args()
493:     if args.query:
494:         exit_code = asyncio.run(cmd_research(args))
495:     elif args.interaction_id:
496:         exit_code = asyncio.run(cmd_status(args))
497:     elif args.wait_id:
498:         args.interaction_id = args.wait_id
499:         exit_code = asyncio.run(cmd_wait(args))
500:     elif args.list:
501:         exit_code = asyncio.run(cmd_list(args))
502:     else:
503:         parser.print_help()
504:         exit_code = 1
505:     sys.exit(exit_code)
506: if __name__ == "__main__":
507:     main()

File: manus-archive-master/skills/deep-research/README.md
================
  1: # Gemini Deep Research Skill
  2: 
  3: Execute autonomous multi-step research tasks using Google's Gemini Deep Research Agent. Unlike standard LLM queries that respond in seconds, Deep Research is an "analyst-in-a-box" that plans, searches, reads, and synthesizes information into comprehensive, cited reports.
  4: 
  5: ## Overview
  6: 
  7: The Deep Research Agent (`deep-research-pro-preview-12-2025`) powered by Gemini 3 Pro:
  8: 
  9: - **Plans** research strategy based on your query
 10: - **Searches** the web and analyzes sources
 11: - **Reads** and extracts relevant information
 12: - **Iterates** through multiple search/read cycles
 13: - **Outputs** detailed, cited reports
 14: 
 15: This process takes 2-10 minutes but produces thorough analysis that would take a human researcher hours.
 16: 
 17: ## Installation
 18: 
 19: ```bash
 20: # Navigate to skill directory
 21: cd skills/deep-research
 22: 
 23: # Install dependencies
 24: pip install -r requirements.txt
 25: 
 26: # Set up API key
 27: cp .env.example .env
 28: # Edit .env and add your GEMINI_API_KEY
 29: ```
 30: 
 31: ### Getting a Gemini API Key
 32: 
 33: 1. Go to [Google AI Studio](https://aistudio.google.com/)
 34: 2. Click "Get API key"
 35: 3. Create a new key or use an existing one
 36: 4. Copy the key to your `.env` file
 37: 
 38: ## Quick Start
 39: 
 40: ```bash
 41: # Basic research query
 42: python3 scripts/research.py --query "Research the competitive landscape of cloud providers in 2024"
 43: 
 44: # Stream progress in real-time
 45: python3 scripts/research.py --query "Compare React, Vue, and Angular frameworks" --stream
 46: 
 47: # Get structured JSON output
 48: python3 scripts/research.py --query "Analyze the EV market" --json
 49: ```
 50: 
 51: ## Commands
 52: 
 53: ### `--query` / `-q`
 54: 
 55: Start a new research task.
 56: 
 57: ```bash
 58: # Basic query
 59: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Research the history of containerization"
 60: 
 61: # With output format specification
 62: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Compare database solutions" \
 63:   --format "1. Executive Summary\n2. Comparison Table\n3. Pros/Cons\n4. Recommendations"
 64: 
 65: # Start without waiting for results
 66: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Research topic" --no-wait
 67: ```
 68: 
 69: ### `--stream`
 70: 
 71: Stream research progress in real-time. Shows thinking steps and builds the report as it's generated.
 72: 
 73: ```bash
 74: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Analyze market trends" --stream
 75: ```
 76: 
 77: ### `--status` / `-s`
 78: 
 79: Check the status of a running research task.
 80: 
 81: ```bash
 82: python3 scripts/research.py --status abc123xyz
 83: ```
 84: 
 85: ### `--wait` / `-w`
 86: 
 87: Wait for a specific research task to complete.
 88: 
 89: ```bash
 90: python3 scripts/research.py --wait abc123xyz
 91: ```
 92: 
 93: ### `--continue`
 94: 
 95: Continue a conversation from previous research. Useful for follow-up questions.
 96: 
 97: ```bash
 98: # First, run initial research
 99: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Research Kubernetes architecture"
100: # Output: Interaction ID: abc123xyz
101: 
102: # Then ask follow-up
103: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Elaborate on the networking section" --continue abc123xyz
104: ```
105: 
106: ### `--list` / `-l`
107: 
108: List recent research tasks from local history.
109: 
110: ```bash
111: python3 scripts/research.py --list
112: python3 scripts/research.py --list --limit 20
113: ```
114: 
115: ## Output Options
116: 
117: | Flag | Description |
118: |------|-------------|
119: | (default) | Human-readable markdown report |
120: | `--json` / `-j` | Structured JSON output |
121: | `--raw` / `-r` | Raw API response |
122: 
123: ## Configuration
124: 
125: ### Environment Variables
126: 
127: | Variable | Default | Description |
128: |----------|---------|-------------|
129: | `GEMINI_API_KEY` | (required) | Your Google Gemini API key |
130: | `DEEP_RESEARCH_TIMEOUT` | `600` | Max wait time in seconds |
131: | `DEEP_RESEARCH_POLL_INTERVAL` | `10` | Seconds between status polls |
132: | `DEEP_RESEARCH_CACHE_DIR` | `~/.cache/deep-research` | Local history cache directory |
133: 
134: ### .env File
135: 
136: ```bash
137: GEMINI_API_KEY=your-api-key-here
138: DEEP_RESEARCH_TIMEOUT=600
139: DEEP_RESEARCH_POLL_INTERVAL=10
140: ```
141: 
142: ## Cost & Performance
143: 
144: ### Estimated Costs
145: 
146: Deep Research uses a pay-as-you-go model based on token usage:
147: 
148: | Task Type | Search Queries | Input Tokens | Output Tokens | Estimated Cost |
149: |-----------|---------------|--------------|---------------|----------------|
150: | Standard | ~80 | ~250k (50-70% cached) | ~60k | $2-3 |
151: | Complex | ~160 | ~900k (50-70% cached) | ~80k | $3-5 |
152: 
153: ### Time Expectations
154: 
155: - **Simple queries**: 2-5 minutes
156: - **Complex analysis**: 5-10 minutes
157: - **Maximum**: 60 minutes (API limit)
158: 
159: ## Use Cases
160: 
161: ### Market Analysis
162: ```bash
163: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Analyze the competitive landscape of \
164:   EV battery manufacturers, including market share, technology, and supply chain"
165: ```
166: 
167: ### Technical Research
168: ```bash
169: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Compare Rust vs Go for building \
170:   high-performance backend services" \
171:   --format "1. Performance Benchmarks\n2. Memory Safety\n3. Ecosystem\n4. Learning Curve"
172: ```
173: 
174: ### Due Diligence
175: ```bash
176: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Research Company XYZ: recent news, \
177:   financial performance, leadership changes, and market position"
178: ```
179: 
180: ### Literature Review
181: ```bash
182: python3 scripts/research.py -q "Review recent developments in \
183:   large language model efficiency and optimization techniques"
184: ```
185: 
186: ## Error Handling
187: 
188: | Error | Cause | Solution |
189: |-------|-------|----------|
190: | `GEMINI_API_KEY not set` | Missing API key | Set in `.env` or environment |
191: | `API error 429` | Rate limited | Wait and retry |
192: | `Research timed out` | Task took too long | Simplify query or increase timeout |
193: | `Failed to parse result` | Unexpected response | Use `--raw` to see actual output |
194: 
195: ## Exit Codes
196: 
197: | Code | Meaning |
198: |------|---------|
199: | 0 | Success |
200: | 1 | Error (API, config, timeout) |
201: | 130 | Cancelled by user (Ctrl+C) |
202: 
203: ## Architecture
204: 
205: ```
206: ┌─────────────────┐      ┌──────────────────────┐
207: │   CLI Script    │──────│  DeepResearchClient  │
208: │  (research.py)  │      │                      │
209: └─────────────────┘      └──────────┬───────────┘
210:                                     │
211:                                     ▼
212:                          ┌──────────────────────┐
213:                          │   Gemini Deep        │
214:                          │   Research API       │
215:                          │                      │
216:                          │  POST /interactions  │
217:                          │  GET  /interactions  │
218:                          └──────────────────────┘
219:                                     │
220:                                     ▼
221:                          ┌──────────────────────┐
222:                          │   HistoryManager     │
223:                          │  (~/.cache/deep-     │
224:                          │   research/)         │
225:                          └──────────────────────┘
226: ```
227: 
228: ## Safety & Privacy
229: 
230: - **Read-only**: This skill only reads/researches; no file modifications
231: - **No secrets in queries**: Avoid including sensitive data in research queries
232: - **Source verification**: Always verify citations in the output
233: - **Cost awareness**: Each task costs $2-5; be mindful of usage
234: 
235: ## Limitations
236: 
237: - **No custom tools**: Cannot use MCP or function calling
238: - **No structured output enforcement**: JSON formatting relies on prompt engineering
239: - **Web-only research**: Cannot access private/authenticated sources
240: - **60-minute max**: Very complex tasks may time out
241: 
242: ## References
243: 
244: - [Gemini Deep Research Documentation](https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/deep-research)
245: - [Google AI Studio](https://aistudio.google.com/)
246: - [Gemini API Pricing](https://ai.google.dev/gemini-api/docs/pricing)

  1: ---
  2: name: deep-research
  3: description: "Execute autonomous multi-step research using Google Gemini Deep Research Agent. Use for: market analysis, competitive landscaping, literature reviews, technical research, due diligence. Takes 2-10 minutes but produces detailed, cited reports. Costs $2-5 per task."
  4: license: Apache-2.0
  5: metadata:
  6:   author: sanjay3290
  7:   version: "1.0"
  8: ---
  9: 
 10: # Gemini Deep Research Skill
 11: 
 12: Run autonomous research tasks that plan, search, read, and synthesize information into comprehensive reports.
 13: 
 14: ## Requirements
 15: 
 16: - Python 3.8+
 17: - httpx: `pip install -r requirements.txt`
 18: - GEMINI_API_KEY environment variable
 19: 
 20: ## Setup
 21: 
 22: 1. Get a Gemini API key from [Google AI Studio](https://aistudio.google.com/)
 23: 2. Set the environment variable:
 24:    ```bash
 25:    export GEMINI_API_KEY=your-api-key-here
 26:    ```
 27:    Or create a `.env` file in the skill directory.
 28: 
 29: ## Usage
 30: 
 31: ### Start a research task
 32: ```bash
 33: python3 scripts/research.py --query "Research the history of Kubernetes"
 34: ```
 35: 
 36: ### With structured output format
 37: ```bash
 38: python3 scripts/research.py --query "Compare Python web frameworks" \
 39:   --format "1. Executive Summary\n2. Comparison Table\n3. Recommendations"
 40: ```
 41: 
 42: ### Stream progress in real-time
 43: ```bash
 44: python3 scripts/research.py --query "Analyze EV battery market" --stream
 45: ```
 46: 
 47: ### Start without waiting
 48: ```bash
 49: python3 scripts/research.py --query "Research topic" --no-wait
 50: ```
 51: 
 52: ### Check status of running research
 53: ```bash
 54: python3 scripts/research.py --status <interaction_id>
 55: ```
 56: 
 57: ### Wait for completion
 58: ```bash
 59: python3 scripts/research.py --wait <interaction_id>
 60: ```
 61: 
 62: ### Continue from previous research
 63: ```bash
 64: python3 scripts/research.py --query "Elaborate on point 2" --continue <interaction_id>
 65: ```
 66: 
 67: ### List recent research
 68: ```bash
 69: python3 scripts/research.py --list
 70: ```
 71: 
 72: ## Output Formats
 73: 
 74: - **Default**: Human-readable markdown report
 75: - **JSON** (`--json`): Structured data for programmatic use
 76: - **Raw** (`--raw`): Unprocessed API response
 77: 
 78: ## Cost & Time
 79: 
 80: | Metric | Value |
 81: |--------|-------|
 82: | Time | 2-10 minutes per task |
 83: | Cost | $2-5 per task (varies by complexity) |
 84: | Token usage | ~250k-900k input, ~60k-80k output |
 85: 
 86: ## Best Use Cases
 87: 
 88: - Market analysis and competitive landscaping
 89: - Technical literature reviews
 90: - Due diligence research
 91: - Historical research and timelines
 92: - Comparative analysis (frameworks, products, technologies)
 93: 
 94: ## Workflow
 95: 
 96: 1. User requests research → Run `--query "..."`
 97: 2. Inform user of estimated time (2-10 minutes)
 98: 3. Monitor with `--stream` or poll with `--status`
 99: 4. Return formatted results
100: 5. Use `--continue` for follow-up questions
101: 
102: ## Exit Codes
103: 
104: - **0**: Success
105: - **1**: Error (API error, config issue, timeout)
106: - **130**: Cancelled by user (Ctrl+C)
