 1: # Output Patterns
 2: 
 3: Use these patterns when skills need to produce consistent, high-quality output.
 4: 
 5: ## Template Pattern
 6: 
 7: Provide templates for output format. Match the level of strictness to your needs.
 8: 
 9: **For strict requirements (like API responses or data formats):**
10: 
11: ```markdown
12: ## Report structure
13: 
14: ALWAYS use this exact template structure:
15: 
16: # [Analysis Title]
17: 
18: ## Executive summary
19: [One-paragraph overview of key findings]
20: 
21: ## Key findings
22: - Finding 1 with supporting data
23: - Finding 2 with supporting data
24: - Finding 3 with supporting data
25: 
26: ## Recommendations
27: 1. Specific actionable recommendation
28: 2. Specific actionable recommendation
29: ```
30: 
31: **For flexible guidance (when adaptation is useful):**
32: 
33: ```markdown
34: ## Report structure
35: 
36: Here is a sensible default format, but use your best judgment:
37: 
38: # [Analysis Title]
39: 
40: ## Executive summary
41: [Overview]
42: 
43: ## Key findings
44: [Adapt sections based on what you discover]
45: 
46: ## Recommendations
47: [Tailor to the specific context]
48: 
49: Adjust sections as needed for the specific analysis type.
50: ```
51: 
52: ## Examples Pattern
53: 
54: For skills where output quality depends on seeing examples, provide input/output pairs:
55: 
56: ```markdown
57: ## Commit message format
58: 
59: Generate commit messages following these examples:
60: 
61: **Example 1:**
62: Input: Added user authentication with JWT tokens
63: Output:
64: ```
65: feat(auth): implement JWT-based authentication
66: 
67: Add login endpoint and token validation middleware
68: ```
69: 
70: **Example 2:**
71: Input: Fixed bug where dates displayed incorrectly in reports
72: Output:
73: ```
74: fix(reports): correct date formatting in timezone conversion
75: 
76: Use UTC timestamps consistently across report generation
77: ```
78: 
79: Follow this style: type(scope): brief description, then detailed explanation.
80: ```
81: 
82: Examples help Manus understand the desired style and level of detail more clearly than descriptions alone.

File: manus-archive-master/skills/skill-creator/references/progressive-disclosure-patterns.md
================
 1: # Progressive Disclosure Patterns
 2: 
 3: Keep SKILL.md body to the essentials and under 500 lines to minimize context bloat. Split content into separate files when approaching this limit. When splitting out content into other files, it is very important to reference them from SKILL.md and describe clearly when to read them, to ensure the reader of the skill knows they exist and when to use them.
 4: 
 5: **Key principle:** When a skill supports multiple variations, frameworks, or options, keep only the core workflow and selection guidance in SKILL.md. Move variant-specific details (patterns, examples, configuration) into separate reference files.
 6: 
 7: **Pattern 1: High-level guide with references**
 8: 
 9: ```markdown
10: # PDF Processing
11: 
12: ## Quick start
13: 
14: Extract text with pdfplumber:
15: [code example]
16: 
17: ## Advanced features
18: 
19: - **Form filling**: See [FORMS.md](FORMS.md) for complete guide
20: - **API reference**: See [REFERENCE.md](REFERENCE.md) for all methods
21: - **Examples**: See [EXAMPLES.md](EXAMPLES.md) for common patterns
22: ```
23: 
24: Manus loads FORMS.md, REFERENCE.md, or EXAMPLES.md only when needed.
25: 
26: **Pattern 2: Domain-specific organization**
27: 
28: For Skills with multiple domains, organize content by domain to avoid loading irrelevant context:
29: 
30: ```
31: bigquery-skill/
32: ├── SKILL.md (overview and navigation)
33: └── reference/
34:     ├── finance.md (revenue, billing metrics)
35:     ├── sales.md (opportunities, pipeline)
36:     ├── product.md (API usage, features)
37:     └── marketing.md (campaigns, attribution)
38: ```
39: 
40: When a user asks about sales metrics, Manus only reads sales.md.
41: 
42: Similarly, for skills supporting multiple frameworks or variants, organize by variant:
43: 
44: ```
45: cloud-deploy/
46: ├── SKILL.md (workflow + provider selection)
47: └── references/
48:     ├── aws.md (AWS deployment patterns)
49:     ├── gcp.md (GCP deployment patterns)
50:     └── azure.md (Azure deployment patterns)
51: ```
52: 
53: When the user chooses AWS, Manus only reads aws.md.
54: 
55: **Pattern 3: Conditional details**
56: 
57: Show basic content, link to advanced content:
58: 
59: ```markdown
60: # DOCX Processing
61: 
62: ## Creating documents
63: 
64: Use docx-js for new documents. See [DOCX-JS.md](DOCX-JS.md).
65: 
66: ## Editing documents
67: 
68: For simple edits, modify the XML directly.
69: 
70: **For tracked changes**: See [REDLINING.md](REDLINING.md)
71: **For OOXML details**: See [OOXML.md](OOXML.md)
72: ```
73: 
74: Manus reads REDLINING.md or OOXML.md only when the user needs those features.
75: 
76: **Important guidelines:**
77: 
78: - **Avoid deeply nested references** - Keep references one level deep from SKILL.md. All reference files should link directly from SKILL.md.
79: - **Structure longer reference files** - For files longer than 100 lines, include a table of contents at the top so Manus can see the full scope when previewing.

================
File: manus-archive-master/skills/skill-creator/references/workflows.md
================
 1: # Workflow Patterns
 2: 
 3: ## Sequential Workflows
 4: 
 5: For complex tasks, break operations into clear, sequential steps. It is often helpful to give Manus an overview of the process towards the beginning of SKILL.md:
 6: 
 7: ```markdown
 8: Filling a PDF form involves these steps:
 9: 
10: 1. Analyze the form (run analyze_form.py)
11: 2. Create field mapping (edit fields.json)
12: 3. Validate mapping (run validate_fields.py)
13: 4. Fill the form (run fill_form.py)
14: 5. Verify output (run verify_output.py)
15: ```
16: 
17: ## Conditional Workflows
18: 
19: For tasks with branching logic, guide Manus through decision points:
20: 
21: ```markdown
22: 1. Determine the modification type:
23:    **Creating new content?** → Follow "Creation workflow" below
24:    **Editing existing content?** → Follow "Editing workflow" below
25: 
26: 2. Creation workflow: [steps]
27: 3. Editing workflow: [steps]
28: ```

  1: import sys
  2: from pathlib import Path
  3: SKILL_TEMPLATE = """---
  4: name: {skill_name}
  5: description: [TODO: Complete and informative explanation of what the skill does and when to use it. Include WHEN to use this skill - specific scenarios, file types, or tasks that trigger it.]
  6: ---
  7: # {skill_title}
  8: ## Overview
  9: [TODO: 1-2 sentences explaining what this skill enables]
 10: ## Structuring This Skill
 11: [TODO: Choose the structure that best fits this skill's purpose. Common patterns:
 12: **1. Workflow-Based** (best for sequential processes)
 13: - Works well when there are clear step-by-step procedures
 14: - Example: DOCX skill with "Workflow Decision Tree" → "Reading" → "Creating" → "Editing"
 15: - Structure: ## Overview → ## Workflow Decision Tree → ## Step 1 → ## Step 2...
 16: **2. Task-Based** (best for tool collections)
 17: - Works well when the skill offers different operations/capabilities
 18: - Example: PDF skill with "Quick Start" → "Merge PDFs" → "Split PDFs" → "Extract Text"
 19: - Structure: ## Overview → ## Quick Start → ## Task Category 1 → ## Task Category 2...
 20: **3. Reference/Guidelines** (best for standards or specifications)
 21: - Works well for brand guidelines, coding standards, or requirements
 22: - Example: Brand styling with "Brand Guidelines" → "Colors" → "Typography" → "Features"
 23: - Structure: ## Overview → ## Guidelines → ## Specifications → ## Usage...
 24: **4. Capabilities-Based** (best for integrated systems)
 25: - Works well when the skill provides multiple interrelated features
 26: - Example: Product Management with "Core Capabilities" → numbered capability list
 27: - Structure: ## Overview → ## Core Capabilities → ### 1. Feature → ### 2. Feature...
 28: Patterns can be mixed and matched as needed. Most skills combine patterns (e.g., start with task-based, add workflow for complex operations).
 29: Delete this entire "Structuring This Skill" section when done - it's just guidance.]
 30: ## [TODO: Replace with the first main section based on chosen structure]
 31: [TODO: Add content here. See examples in existing skills:
 32: - Code samples for technical skills
 33: - Decision trees for complex workflows
 34: - Concrete examples with realistic user requests
 35: - References to scripts/templates/references as needed]
 36: ## Resources
 37: This skill includes example resource directories that demonstrate how to organize different types of bundled resources:
 38: ### scripts/
 39: Executable code (Python/Bash/etc.) that can be run directly to perform specific operations.
 40: **Examples from other skills:**
 41: - PDF skill: `fill_fillable_fields.py`, `extract_form_field_info.py` - utilities for PDF manipulation
 42: - DOCX skill: `document.py`, `utilities.py` - Python modules for document processing
 43: **Appropriate for:** Python scripts, shell scripts, or any executable code that performs automation, data processing, or specific operations.
 44: **Note:** Scripts may be executed without loading into context, but can still be read by Manus for patching or environment adjustments.
 45: ### references/
 46: Documentation and reference material intended to be loaded into context to inform Manus's process and thinking.
 47: **Examples from other skills:**
 48: - Product management: `communication.md`, `context_building.md` - detailed workflow guides
 49: - BigQuery: API reference documentation and query examples
 50: - Finance: Schema documentation, company policies
 51: **Appropriate for:** In-depth documentation, API references, database schemas, comprehensive guides, or any detailed information that Manus should reference while working.
 52: ### templates/
 53: Files not intended to be loaded into context, but rather used within the output Manus produces.
 54: **Examples from other skills:**
 55: - Brand styling: PowerPoint template files (.pptx), logo files
 56: - Frontend builder: HTML/React boilerplate project directories
 57: - Typography: Font files (.ttf, .woff2)
 58: **Appropriate for:** Templates, boilerplate code, document templates, images, icons, fonts, or any files meant to be copied or used in the final output.
 59: ---
 60: **Any unneeded directories can be deleted.** Not every skill requires all three types of resources.

125: def title_case_skill_name(skill_name):
126:     return ' '.join(word.capitalize() for word in skill_name.split('-'))
127: SKILLS_BASE_PATH = "/home/ubuntu/skills"
128: def init_skill(skill_name):
129:     skill_dir = Path(SKILLS_BASE_PATH) / skill_name
130:     if skill_dir.exists():
131:         print(f"❌ Error: Skill directory already exists: {skill_dir}")
132:         return None
133:     # Create skill directory
134:     try:
135:         skill_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)
136:         print(f"✅ Created skill directory: {skill_dir}")
137:     except Exception as e:
138:         print(f"❌ Error creating directory: {e}")
139:         return None
140:     # Create SKILL.md from template
141:     skill_title = title_case_skill_name(skill_name)
142:     skill_content = SKILL_TEMPLATE.format(
143:         skill_name=skill_name,
144:         skill_title=skill_title
145:     )
146:     skill_md_path = skill_dir / 'SKILL.md'
147:     try:
148:         skill_md_path.write_text(skill_content)
149:         print("✅ Created SKILL.md")
150:     except Exception as e:
151:         print(f"❌ Error creating SKILL.md: {e}")
152:         return None
153:     # Create resource directories with example files
154:     try:
155:         # Create scripts/ directory with example script
156:         scripts_dir = skill_dir / 'scripts'
157:         scripts_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
158:         example_script = scripts_dir / 'example.py'
159:         example_script.write_text(EXAMPLE_SCRIPT.format(skill_name=skill_name))
160:         example_script.chmod(0o755)
161:         print("✅ Created scripts/example.py")
162:         references_dir = skill_dir / 'references'
163:         references_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
164:         example_reference = references_dir / 'api_reference.md'
165:         example_reference.write_text(EXAMPLE_REFERENCE.format(skill_title=skill_title))
166:         print("✅ Created references/api_reference.md")
167:         templates_dir = skill_dir / 'templates'
168:         templates_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
169:         example_template = templates_dir / 'example_template.txt'
170:         example_template.write_text(EXAMPLE_TEMPLATE)
171:         print("✅ Created templates/example_template.txt")
172:     except Exception as e:
173:         print(f"❌ Error creating resource directories: {e}")
174:         return None
175:     # Print next steps
176:     print(f"\n✅ Skill '{skill_name}' initialized successfully at {skill_dir}")
177:     print("\nNext steps:")
178:     print("1. Edit SKILL.md to complete the TODO items and update the description")
179:     print("2. Customize or delete the example files in scripts/, references/, and templates/")
180:     print("3. Run the validator when ready to check the skill structure")
181:     return skill_dir
182: def main():
183:     if len(sys.argv) != 2:
184:         print("Usage: init_skill.py <skill-name>")
185:         print("\nSkill name requirements:")
186:         print("  - Hyphen-case identifier (e.g., 'data-analyzer')")
187:         print("  - Lowercase letters, digits, and hyphens only")
188:         print("  - Max 64 characters")

192:         print("  init_skill.py my-api-helper")
193:         print(f"\nSkills are created at {SKILLS_BASE_PATH}/<skill-name>/")
194:         sys.exit(1)
195:     skill_name = sys.argv[1]
196:     print(f"🚀 Initializing skill: {skill_name}")
197:     print(f"   Location: {SKILLS_BASE_PATH}/{skill_name}")
198:     print()

File: manus-archive-master/skills/skill-creator/scripts/quick_validate.py
================
 1: import sys
 2: import re
 3: import yaml
 4: from pathlib import Path
 5: SKILLS_BASE_PATH = Path("/home/ubuntu/skills")
 6: def resolve_skill_path(skill_path_or_name):
 7:     path = Path(skill_path_or_name)
 8:     if path.is_absolute():
 9:         return path
10:     return SKILLS_BASE_PATH / skill_path_or_name
11: def validate_skill(skill_path_or_name):
12:     skill_path = resolve_skill_path(skill_path_or_name)
13:     skill_md = skill_path / 'SKILL.md'
14:     if not skill_md.exists():
15:         return False, "SKILL.md not found"
16:     content = skill_md.read_text()
17:     if not content.startswith('---'):
18:         return False, "No YAML frontmatter found"
19:     match = re.match(r'^---\n(.*?)\n---', content, re.DOTALL)
20:     if not match:
21:         return False, "Invalid frontmatter format"
22:     frontmatter_text = match.group(1)
23:     # Parse YAML frontmatter
24:     try:
25:         frontmatter = yaml.safe_load(frontmatter_text)
26:         if not isinstance(frontmatter, dict):
27:             return False, "Frontmatter must be a YAML dictionary"
28:     except yaml.YAMLError as e:
29:         return False, f"Invalid YAML in frontmatter: {e}"
30:     # Define allowed properties
31:     ALLOWED_PROPERTIES = {'name', 'description', 'license', 'allowed-tools', 'metadata'}
32:     unexpected_keys = set(frontmatter.keys()) - ALLOWED_PROPERTIES
33:     if unexpected_keys:
34:         return False, (
35:             f"Unexpected key(s) in SKILL.md frontmatter: {', '.join(sorted(unexpected_keys))}. "
36:             f"Allowed properties are: {', '.join(sorted(ALLOWED_PROPERTIES))}"
37:         )
38:     # Check required fields
39:     if 'name' not in frontmatter:
40:         return False, "Missing 'name' in frontmatter"
41:     if 'description' not in frontmatter:
42:         return False, "Missing 'description' in frontmatter"
43:     name = frontmatter.get('name', '')
44:     if not isinstance(name, str):
45:         return False, f"Name must be a string, got {type(name).__name__}"
46:     name = name.strip()
47:     if name:
48:         # Check naming convention (hyphen-case: lowercase with hyphens)
49:         if not re.match(r'^[a-z0-9-]+$', name):
50:             return False, f"Name '{name}' should be hyphen-case (lowercase letters, digits, and hyphens only)"
51:         if name.startswith('-') or name.endswith('-') or '--' in name:
52:             return False, f"Name '{name}' cannot start/end with hyphen or contain consecutive hyphens"
53:         # Check name length (max 64 characters per spec)
54:         if len(name) > 64:
55:             return False, f"Name is too long ({len(name)} characters). Maximum is 64 characters."
56:     # Extract and validate description
57:     description = frontmatter.get('description', '')
58:     if not isinstance(description, str):
59:         return False, f"Description must be a string, got {type(description).__name__}"
60:     description = description.strip()
61:     if description:
62:         # Check for angle brackets
63:         if '<' in description or '>' in description:
64:             return False, "Description cannot contain angle brackets (< or >)"
65:         if len(description) > 1024:
66:             return False, f"Description is too long ({len(description)} characters). Maximum is 1024 characters."
67:     return True, "Skill is valid!"
68: if __name__ == "__main__":
69:     if len(sys.argv) != 2:
70:         print("Usage: quick_validate.py <skill-name>")
71:         print("       quick_validate.py <absolute-path-to-skill>")
72:         print("\nExamples:")
73:         print("  quick_validate.py my-skill")
74:         print("  quick_validate.py /home/ubuntu/skills/my-skill")
75:         print(f"\nSkills are expected at {SKILLS_BASE_PATH}/<skill-name>/")
76:         sys.exit(1)
77:     skill_input = sys.argv[1]
78:     resolved_path = resolve_skill_path(skill_input)
79:     print(f"🔍 Validating skill at: {resolved_path}")
80:     valid, message = validate_skill(skill_input)
81:     print(message)
82:     sys.exit(0 if valid else 1)

================
File: manus-archive-master/skills/skill-creator/SKILL.md
================
  1: ---
  2: name: skill-creator
  3: description: Guide for creating or updating skills that extend Manus via specialized knowledge, workflows, or tool integrations. For any modification or improvement request, MUST first read this skill and follow its update workflow instead of editing files directly.
  4: license: Complete terms in LICENSE.txt
  5: ---
  6: 
  7: # Skill Creator
  8: 
  9: This skill provides guidance for creating effective skills.
 10: 
 11: ## About Skills
 12: 
 13: Skills are modular, self-contained packages that extend Manus's capabilities by providing specialized knowledge, workflows, and tools. Think of them as "onboarding guides" for specific domains or tasks—they transform Manus from a general-purpose agent into a specialized agent equipped with procedural knowledge that no model can fully possess.
 14: 
 15: ### What Skills Provide
 16: 
 17: 1. Specialized workflows - Multi-step procedures for specific domains
 18: 2. Tool integrations - Instructions for working with specific file formats or APIs
 19: 3. Domain expertise - Company-specific knowledge, schemas, business logic
 20: 4. Bundled resources - Scripts, references, and assets for complex and repetitive tasks
 21: 
 22: ## Core Principles
 23: 
 24: ### Concise is Key
 25: 
 26: The context window is a public good. Skills share the context window with everything else Manus needs: system prompt, conversation history, other Skills' metadata, and the actual user request.
 27: 
 28: **Default assumption: Manus is already very smart.** Only add context Manus doesn't already have. Challenge each piece of information: "Does Manus really need this explanation?" and "Does this paragraph justify its token cost?"
 29: 
 30: Prefer concise examples over verbose explanations.
 31: 
 32: ### Set Appropriate Degrees of Freedom
 33: 
 34: Match the level of specificity to the task's fragility and variability:
 35: 
 36: **High freedom (text-based instructions)**: Use when multiple approaches are valid, decisions depend on context, or heuristics guide the approach.
 37: 
 38: **Medium freedom (pseudocode or scripts with parameters)**: Use when a preferred pattern exists, some variation is acceptable, or configuration affects behavior.
 39: 
 40: **Low freedom (specific scripts, few parameters)**: Use when operations are fragile and error-prone, consistency is critical, or a specific sequence must be followed.
 41: 
 42: Think of Manus as exploring a path: a narrow bridge with cliffs needs specific guardrails (low freedom), while an open field allows many routes (high freedom).
 43: 
 44: ### Anatomy of a Skill
 45: 
 46: Every skill consists of a required SKILL.md file and optional bundled resources:
 47: 
 48: ```
 49: skill-name/
 50: ├── SKILL.md (required)
 51: │   ├── YAML frontmatter metadata (required)
 52: │   │   ├── name: (required)
 53: │   │   └── description: (required)
 54: │   └── Markdown instructions (required)
 55: └── Bundled Resources (optional)
 56:     ├── scripts/          - Executable code (Python/Bash/etc.)
 57:     ├── references/       - Documentation intended to be loaded into context as needed
 58:     └── templates/        - Files used in output (templates, icons, fonts, etc.)
 59: ```
 60: 
 61: #### SKILL.md (required)
 62: 
 63: Every SKILL.md consists of:
 64: 
 65: - **Frontmatter** (YAML): Contains `name` and `description` fields. These are the only fields that Manus reads to determine when the skill gets used, thus it is very important to be clear and comprehensive in describing what the skill is, and when it should be used.
 66: - **Body** (Markdown): Instructions and guidance for using the skill. Only loaded AFTER the skill triggers (if at all).
 67: 
 68: #### Bundled Resources (optional)
 69: 
 70: - **`scripts/`** - Executable code for repetitive or deterministic tasks (e.g., `rotate_pdf.py`). Token efficient, can run without loading into context.
 71: - **`references/`** - Documentation loaded as needed (schemas, API docs, policies). Keeps SKILL.md lean. For large files (>10k words), include grep patterns in SKILL.md.
 72: - **`templates/`** - Output assets not loaded into context (logos, fonts, boilerplate code).
 73: 
 74: **Avoid duplication**: Information lives in SKILL.md OR references, not both.
 75: 
 76: **Do NOT include**: README.md, CHANGELOG.md, or other auxiliary documentation. Skills are for AI agents, not users.
 77: 
 78: ### Progressive Disclosure
 79: 
 80: Three-level loading system:
 81: 1. **Metadata** - Always in context (~100 words)
 82: 2. **SKILL.md body** - When skill triggers (<500 lines)
 83: 3. **Bundled resources** - As needed
 84: 
 85: Keep SKILL.md under 500 lines. When splitting content to references, clearly describe when to read them.
 86: 
 87: **Key principle:** Keep core workflow in SKILL.md; move variant-specific details to reference files.
 88: 
 89: Example structure for multi-domain skills:
 90: 
 91: ```
 92: bigquery-skill/
 93: ├── SKILL.md (overview + navigation)
 94: └── references/
 95:     ├── finance.md
 96:     ├── sales.md
 97:     └── product.md
 98: ```
 99: 
100: Manus only loads the relevant reference file when needed.
101: 
102: ## Skill Creation Process
103: 
104: Skill creation involves these steps:
105: 
106: 1. Understand the skill with concrete examples
107: 2. Plan reusable skill contents (scripts, references, templates)
108: 3. Initialize the skill (run init_skill.py)
109: 4. Edit the skill (implement resources and write SKILL.md)
110: 5. Deliver the skill (send SKILL.md path via notify_user)
111: 6. Iterate based on real usage
112: 
113: Follow these steps in order, skipping only if there is a clear reason why they are not applicable.
114: 
115: ### Step 1: Understanding the Skill with Concrete Examples
116: 
117: Skip this step only when the skill's usage patterns are already clearly understood.
118: 
119: Gather concrete examples of how the skill will be used. Ask questions like:
120: - "What functionality should this skill support?"
121: - "Can you give examples of how it would be used?"
122: 
123: Avoid asking too many questions at once. Conclude when you have a clear sense of the functionality.
124: 
125: ### Step 2: Planning the Reusable Skill Contents
126: 
127: For each example, identify reusable resources:
128: 
129: | Resource Type | When to Use                     | Example                               |
130: | ------------- | ------------------------------- | ------------------------------------- |
131: | `scripts/`    | Code rewritten repeatedly       | `rotate_pdf.py` for PDF rotation      |
132: | `templates/`  | Same boilerplate each time      | HTML/React starter for webapp builder |
133: | `references/` | Documentation needed repeatedly | Database schemas for BigQuery skill   |
134: 
135: ### Step 3: Initializing the Skill
136: 
137: At this point, it is time to actually create the skill.
138: 
139: Skip this step only if the skill being developed already exists, and iteration or packaging is needed. In this case, continue to the next step.
140: 
141: When creating a new skill from scratch, always run the `init_skill.py` script. The script conveniently generates a new template skill directory that automatically includes everything a skill requires, making the skill creation process much more efficient and reliable.
142: 
143: Usage:
144: 
145: ```bash
146: python /home/ubuntu/skills/skill-creator/scripts/init_skill.py <skill-name>
147: ```
148: 
149: The script:
150: 
151: - Creates the skill directory at `/home/ubuntu/skills/<skill-name>/`
152: - Generates a SKILL.md template with proper frontmatter and TODO placeholders
153: - Creates example resource directories: `scripts/`, `references/`, and `templates/`
154: - Adds example files in each directory that can be customized or deleted
155: 
156: After initialization, customize or remove the generated SKILL.md and example files as needed.
157: 
158: ### Step 4: Edit the Skill
159: 
160: When editing the (newly-generated or existing) skill, remember that the skill is being created for another instance of Manus to use. Include information that would be beneficial and non-obvious to Manus. Consider what procedural knowledge, domain-specific details, or reusable assets would help another Manus instance execute these tasks more effectively.
161: 
162: #### Learn Proven Design Patterns
163: 
164: Consult these helpful guides based on your skill's needs:
165: 
166: - **Multi-step processes**: See `/home/ubuntu/skills/skill-creator/references/workflows.md` for sequential workflows and conditional logic
167: - **Output formats or quality standards**: See `/home/ubuntu/skills/skill-creator/references/output-patterns.md` for template and example patterns
168: - **Progressive Disclosure Patterns**: See `/home/ubuntu/skills/skill-creator/references/progressive-disclosure-patterns.md` for splitting content across files.
169: 
170: These files contain established best practices for effective skill design.
171: 
172: #### Start with Reusable Skill Contents
173: 
174: Begin with the `scripts/`, `references/`, and `templates/` files identified in Step 2. This may require user input (e.g., brand assets for `templates/`, documentation for `references/`).
175: 
176: Test added scripts by running them to ensure they work correctly. For many similar scripts, test a representative sample.
177: 
178: Delete any unused example files from initialization.
179: 
180: #### Update SKILL.md
181: 
182: **Writing Guidelines:** Always use imperative/infinitive form.
183: 
184: ##### Frontmatter
185: 
186: Write the YAML frontmatter with `name` and `description`:
187: 
188: - `name`: The skill name
189: - `description`: Primary trigger mechanism. Must include what the skill does AND when to use it (body only loads after triggering).
190:   - Example: "Document creation and editing with tracked changes. Use for: creating .docx files, modifying content, working with tracked changes."
191: 
192: ##### Body
193: 
194: Write instructions for using the skill and its bundled resources.
195: 
196: ### Step 5: Delivering the Skill
197: 
198: Once development of the skill is complete, validate and deliver it to the user.
199: 
200: #### Validate the Skill
201: 
202: Run the validation script to ensure the skill meets all requirements:
203: 
204: ```bash
205: python /home/ubuntu/skills/skill-creator/scripts/quick_validate.py <skill-name>
206: ```
207: 
208: If validation fails, fix the errors and run validation again.
209: 
210: #### Deliver to User
211: 
212: Use `message` tool to send the SKILL.md file as attachment:
213: 
214: ```
215: /home/ubuntu/skills/{skill-name}/SKILL.md
216: ```
217: 
218: The system will automatically:
219: 
220: 1. Detect the path pattern `/home/ubuntu/skills/*/SKILL.md`
221: 2. Package the skill directory into a `.skill` file
222: 3. Send to frontend as a special card with options:
223:    - Add to My Skills
224:    - Download
225:    - Preview
226: 
227: ### Step 6: Iterate
228: 
229: After testing the skill, users may request improvements. Often this happens right after using the skill, with fresh context of how the skill performed.
230: 
231: **Iteration workflow:**
232: 
233: 1. Use the skill on real tasks
234: 2. Notice struggles or inefficiencies
235: 3. Identify how SKILL.md or bundled resources should be updated
236: 4. Implement changes and test again

 13: - Read her voice texts and mistyped messages with intuition. Poor grammar = voice-to-text errors. Decode intent from context.

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/components/ui/accordion.tsx

 1: import * as React from "react";
 2: import * as AccordionPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-accordion";
 3: import { ChevronDownIcon } from "lucide-react";
 4: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 5: function Accordion({
 6:   ...props
 7: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof AccordionPrimitive.Root>) {
 8:   return <AccordionPrimitive.Root data-slot="accordion" {...props} />;
 9: }
10: function AccordionItem({
11:   className,
12:   ...props
13: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof AccordionPrimitive.Item>) {
14:   return (
15:     <AccordionPrimitive.Item
16:       data-slot="accordion-item"
17:       className={cn("border-b last:border-b-0", className)}
18:       {...props}
19:     />
20:   );
21: }
22: function AccordionTrigger({
23:   className,
24:   children,
25:   ...props
26: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof AccordionPrimitive.Trigger>) {
27:   return (
28:     <AccordionPrimitive.Header className="flex">
29:       <AccordionPrimitive.Trigger
30:         data-slot="accordion-trigger"
31:         className={cn(
32:           "focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 flex flex-1 items-start justify-between gap-4 rounded-md py-4 text-left text-sm font-medium transition-all outline-none hover:underline focus-visible:ring-[3px] disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 [&[data-state=open]>svg]:rotate-180",
33:           className
34:         )}
35:         {...props}
36:       >
37:         {children}
38:         <ChevronDownIcon className="text-muted-foreground pointer-events-none size-4 shrink-0 translate-y-0.5 transition-transform duration-200" />
39:       </AccordionPrimitive.Trigger>
40:     </AccordionPrimitive.Header>
41:   );
42: }
43: function AccordionContent({
44:   className,
45:   children,
46:   ...props
47: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof AccordionPrimitive.Content>) {
48:   return (
49:     <AccordionPrimitive.Content
50:       data-slot="accordion-content"

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/components/ui/carousel.tsx

  1: import * as React from "react";
  2: import useEmblaCarousel, {
  3:   type UseEmblaCarouselType,
  4: } from "embla-carousel-react";
  5: import { ArrowLeft, ArrowRight } from "lucide-react";
  6: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  7: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  8: type CarouselApi = UseEmblaCarouselType[1];
  9: type UseCarouselParameters = Parameters<typeof useEmblaCarousel>;
 10: type CarouselOptions = UseCarouselParameters[0];
 11: type CarouselPlugin = UseCarouselParameters[1];
 12: type CarouselProps = {
 13:   opts?: CarouselOptions;
 14:   plugins?: CarouselPlugin;
 15:   orientation?: "horizontal" | "vertical";
 16:   setApi?: (api: CarouselApi) => void;
 17: };
 18: type CarouselContextProps = {
 19:   carouselRef: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[0];
 20:   api: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[1];
 21:   scrollPrev: () => void;
 22:   scrollNext: () => void;
 23:   canScrollPrev: boolean;
 24:   canScrollNext: boolean;
 25: } & CarouselProps;
 26: const CarouselContext = React.createContext<CarouselContextProps | null>(null);
 27: function useCarousel() {
 28:   const context = React.useContext(CarouselContext);
 29:   if (!context) {
 30:     throw new Error("useCarousel must be used within a <Carousel />");
 31:   }
 32:   return context;
 33: }
 34: function Carousel({
 35:   orientation = "horizontal",
 36:   opts,
 37:   setApi,
 38:   plugins,
 39:   className,
 40:   children,
 41:   ...props
 42: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & CarouselProps) {
 43:   const [carouselRef, api] = useEmblaCarousel(
 44:     {
 45:       ...opts,
 46:       axis: orientation === "horizontal" ? "x" : "y",
 47:     },
 48:     plugins
 49:   );
 50:   const [canScrollPrev, setCanScrollPrev] = React.useState(false);
 51:   const [canScrollNext, setCanScrollNext] = React.useState(false);
 52:   const onSelect = React.useCallback((api: CarouselApi) => {
 53:     if (!api) return;
 54:     setCanScrollPrev(api.canScrollPrev());
 55:     setCanScrollNext(api.canScrollNext());
 56:   }, []);
 57:   const scrollPrev = React.useCallback(() => {
 58:     api?.scrollPrev();
 59:   }, [api]);
 60:   const scrollNext = React.useCallback(() => {
 61:     api?.scrollNext();
 62:   }, [api]);
 63:   const handleKeyDown = React.useCallback(
 64:     (event: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
 65:       if (event.key === "ArrowLeft") {
 66:         event.preventDefault();
 67:         scrollPrev();
 68:       } else if (event.key === "ArrowRight") {
 69:         event.preventDefault();
 70:         scrollNext();
 71:       }
 72:     },
 73:     [scrollPrev, scrollNext]
 74:   );
 75:   React.useEffect(() => {
 76:     if (!api || !setApi) return;
 77:     setApi(api);
 78:   }, [api, setApi]);
 79:   React.useEffect(() => {
 80:     if (!api) return;
 81:     onSelect(api);
 82:     api.on("reInit", onSelect);
 83:     api.on("select", onSelect);
 84:     return () => {
 85:       api?.off("select", onSelect);
 86:     };
 87:   }, [api, onSelect]);
 88:   return (
 89:     <CarouselContext.Provider
 90:       value={{
 91:         carouselRef,
 92:         api: api,
 93:         opts,
 94:         orientation:
 95:           orientation || (opts?.axis === "y" ? "vertical" : "horizontal"),
 96:         scrollPrev,
 97:         scrollNext,
 98:         canScrollPrev,
 99:         canScrollNext,
100:       }}
101:     >
102:       <div
103:         onKeyDownCapture={handleKeyDown}
104:         className={cn("relative", className)}
105:         role="region"
106:         aria-roledescription="carousel"
107:         data-slot="carousel"
108:         {...props}
109:       >
110:         {children}
111:       </div>
112:     </CarouselContext.Provider>
113:   );
114: }
115: function CarouselContent({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
116:   const { carouselRef, orientation } = useCarousel();
117:   return (
118:     <div
119:       ref={carouselRef}
120:       className="overflow-hidden"
121:       data-slot="carousel-content"
122:     >
123:       <div
124:         className={cn(
125:           "flex",
126:           orientation === "horizontal" ? "-ml-4" : "-mt-4 flex-col",
127:           className
128:         )}
129:         {...props}
130:       />
131:     </div>
132:   );
133: }
134: function CarouselItem({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
135:   const { orientation } = useCarousel();
136:   return (
137:     <div
138:       role="group"
139:       aria-roledescription="slide"
140:       data-slot="carousel-item"
141:       className={cn(
142:         "min-w-0 shrink-0 grow-0 basis-full",
143:         orientation === "horizontal" ? "pl-4" : "pt-4",
144:         className
145:       )}
146:       {...props}
147:     />
148:   );
149: }
150: function CarouselPrevious({
151:   className,
152:   variant = "outline",
153:   size = "icon",
154:   ...props
155: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Button>) {
156:   const { orientation, scrollPrev, canScrollPrev } = useCarousel();
157:   return (
158:     <Button
159:       data-slot="carousel-previous"
160:       variant={variant}
161:       size={size}
162:       className={cn(
163:         "absolute size-8 rounded-full",
164:         orientation === "horizontal"
165:           ? "top-1/2 -left-12 -translate-y-1/2"
166:           : "-top-12 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 rotate-90",
167:         className
168:       )}
169:       disabled={!canScrollPrev}
170:       onClick={scrollPrev}
171:       {...props}
172:     >
173:       <ArrowLeft />
174:       <span className="sr-only">Previous slide</span>
175:     </Button>
176:   );
177: }
178: function CarouselNext({
179:   className,
180:   variant = "outline",
181:   size = "icon",
182:   ...props
183: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Button>) {
184:   const { orientation, scrollNext, canScrollNext } = useCarousel();
185:   return (
186:     <Button
187:       data-slot="carousel-next"
188:       variant={variant}
189:       size={size}
190:       className={cn(
191:         "absolute size-8 rounded-full",
192:         orientation === "horizontal"
193:           ? "top-1/2 -right-12 -translate-y-1/2"
194:           : "-bottom-12 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 rotate-90",
195:         className
196:       )}
197:       disabled={!canScrollNext}
198:       onClick={scrollNext}
199:       {...props}
200:     >
201:       <ArrowRight />
202:       <span className="sr-only">Next slide</span>
203:     </Button>
204:   );
205: }
206: export {
207:   type CarouselApi,
208:   Carousel,

212:   CarouselNext,
213: };

172:                 ) : (
173:                   <>

175:                       <itemConfig.icon />
176:                     ) : (

228:   hideIcon = false,
229:   payload,
230:   verticalAlign = "bottom",
231:   nameKey,
232: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> &
233:   Pick<RechartsPrimitive.LegendProps, "payload" | "verticalAlign"> & {
234:     hideIcon?: boolean;
235:     nameKey?: string;
236:   }) {
237:   const { config } = useChart();
238:   if (!payload?.length) {
239:     return null;
240:   }
241:   return (
242:     <div
243:       className={cn(
244:         "flex items-center justify-center gap-4",
245:         verticalAlign === "top" ? "pb-3" : "pt-3",
246:         className
247:       )}
248:     >
249:       {payload
250:         .filter(item => item.type !== "none")
251:         .map(item => {
252:           const key = `${nameKey || item.dataKey || "value"}`;
253:           const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);
254:           return (
255:             <div
256:               key={item.value}
257:               className={cn(
258:                 "[&>svg]:text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1.5 [&>svg]:h-3 [&>svg]:w-3"
259:               )}
260:             >
261:               {itemConfig?.icon && !hideIcon ? (
262:                 <itemConfig.icon />
263:               ) : (
264:                 <div
265:                   className="h-2 w-2 shrink-0 rounded-[2px]"
266:                   style={{
267:                     backgroundColor: item.color,
268:                   }}
269:                 />
270:               )}
271:               {itemConfig?.label}
272:             </div>
273:           );
274:         })}
275:     </div>
276:   );
277: }
278: function getPayloadConfigFromPayload(
279:   config: ChartConfig,
280:   payload: unknown,
281:   key: string
282: ) {
283:   if (typeof payload !== "object" || payload === null) {
284:     return undefined;
285:   }
286:   const payloadPayload =
287:     "payload" in payload &&
288:     typeof payload.payload === "object" &&
289:     payload.payload !== null
290:       ? payload.payload
291:       : undefined;
292:   let configLabelKey: string = key;
293:   if (
294:     key in payload &&
295:     typeof payload[key as keyof typeof payload] === "string"
296:   ) {
297:     configLabelKey = payload[key as keyof typeof payload] as string;
298:   } else if (
299:     payloadPayload &&
300:     key in payloadPayload &&
301:     typeof payloadPayload[key as keyof typeof payloadPayload] === "string"
302:   ) {
303:     configLabelKey = payloadPayload[
304:       key as keyof typeof payloadPayload
305:     ] as string;
306:   }
307:   return configLabelKey in config
308:     ? config[configLabelKey]
309:     : config[key as keyof typeof config];
310: }
311: export {
312:   ChartContainer,
313:   ChartTooltip,
314:   ChartTooltipContent,
315:   ChartLegend,
316:   ChartLegendContent,
317:   ChartStyle,
318: };

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/components/ui/dialog.tsx

  1: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  2: import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog";
  3: import { XIcon } from "lucide-react";
  4: import * as React from "react";
  5: const DialogCompositionContext = React.createContext<{
  6:   isComposing: () => boolean;
  7:   setComposing: (composing: boolean) => void;
  8:   justEndedComposing: () => boolean;
  9:   markCompositionEnd: () => void;
 10: }>({
 11:   isComposing: () => false,
 12:   setComposing: () => {},
 13:   justEndedComposing: () => false,
 14:   markCompositionEnd: () => {},
 15: });
 16: export const useDialogComposition = () =>
 17:   React.useContext(DialogCompositionContext);
 18: function Dialog({
 19:   ...props
 20: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Root>) {
 21:   const composingRef = React.useRef(false);
 22:   const justEndedRef = React.useRef(false);
 23:   const endTimerRef = React.useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);
 24:   const contextValue = React.useMemo(
 25:     () => ({
 26:       isComposing: () => composingRef.current,
 27:       setComposing: (composing: boolean) => {
 28:         composingRef.current = composing;
 29:       },
 30:       justEndedComposing: () => justEndedRef.current,
 31:       markCompositionEnd: () => {
 32:         justEndedRef.current = true;
 33:         if (endTimerRef.current) {
 34:           clearTimeout(endTimerRef.current);
 35:         }
 36:         endTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
 37:           justEndedRef.current = false;
 38:         }, 150);
 39:       },
 40:     }),
 41:     []
 42:   );
 43:   return (
 44:     <DialogCompositionContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
 45:       <DialogPrimitive.Root data-slot="dialog" {...props} />
 46:     </DialogCompositionContext.Provider>
 47:   );
 48: }
 49: function DialogTrigger({
 50:   ...props
 51: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Trigger>) {
 52:   return <DialogPrimitive.Trigger data-slot="dialog-trigger" {...props} />;
 53: }
 54: function DialogPortal({
 55:   ...props
 56: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Portal>) {
 57:   return <DialogPrimitive.Portal data-slot="dialog-portal" {...props} />;
 58: }
 59: function DialogClose({
 60:   ...props
 61: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Close>) {
 62:   return <DialogPrimitive.Close data-slot="dialog-close" {...props} />;
 63: }
 64: function DialogOverlay({
 65:   className,
 66:   ...props
 67: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>) {
 68:   return (
 69:     <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
 70:       data-slot="dialog-overlay"
 71:       className={cn(
 72:         "data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/50",
 73:         className
 74:       )}
 75:       {...props}
 76:     />
 77:   );
 78: }
 79: DialogOverlay.displayName = "DialogOverlay";
 80: function DialogContent({
 81:   className,
 82:   children,
 83:   showCloseButton = true,
 84:   onEscapeKeyDown,
 85:   ...props
 86: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content> & {
 87:   showCloseButton?: boolean;
 88: }) {
 89:   const { isComposing } = useDialogComposition();
 90:   const handleEscapeKeyDown = React.useCallback(
 91:     (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
 92:       const isCurrentlyComposing = (e as any).isComposing || isComposing();
 93:       if (isCurrentlyComposing) {
 94:         e.preventDefault();
 95:         return;
 96:       }
 97:       onEscapeKeyDown?.(e);
 98:     },
 99:     [isComposing, onEscapeKeyDown]
100:   );
101:   return (
102:     <DialogPortal data-slot="dialog-portal">
103:       <DialogOverlay />
104:       <DialogPrimitive.Content
105:         data-slot="dialog-content"
106:         className={cn(
107:           "bg-background data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 fixed top-[50%] left-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 rounded-lg border p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 sm:max-w-lg",
108:           className
109:         )}
110:         onEscapeKeyDown={handleEscapeKeyDown}
111:         {...props}
112:       >
113:         {children}
114:         {showCloseButton && (
115:           <DialogPrimitive.Close
116:             data-slot="dialog-close"
117:             className="ring-offset-background focus:ring-ring data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground absolute top-4 right-4 rounded-xs opacity-70 transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 focus:outline-hidden disabled:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:shrink-0 [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4"
118:           >
119:             <XIcon />
120:             <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
121:           </DialogPrimitive.Close>
122:         )}
123:       </DialogPrimitive.Content>
124:     </DialogPortal>
125:   );
126: }
127: function DialogHeader({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
128:   return (
129:     <div
130:       data-slot="dialog-header"
131:       className={cn("flex flex-col gap-2 text-center sm:text-left", className)}
132:       {...props}
133:     />
134:   );
135: }
136: function DialogFooter({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {

143:       )}
144:       {...props}
145:     />
146:   );
147: }

149:   className,
150:   ...props
151: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Title>) {

130:   return (
131:     <p
132:       data-slot="field-description"
133:       className={cn(
134:         "text-muted-foreground text-sm leading-normal font-normal group-has-[[data-orientation=horizontal]]/field:text-balance",
135:         "last:mt-0 nth-last-2:-mt-1 [[data-variant=legend]+&]:-mt-1.5",
136:         "[&>a:hover]:text-primary [&>a]:underline [&>a]:underline-offset-4",
137:         className
138:       )}
139:       {...props}
140:     />
141:   );
142: }
143: function FieldSeparator({
144:   children,
145:   className,
146:   ...props
147: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
148:   children?: React.ReactNode;
149: }) {
150:   return (
151:     <div
152:       data-slot="field-separator"
153:       data-content={!!children}
154:       className={cn(
155:         "relative -my-2 h-5 text-sm group-data-[variant=outline]/field-group:-mb-2",
156:         className
157:       )}
158:       {...props}
159:     >
160:       <Separator className="absolute inset-0 top-1/2" />
161:       {children && (
162:         <span
163:           className="bg-background text-muted-foreground relative mx-auto block w-fit px-2"
164:           data-slot="field-separator-content"
165:         >
166:           {children}
167:         </span>
168:       )}
169:     </div>
170:   );
171: }
172: function FieldError({
173:   className,
174:   children,
175:   errors,
176:   ...props
177: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
178:   errors?: Array<{ message?: string } | undefined>;
179: }) {
180:   const content = useMemo(() => {
181:     if (children) {
182:       return children;
183:     }
184:     if (!errors) {
185:       return null;
186:     }
187:     if (errors?.length === 1 && errors[0]?.message) {
188:       return errors[0].message;
189:     }
190:     return (
191:       <ul className="ml-4 flex list-disc flex-col gap-1">
192:         {errors.map(
193:           (error, index) =>
194:             error?.message && <li key={index}>{error.message}</li>
195:         )}
196:       </ul>
197:     );
198:   }, [children, errors]);
199:   if (!content) {
200:     return null;
201:   }
202:   return (
203:     <div
204:       role="alert"
205:       data-slot="field-error"
206:       className={cn("text-destructive text-sm font-normal", className)}
207:       {...props}
208:     >
209:       {content}
210:     </div>
211:   );
212: }
213: export {
214:   Field,
215:   FieldLabel,
216:   FieldDescription,
217:   FieldError,
218:   FieldGroup,
219:   FieldLegend,
220:   FieldSeparator,
221:   FieldSet,
222:   FieldContent,
223:   FieldTitle,
224: };

  1: "use client";
  2: import * as React from "react";
  3: import * as LabelPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-label";
  4: import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot";
  5: import {
  6:   Controller,
  7:   FormProvider,
  8:   useFormContext,
  9:   useFormState,
 10:   type ControllerProps,
 11:   type FieldPath,
 12:   type FieldValues,
 13: } from "react-hook-form";
 14: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 15: import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
 16: const Form = FormProvider;
 17: type FormFieldContextValue<
 18:   TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
 19:   TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
 20: > = {
 21:   name: TName;
 22: };
 23: const FormFieldContext = React.createContext<FormFieldContextValue>(
 24:   {} as FormFieldContextValue
 25: );
 26: const FormField = <
 27:   TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
 28:   TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
 29: >({
 30:   ...props
 31: }: ControllerProps<TFieldValues, TName>) => {
 32:   return (
 33:     <FormFieldContext.Provider value={{ name: props.name }}>
 34:       <Controller {...props} />
 35:     </FormFieldContext.Provider>
 36:   );
 37: };
 38: const useFormField = () => {
 39:   const fieldContext = React.useContext(FormFieldContext);
 40:   const itemContext = React.useContext(FormItemContext);
 41:   const { getFieldState } = useFormContext();
 42:   const formState = useFormState({ name: fieldContext.name });
 43:   const fieldState = getFieldState(fieldContext.name, formState);
 44:   if (!fieldContext) {
 45:     throw new Error("useFormField should be used within <FormField>");
 46:   }
 47:   const { id } = itemContext;
 48:   return {
 49:     id,
 50:     name: fieldContext.name,
 51:     formItemId: `${id}-form-item`,
 52:     formDescriptionId: `${id}-form-item-description`,
 53:     formMessageId: `${id}-form-item-message`,
 54:     ...fieldState,
 55:   };
 56: };
 57: type FormItemContextValue = {
 58:   id: string;
 59: };
 60: const FormItemContext = React.createContext<FormItemContextValue>(
 61:   {} as FormItemContextValue
 62: );
 63: function FormItem({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
 64:   const id = React.useId();
 65:   return (
 66:     <FormItemContext.Provider value={{ id }}>
 67:       <div
 68:         data-slot="form-item"
 69:         className={cn("grid gap-2", className)}
 70:         {...props}
 71:       />
 72:     </FormItemContext.Provider>
 73:   );
 74: }
 75: function FormLabel({
 76:   className,
 77:   ...props
 78: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof LabelPrimitive.Root>) {
 79:   const { error, formItemId } = useFormField();
 80:   return (
 81:     <Label
 82:       data-slot="form-label"
 83:       data-error={!!error}
 84:       className={cn("data-[error=true]:text-destructive", className)}
 85:       htmlFor={formItemId}
 86:       {...props}
 87:     />
 88:   );
 89: }
 90: function FormControl({ ...props }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Slot>) {
 91:   const { error, formItemId, formDescriptionId, formMessageId } =
 92:     useFormField();
 93:   return (
 94:     <Slot
 95:       data-slot="form-control"
 96:       id={formItemId}
 97:       aria-describedby={
 98:         !error
 99:           ? `${formDescriptionId}`
100:           : `${formDescriptionId} ${formMessageId}`
101:       }
102:       aria-invalid={!!error}
103:       {...props}
104:     />
105:   );
106: }
107: function FormDescription({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
108:   const { formDescriptionId } = useFormField();
109:   return (
110:     <p
111:       data-slot="form-description"
112:       id={formDescriptionId}
113:       className={cn("text-muted-foreground text-sm", className)}
114:       {...props}
115:     />
116:   );
117: }
118: function FormMessage({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
119:   const { error, formMessageId } = useFormField();
120:   const body = error ? String(error?.message ?? "") : props.children;
121:   if (!body) {
122:     return null;
123:   }
124:   return (
125:     <p
126:       data-slot="form-message"
127:       id={formMessageId}
128:       className={cn("text-destructive text-sm", className)}
129:       {...props}
130:     >
131:       {body}
132:     </p>
133:   );
134: }
135: export {
136:   useFormField,
137:   Form,
138:   FormItem,
139:   FormLabel,
140:   FormControl,
141:   FormDescription,
142:   FormMessage,
143:   FormField,
144: };

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/components/ui/input.tsx

 1: import { useDialogComposition } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
 2: import { useComposition } from "@/hooks/useComposition";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: import * as React from "react";
 5: function Input({
 6:   className,
 7:   type,
 8:   onKeyDown,
 9:   onCompositionStart,
10:   onCompositionEnd,
11:   ...props
12: }: React.ComponentProps<"input">) {
13:   const dialogComposition = useDialogComposition();
14:   const {
15:     onCompositionStart: handleCompositionStart,
16:     onCompositionEnd: handleCompositionEnd,
17:     onKeyDown: handleKeyDown,
18:   } = useComposition<HTMLInputElement>({
19:     onKeyDown: (e) => {
20:       const isComposing = (e.nativeEvent as any).isComposing || dialogComposition.justEndedComposing();
21:       if (e.key === "Enter" && isComposing) {
22:         return;
23:       }
24:       onKeyDown?.(e);
25:     },
26:     onCompositionStart: e => {
27:       dialogComposition.setComposing(true);
28:       onCompositionStart?.(e);
29:     },
30:     onCompositionEnd: e => {
31:       dialogComposition.markCompositionEnd();
32:       setTimeout(() => {
33:         dialogComposition.setComposing(false);
34:       }, 100);
35:       onCompositionEnd?.(e);
36:     },
37:   });
38:   return (
39:     <input
40:       type={type}
41:       data-slot="input"
42:       className={cn(
43:         "file:text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground selection:bg-primary selection:text-primary-foreground dark:bg-input/30 border-input h-9 w-full min-w-0 rounded-md border bg-transparent px-3 py-1 text-base shadow-xs transition-[color,box-shadow] outline-none file:inline-flex file:h-7 file:border-0 file:bg-transparent file:text-sm file:font-medium disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 md:text-sm",
44:         "focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px]",
45:         "aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",
46:         className
47:       )}
48:       onCompositionStart={handleCompositionStart}
49:       onCompositionEnd={handleCompositionEnd}
50:       onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
51:       {...props}
52:     />
53:   );
54: }
55: export { Input };

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/components/ui/sidebar.tsx

  1: "use client";
  2: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  3: import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
  4: import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator";
  5: import {
  6:   Sheet,
  7:   SheetContent,
  8:   SheetDescription,
  9:   SheetHeader,
 10:   SheetTitle,
 11: } from "@/components/ui/sheet";
 12: import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
 13: import {
 14:   Tooltip,
 15:   TooltipContent,
 16:   TooltipProvider,
 17:   TooltipTrigger,
 18: } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
 19: import { useIsMobile } from "@/hooks/useMobile";
 20: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 21: import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot";
 22: import { cva, VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority";
 23: import { PanelLeftIcon } from "lucide-react";
 24: import * as React from "react";
 25: const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME = "sidebar_state";
 26: const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE = 60 * 60 * 24 * 7;
 27: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH = "16rem";
 28: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE = "18rem";
 29: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON = "3rem";
 30: const SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT = "b";
 31: type SidebarContextProps = {
 32:   state: "expanded" | "collapsed";
 33:   open: boolean;
 34:   setOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
 35:   openMobile: boolean;
 36:   setOpenMobile: (open: boolean) => void;
 37:   isMobile: boolean;
 38:   toggleSidebar: () => void;
 39: };
 40: const SidebarContext = React.createContext<SidebarContextProps | null>(null);
 41: function useSidebar() {
 42:   const context = React.useContext(SidebarContext);
 43:   if (!context) {
 44:     throw new Error("useSidebar must be used within a SidebarProvider.");
 45:   }
 46:   return context;
 47: }
 48: function SidebarProvider({
 49:   defaultOpen = true,
 50:   open: openProp,
 51:   onOpenChange: setOpenProp,
 52:   className,
 53:   style,
 54:   children,
 55:   ...props
 56: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
 57:   defaultOpen?: boolean;
 58:   open?: boolean;
 59:   onOpenChange?: (open: boolean) => void;
 60: }) {
 61:   const isMobile = useIsMobile();
 62:   const [openMobile, setOpenMobile] = React.useState(false);
 63:   const [_open, _setOpen] = React.useState(defaultOpen);
 64:   const open = openProp ?? _open;
 65:   const setOpen = React.useCallback(
 66:     (value: boolean | ((value: boolean) => boolean)) => {
 67:       const openState = typeof value === "function" ? value(open) : value;
 68:       if (setOpenProp) {
 69:         setOpenProp(openState);
 70:       } else {
 71:         _setOpen(openState);
 72:       }
 73:       document.cookie = `${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME}=${openState}; path=/; max-age=${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE}`;
 74:     },
 75:     [setOpenProp, open]
 76:   );
 77:   const toggleSidebar = React.useCallback(() => {
 78:     return isMobile ? setOpenMobile(open => !open) : setOpen(open => !open);
 79:   }, [isMobile, setOpen, setOpenMobile]);
 80:   React.useEffect(() => {
 81:     const handleKeyDown = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
 82:       if (
 83:         event.key === SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT &&
 84:         (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey)
 85:       ) {
 86:         event.preventDefault();
 87:         toggleSidebar();
 88:       }
 89:     };
 90:     window.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
 91:     return () => window.removeEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
 92:   }, [toggleSidebar]);
 93:   const state = open ? "expanded" : "collapsed";
 94:   const contextValue = React.useMemo<SidebarContextProps>(
 95:     () => ({
 96:       state,
 97:       open,
 98:       setOpen,
 99:       isMobile,
100:       openMobile,
101:       setOpenMobile,
102:       toggleSidebar,
103:     }),
104:     [state, open, setOpen, isMobile, openMobile, setOpenMobile, toggleSidebar]
105:   );
106:   return (
107:     <SidebarContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
108:       <TooltipProvider delayDuration={0}>
109:         <div
110:           data-slot="sidebar-wrapper"
111:           style={
112:             {
113:               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH,
114:               "--sidebar-width-icon": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON,
115:               ...style,
116:             } as React.CSSProperties
117:           }
118:           className={cn(
119:             "group/sidebar-wrapper has-data-[variant=inset]:bg-sidebar flex min-h-svh w-full",
120:             className
121:           )}
122:           {...props}
123:         >
124:           {children}
125:         </div>
126:       </TooltipProvider>
127:     </SidebarContext.Provider>
128:   );
129: }
130: function Sidebar({
131:   side = "left",
132:   variant = "sidebar",
133:   collapsible = "offcanvas",
134:   disableTransition = false,
135:   className,
136:   children,
137:   ...props
138: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
139:   side?: "left" | "right";
140:   variant?: "sidebar" | "floating" | "inset";
141:   collapsible?: "offcanvas" | "icon" | "none";
142:   disableTransition?: boolean;
143: }) {
144:   const { isMobile, state, openMobile, setOpenMobile } = useSidebar();
145:   if (collapsible === "none") {
146:     return (
147:       <div
148:         data-slot="sidebar"
149:         className={cn(
150:           "bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground flex h-full w-(--sidebar-width) flex-col",
151:           className
152:         )}
153:         {...props}
154:       >
155:         {children}
156:       </div>
157:     );
158:   }
159:   if (isMobile) {
160:     return (
161:       <Sheet open={openMobile} onOpenChange={setOpenMobile} {...props}>
162:         <SheetContent
163:           data-sidebar="sidebar"
164:           data-slot="sidebar"
165:           data-mobile="true"
166:           className="bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground w-(--sidebar-width) p-0 [&>button]:hidden"
167:           style={
168:             {
169:               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE,
170:             } as React.CSSProperties
171:           }
172:           side={side}
173:         >
174:           <SheetHeader className="sr-only">
175:             <SheetTitle>Sidebar</SheetTitle>
176:             <SheetDescription>Displays the mobile sidebar.</SheetDescription>
177:           </SheetHeader>
178:           <div className="flex h-full w-full flex-col">{children}</div>
179:         </SheetContent>
180:       </Sheet>
181:     );
182:   }
183:   return (
184:     <div
185:       className="group peer text-sidebar-foreground hidden md:block"
186:       data-state={state}
187:       data-collapsible={state === "collapsed" ? collapsible : ""}
188:       data-variant={variant}
189:       data-side={side}
190:       data-slot="sidebar"
191:     >
192:       {}
193:       <div
194:         data-slot="sidebar-gap"
195:         className={cn(
196:           "relative w-(--sidebar-width) bg-transparent",
197:           disableTransition
198:             ? "transition-none"
199:             : "transition-[width] duration-200 ease-linear",
200:           "group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:w-0",
201:           "group-data-[side=right]:rotate-180",
202:           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
203:             ? "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+(--spacing(4)))]"
204:             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-(--sidebar-width-icon)"
205:         )}
206:       />
207:       <div
208:         data-slot="sidebar-container"
209:         className={cn(
210:           "fixed inset-y-0 z-10 hidden h-svh w-(--sidebar-width) md:flex",
211:           disableTransition
212:             ? "transition-none"
213:             : "transition-[left,right,width] duration-200 ease-linear",
214:           side === "left"
215:             ? "left-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:left-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]"
216:             : "right-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:right-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]",
217:           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
218:             ? "p-2 group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+(--spacing(4))+2px)]"
219:             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-(--sidebar-width-icon) group-data-[side=left]:border-r group-data-[side=right]:border-l",
220:           className
221:         )}
222:         {...props}
223:       >
224:         <div
225:           data-sidebar="sidebar"
226:           data-slot="sidebar-inner"
227:           className="bg-sidebar group-data-[variant=floating]:border-sidebar-border flex h-full w-full flex-col group-data-[variant=floating]:rounded-lg group-data-[variant=floating]:border group-data-[variant=floating]:shadow-sm"
228:         >
229:           {children}
230:         </div>
231:       </div>
232:     </div>
233:   );
234: }

436: const sidebarMenuButtonVariants = cva(
437:   "peer/menu-button flex w-full items-center gap-2 overflow-hidden rounded-md p-2 text-left text-sm outline-hidden ring-sidebar-ring transition-[width,height,padding] hover:bg-sidebar-accent hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground focus-visible:ring-2 active:bg-sidebar-accent active:text-sidebar-accent-foreground disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 group-has-data-[sidebar=menu-action]/menu-item:pr-8 aria-disabled:pointer-events-none aria-disabled:opacity-50 data-[active=true]:bg-sidebar-accent data-[active=true]:font-medium data-[active=true]:text-sidebar-accent-foreground data-[state=open]:hover:bg-sidebar-accent data-[state=open]:hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground group-data-[collapsible=icon]:size-8! group-data-[collapsible=icon]:p-2! [&>span:last-child]:truncate [&>svg]:size-4 [&>svg]:shrink-0",
438:   {

444:       },

457: function SidebarMenuButton({
458:   asChild = false,
459:   isActive = false,
460:   variant = "default",
461:   size = "default",
462:   tooltip,
463:   className,
464:   ...props
465: }: React.ComponentProps<"button"> & {
466:   asChild?: boolean;
467:   isActive?: boolean;
468:   tooltip?: string | React.ComponentProps<typeof TooltipContent>;
469: } & VariantProps<typeof sidebarMenuButtonVariants>) {
470:   const Comp = asChild ? Slot : "button";
471:   const { isMobile, state } = useSidebar();
472:   const button = (
473:     <Comp
474:       data-slot="sidebar-menu-button"
475:       data-sidebar="menu-button"
476:       data-size={size}
477:       data-active={isActive}
478:       className={cn(sidebarMenuButtonVariants({ variant, size }), className)}
479:       {...props}
480:     />
481:   );
482:   if (!tooltip) {
483:     return button;
484:   }
485:   if (typeof tooltip === "string") {
486:     tooltip = {
487:       children: tooltip,
488:     };
489:   }
490:   return (
491:     <Tooltip>
492:       <TooltipTrigger asChild>{button}</TooltipTrigger>
493:       <TooltipContent
494:         side="right"
495:         align="center"
496:         hidden={state !== "collapsed" || isMobile}
497:         {...tooltip}
498:       />
499:     </Tooltip>
500:   );
501: }

 1: import * as React from "react";
 2: import * as SliderPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-slider";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: function Slider({
 5:   className,
 6:   defaultValue,
 7:   value,
 8:   min = 0,
 9:   max = 100,
10:   ...props
11: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof SliderPrimitive.Root>) {
12:   const _values = React.useMemo(
13:     () =>
14:       Array.isArray(value)
15:         ? value
16:         : Array.isArray(defaultValue)
17:           ? defaultValue
18:           : [min, max],
19:     [value, defaultValue, min, max]
20:   );
21:   return (
22:     <SliderPrimitive.Root
23:       data-slot="slider"
24:       defaultValue={defaultValue}
25:       value={value}
26:       min={min}
27:       max={max}
28:       className={cn(
29:         "relative flex w-full touch-none items-center select-none data-[disabled]:opacity-50 data-[orientation=vertical]:h-full data-[orientation=vertical]:min-h-44 data-[orientation=vertical]:w-auto data-[orientation=vertical]:flex-col",
30:         className
31:       )}
32:       {...props}
33:     >
34:       <SliderPrimitive.Track
35:         data-slot="slider-track"
36:         className={cn(
37:           "bg-muted relative grow overflow-hidden rounded-full data-[orientation=horizontal]:h-1.5 data-[orientation=horizontal]:w-full data-[orientation=vertical]:h-full data-[orientation=vertical]:w-1.5"
38:         )}
39:       >
40:         <SliderPrimitive.Range
41:           data-slot="slider-range"
42:           className={cn(
43:             "bg-primary absolute data-[orientation=horizontal]:h-full data-[orientation=vertical]:w-full"
44:           )}
45:         />
46:       </SliderPrimitive.Track>
47:       {Array.from({ length: _values.length }, (_, index) => (
48:         <SliderPrimitive.Thumb
49:           data-slot="slider-thumb"
50:           key={index}
51:           className="border-primary ring-ring/50 block size-4 shrink-0 rounded-full border bg-white shadow-sm transition-[color,box-shadow] hover:ring-4 focus-visible:ring-4 focus-visible:outline-hidden disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50"
52:         />
53:       ))}
54:     </SliderPrimitive.Root>
55:   );
56: }
57: export { Slider };

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/components/ui/textarea.tsx

 1: import { useDialogComposition } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
 2: import { useComposition } from "@/hooks/useComposition";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: import * as React from "react";
 5: function Textarea({
 6:   className,
 7:   onKeyDown,
 8:   onCompositionStart,
 9:   onCompositionEnd,
10:   ...props
11: }: React.ComponentProps<"textarea">) {
12:   const dialogComposition = useDialogComposition();
13:   const {
14:     onCompositionStart: handleCompositionStart,
15:     onCompositionEnd: handleCompositionEnd,
16:     onKeyDown: handleKeyDown,
17:   } = useComposition<HTMLTextAreaElement>({
18:     onKeyDown: (e) => {
19:       const isComposing = (e.nativeEvent as any).isComposing || dialogComposition.justEndedComposing();
20:       if (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey && isComposing) {
21:         return;
22:       }
23:       onKeyDown?.(e);
24:     },
25:     onCompositionStart: e => {
26:       dialogComposition.setComposing(true);
27:       onCompositionStart?.(e);
28:     },
29:     onCompositionEnd: e => {
30:       dialogComposition.markCompositionEnd();
31:       setTimeout(() => {
32:         dialogComposition.setComposing(false);
33:       }, 100);
34:       onCompositionEnd?.(e);
35:     },
36:   });
37:   return (
38:     <textarea
39:       data-slot="textarea"
40:       className={cn(
41:         "border-input placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive dark:bg-input/30 flex field-sizing-content min-h-16 w-full rounded-md border bg-transparent px-3 py-2 text-base shadow-xs transition-[color,box-shadow] outline-none focus-visible:ring-[3px] disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 md:text-sm",
42:         className
43:       )}
44:       onCompositionStart={handleCompositionStart}
45:       onCompositionEnd={handleCompositionEnd}
46:       onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
47:       {...props}
48:     />
49:   );
50: }

 6:   "inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-md text-sm font-medium hover:bg-muted hover:text-muted-foreground disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 data-[state=on]:bg-accent data-[state=on]:text-accent-foreground [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4 [&_svg]:shrink-0 focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px] outline-none transition-[color,box-shadow] aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive whitespace-nowrap",
 7:   {
 8:     variants: {
 9:       variant: {

 1: import { useRef } from 'react'
 2: import { motion, useScroll, useTransform } from 'framer-motion'
 3: const MessageFromCouple = () => {
 4:   const ref = useRef(null)
 5:   const { scrollYProgress } = useScroll({
 6:     target: ref,
 7:     offset: ["start 0.8", "end 0.2"]
 8:   })
 9:   const message = "We're getting married! And we're so excited to celebrate our day with you. On this page, you'll find everything you need to know – schedule, location, dress code, accommodation – and you can RSVP directly here. See you this summer!"
10:   const words = message.split(' ')
11:   return (
12:     <section className="py-20 bg-cream" ref={ref}>
13:       <div className="container mx-auto px-6">
14:         <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto text-center">
15:           {}
16:           <motion.div
17:             className="flex justify-center space-x-2 mb-8"
18:             initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
19:             whileInView={{ opacity: 1 }}
20:             transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
21:             viewport={{ once: true }}
22:           >
23:             <span className="text-charcoal/60">♥</span>
24:             <span className="text-charcoal/60">♥</span>
25:             <span className="text-charcoal/60">♥</span>
26:           </motion.div>
27:           <div className="text-2xl md:text-3xl leading-relaxed text-charcoal font-light">
28:             {words.map((word, index) => {
29:               const wordProgress = useTransform(
30:                 scrollYProgress,
31:                 [index / words.length, (index + 1) / words.length],
32:                 [0, 1]
33:               )
34:               return (
35:                 <motion.span
36:                   key={index}
37:                   className="inline-block mr-2"
38:                   style={{
39:                     color: useTransform(
40:                       wordProgress,
41:                       [0, 0.5, 1],
42:                       ['#D1C7BD', '#8B7D6B', '#2D2D2D']
43:                     )
44:                   }}
45:                 >
46:                   {word}
47:                 </motion.span>
48:               )
49:             })}
50:           </div>
51:         </div>
52:       </div>
53:     </section>
54:   )
55: }
56: export default MessageFromCouple

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/components/wedding/Navigation.tsx
================
 1: import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
 2: import { motion } from 'framer-motion'
 3: const Navigation = () => {
 4:   const [isScrolled, setIsScrolled] = useState(false)
 5:   useEffect(() => {
 6:     const handleScroll = () => {
 7:       const scrollPosition = window.scrollY
 8:       setIsScrolled(scrollPosition > window.innerHeight * 0.8)
 9:     }
10:     window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
11:     return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll)
12:   }, [])
13:   const navItems = ['Location', 'The Day', 'FAQ']
14:   return (
15:     <motion.nav
16:       className={`fixed top-0 left-0 right-0 z-50 transition-all duration-300 ${
17:         isScrolled ? 'bg-charcoal text-cream' : 'bg-transparent text-white'
18:       }`}
19:       initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
20:       animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
21:       transition={{ duration: 0.5 }}
22:     >
23:       <div className="container mx-auto px-6 py-4">
24:         <div className="flex justify-between items-center">
25:           <div className="flex space-x-8">
26:             {navItems.map((item, index) => (
27:               <a
28:                 key={index}
29:                 href={`#${item.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g, '-')}`}
30:                 className="hover:opacity-70 transition-opacity duration-200"
31:               >
32:                 {item}
33:               </a>
34:             ))}
35:           </div>
36:           {isScrolled && (
37:             <motion.div
38:               className="text-xl font-serif"
39:               initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
40:               animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
41:               transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
42:             >
43:               Emma & Karl
44:             </motion.div>
45:           )}
46:         </div>
47:       </div>
48:     </motion.nav>
49:   )
50: }
51: export default Navigation

 1: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 2: import { AlertTriangle, RotateCcw } from "lucide-react";
 3: import { Component, ReactNode } from "react";
 4: interface Props {
 5:   children: ReactNode;
 6: }
 7: interface State {
 8:   hasError: boolean;
 9:   error: Error | null;
10: }
11: class ErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {
12:   constructor(props: Props) {
13:     super(props);
14:     this.state = { hasError: false, error: null };
15:   }
16:   static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): State {
17:     return { hasError: true, error };
18:   }
19:   render() {
20:     if (this.state.hasError) {
21:       return (
22:         <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-8 bg-background">
23:           <div className="flex flex-col items-center w-full max-w-2xl p-8">
24:             <AlertTriangle
25:               size={48}
26:               className="text-destructive mb-6 flex-shrink-0"
27:             />
28:             <h2 className="text-xl mb-4">An unexpected error occurred.</h2>
29:             <div className="p-4 w-full rounded bg-muted overflow-auto mb-6">
30:               <pre className="text-sm text-muted-foreground whitespace-break-spaces">
31:                 {this.state.error?.stack}
32:               </pre>
33:             </div>
34:             <button
35:               onClick={() => window.location.reload()}
36:               className={cn(
37:                 "flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg",
38:                 "bg-primary text-primary-foreground",
39:                 "hover:opacity-90 cursor-pointer"
40:               )}
41:             >
42:               <RotateCcw size={16} />
43:               Reload Page
44:             </button>
45:           </div>
46:         </div>
47:       );
48:     }
49:     return this.props.children;
50:   }
51: }
52: export default ErrorBoundary;
