 1: import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
 2: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 3: import { APP_LOGO, APP_TITLE } from "@/const";
 4: import {
 5:   Dialog,
 6:   DialogContent,
 7:   DialogDescription,
 8:   DialogFooter,
 9:   DialogTitle,
10: } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
11: interface ManusDialogProps {
12:   title?: string;
13:   logo?: string;
14:   open?: boolean;
15:   onLogin: () => void;
16:   onOpenChange?: (open: boolean) => void;
17:   onClose?: () => void;
18: }
19: export function ManusDialog({
20:   title = APP_TITLE,
21:   logo = APP_LOGO,
22:   open = false,
23:   onLogin,
24:   onOpenChange,
25:   onClose,
26: }: ManusDialogProps) {
27:   const [internalOpen, setInternalOpen] = useState(open);
28:   useEffect(() => {
29:     if (!onOpenChange) {
30:       setInternalOpen(open);
31:     }
32:   }, [open, onOpenChange]);
33:   const handleOpenChange = (nextOpen: boolean) => {
34:     if (onOpenChange) {
35:       onOpenChange(nextOpen);
36:     } else {
37:       setInternalOpen(nextOpen);
38:     }
39:     if (!nextOpen) {
40:       onClose?.();
41:     }
42:   };
43:   return (
44:     <Dialog
45:       open={onOpenChange ? open : internalOpen}
46:       onOpenChange={handleOpenChange}
47:     >
48:       <DialogContent className="py-5 bg-[#f8f8f7] rounded-[20px] w-[400px] shadow-[0px_4px_11px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.08)] border border-[rgba(0,0,0,0.08)] backdrop-blur-2xl p-0 gap-0 text-center">
49:         <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2 p-5 pt-12">
50:           <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-white rounded-xl border border-[rgba(0,0,0,0.08)] flex items-center justify-center">
51:             <img src={logo} alt="App icon" className="w-10 h-10 rounded-md" />
52:           </div>
53:           {}
54:           <DialogTitle className="text-xl font-semibold text-[#34322d] leading-[26px] tracking-[-0.44px]">
55:             {title}
56:           </DialogTitle>
57:           <DialogDescription className="text-sm text-[#858481] leading-5 tracking-[-0.154px]">
58:             Please login with Manus to continue
59:           </DialogDescription>
60:         </div>
61:         <DialogFooter className="px-5 py-5">
62:           {}
63:           <Button
64:             onClick={onLogin}
65:             className="w-full h-10 bg-[#1a1a19] hover:bg-[#1a1a19]/90 text-white rounded-[10px] text-sm font-medium leading-5 tracking-[-0.154px]"
66:           >
67:             Login with Manus
68:           </Button>

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/contexts/ThemeContext.tsx
================
 1: import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from "react";
 2: type Theme = "light" | "dark";
 3: interface ThemeContextType {
 4:   theme: Theme;
 5:   toggleTheme?: () => void;
 6:   switchable: boolean;
 7: }
 8: const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextType | undefined>(undefined);
 9: interface ThemeProviderProps {
10:   children: React.ReactNode;
11:   defaultTheme?: Theme;
12:   switchable?: boolean;
13: }
14: export function ThemeProvider({
15:   children,
16:   defaultTheme = "light",
17:   switchable = false,
18: }: ThemeProviderProps) {
19:   const [theme, setTheme] = useState<Theme>(() => {
20:     if (switchable) {
21:       const stored = localStorage.getItem("theme");
22:       return (stored as Theme) || defaultTheme;
23:     }
24:     return defaultTheme;
25:   });
26:   useEffect(() => {
27:     const root = document.documentElement;
28:     if (theme === "dark") {
29:       root.classList.add("dark");
30:     } else {
31:       root.classList.remove("dark");
32:     }
33:     if (switchable) {
34:       localStorage.setItem("theme", theme);
35:     }
36:   }, [theme, switchable]);
37:   const toggleTheme = switchable
38:     ? () => {
39:         setTheme(prev => (prev === "light" ? "dark" : "light"));
40:       }
41:     : undefined;
42:   return (
43:     <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, toggleTheme, switchable }}>
44:       {children}
45:     </ThemeContext.Provider>
46:   );
47: }
48: export function useTheme() {
49:   const context = useContext(ThemeContext);
50:   if (!context) {
51:     throw new Error("useTheme must be used within ThemeProvider");
52:   }
53:   return context;
54: }

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/hooks/useComposition.ts
================
 1: import { useRef } from "react";
 2: import { usePersistFn } from "./usePersistFn";
 3: export interface UseCompositionReturn<
 4:   T extends HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement,
 5: > {
 6:   onCompositionStart: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
 7:   onCompositionEnd: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
 8:   onKeyDown: React.KeyboardEventHandler<T>;
 9:   isComposing: () => boolean;
10: }
11: export interface UseCompositionOptions<
12:   T extends HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement,
13: > {
14:   onKeyDown?: React.KeyboardEventHandler<T>;
15:   onCompositionStart?: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
16:   onCompositionEnd?: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
17: }
18: type TimerResponse = ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>;
19: export function useComposition<
20:   T extends HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement = HTMLInputElement,
21: >(options: UseCompositionOptions<T> = {}): UseCompositionReturn<T> {
22:   const {
23:     onKeyDown: originalOnKeyDown,
24:     onCompositionStart: originalOnCompositionStart,
25:     onCompositionEnd: originalOnCompositionEnd,
26:   } = options;
27:   const c = useRef(false);
28:   const timer = useRef<TimerResponse | null>(null);
29:   const timer2 = useRef<TimerResponse | null>(null);
30:   const onCompositionStart = usePersistFn((e: React.CompositionEvent<T>) => {
31:     if (timer.current) {
32:       clearTimeout(timer.current);
33:       timer.current = null;
34:     }
35:     if (timer2.current) {
36:       clearTimeout(timer2.current);
37:       timer2.current = null;
38:     }
39:     c.current = true;
40:     originalOnCompositionStart?.(e);
41:   });
42:   const onCompositionEnd = usePersistFn((e: React.CompositionEvent<T>) => {
43:     timer.current = setTimeout(() => {
44:       timer2.current = setTimeout(() => {
45:         c.current = false;
46:       });
47:     });
48:     originalOnCompositionEnd?.(e);
49:   });
50:   const onKeyDown = usePersistFn((e: React.KeyboardEvent<T>) => {
51:     if (
52:       c.current &&
53:       (e.key === "Escape" || (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey))
54:     ) {
55:       e.stopPropagation();
56:       return;
57:     }
58:     originalOnKeyDown?.(e);
59:   });
60:   const isComposing = usePersistFn(() => {
61:     return c.current;
62:   });
63:   return {
64:     onCompositionStart,
65:     onCompositionEnd,
66:     onKeyDown,
67:     isComposing,
68:   };
69: }

File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/hooks/useMobile.tsx
================
 1: import * as React from "react";
 2: const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768;
 3: export function useIsMobile() {
 4:   const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(
 5:     undefined
 6:   );
 7:   React.useEffect(() => {
 8:     const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`);
 9:     const onChange = () => {
10:       setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
11:     };
12:     mql.addEventListener("change", onChange);
13:     setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
14:     return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange);
15:   }, []);
16:   return !!isMobile;
17: }

================
File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/client/src/hooks/usePersistFn.ts
================
 1: import { useRef } from "react";
 2: type noop = (...args: any[]) => any;
 3: export function usePersistFn<T extends noop>(fn: T) {
 4:   const fnRef = useRef<T>(fn);
 5:   fnRef.current = fn;
 6:   const persistFn = useRef<T>(null);
 7:   if (!persistFn.current) {
 8:     persistFn.current = function (this: unknown, ...args) {
 9:       return fnRef.current!.apply(this, args);
10:     } as T;
11:   }
12:   return persistFn.current!;
13: }

1: import { clsx, type ClassValue } from "clsx";
2: import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge";
3: export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
4:   return twMerge(clsx(inputs));
5: }

12:   url.searchParams.set("appId", appId);
13:   url.searchParams.set("redirectUri", redirectUri);
14:   url.searchParams.set("state", state);
15:   url.searchParams.set("type", "signIn");
16:   return url.toString();
17: };

 2: import { createServer } from "http";
 3: import path from "path";
 4: import { fileURLToPath } from "url";
 5: const __filename = fileURLToPath(import.meta.url);
 6: const __dirname = path.dirname(__filename);
 7: async function startServer() {
 8:   const app = express();
 9:   const server = createServer(app);
10:   const staticPath =
11:     process.env.NODE_ENV === "production"
12:       ? path.resolve(__dirname, "public")
13:       : path.resolve(__dirname, "..", "dist", "public");
14:   app.use(express.static(staticPath));
15:   app.get("*", (_req, res) => {
16:     res.sendFile(path.join(staticPath, "index.html"));
17:   });
18:   const port = process.env.PORT || 3000;
19:   server.listen(port, () => {
20:     console.log(`Server running on http://localhost:${port}/`);
21:   });
22: }
23: startServer().catch(console.error);

================
File: manus-archive-master/templates/elegant-wedding-template/elegant-wedding-template/README.md
================
  1: # Web App Template (Static Frontend)
  2: 
  3: Pure React + Tailwind template with shadcn/ui baked in. **Use this README as the checklist for shipping static experiences.**
  4: 
  5: > **Note:** This template includes a minimal `shared/` and `server/` directory with placeholder types to support imported templates. These are just compatibility placeholders - web-static remains a true static-only template without API functionality.
  6: 
  7: ---
  8: 
  9: ## 🤖 AI Development Guide
 10: 
 11: ### Stack Overview
 12: - Client-only routing powered by React + Wouter.
 13: - Design tokens are provided through `client/src/index.css` and `tailwind.config.ts`—keep them intact.
 14: 
 15: ### Component Patterns
 16: 
 17: ```tsx
 18: // Compose pages from shadcn/ui primitives
 19: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 20: 
 21: export function Hero() {
 22:   return (
 23:     <section className="rounded-3xl bg-white p-10 shadow-xl">
 24:       <h1 className="text-4xl font-bold text-slate-900">Launch Quickly</h1>
 25:       <Button size="lg" className="mt-6">Get Started</Button>
 26:     </section>
 27:   );
 28: }
 29: ```
 30: 
 31: ### File Structure
 32: 
 33: ```
 34: client/
 35:   public/         ← Static assets copied verbatim to '/'
 36:   src/
 37:     pages/        ← Page-level components
 38:     components/   ← Reusable UI & shadcn/ui
 39:     contexts/     ← React contexts
 40:     hooks/        ← Custom React hooks
 41:     lib/          ← Utility helpers
 42:     App.tsx       ← Routes & top-level layout
 43:     main.tsx      ← React entry point
 44:     index.css     ← global style
 45: server/         ← Placeholder for imported template compatibility
 46: shared/         ← Placeholder for imported template compatibility
 47:   const.ts      ← Shared constants
 48: ```
 49: 
 50: Assets placed under `client/public` are served with aggressive caching, so add a content hash to filenames (for example, `logo.3fa9b2e4.svg`) whenever you replace a file and update its references to avoid stale assets.
 51: 
 52: Files in `client/public` are available at the root of your site—reference them with absolute paths (`/logo.3fa9b2e4.svg`, `/robots.txt`, etc.) from HTML templates, JSX, or meta tags.
 53: 
 54: ---
 55: 
 56: ## 🎯 Development Workflow
 57: 
 58: 1. **Compose pages** in `client/src/pages/`. Keep sections modular so they can be reused across routes.
 59: 2. **Share primitives** via `client/src/components/`—extend shadcn/ui when needed instead of duplicating markup.
 60: 3. **Keep styling consistent** by relying on existing Tailwind tokens (spacing, colors, typography).
 61: 4. **Fetch external data** with `useEffect` if the site needs dynamic content from public APIs.
 62: 
 63: ---
 64: 
 65: ## 🧱 Tailwind Safeguards
 66: 
 67: - Preserve the `@layer base` block in `client/src/index.css`; removing it breaks utilities like `border-border`.
 68: - Do not strip values from `theme.extend` in `tailwind.config.ts`—they power the design tokens used in the UI kit.
 69: - Stick to utility classes for responsiveness (mobile-first by default).
 70: ## ✅ Launch Checklist
 71: - [ ] UI layout and navigation structure correct, all image src valid.
 72: - [ ] Success + error paths verified in the browser
 73: 
 74: ---
 75: 
 76: ## 🎨 Frontend Best Practices (shadcn-first)
 77: 
 78: - Prefer shadcn/ui components for interactions to keep a modern, consistent look; import from `@/components/ui/*` (e.g., `button`, `card`, `dialog`).
 79: - Compose Tailwind utilities with component variants for layout and states; avoid excessive custom CSS. Use built-in `variant`, `size`, etc. where available.
 80: - Preserve design tokens: keep the `@layer base` rules in `client/src/index.css`. Utilities like `border-border` and `font-sans` depend on them.
 81: - Consistent design language: use spacing, radius, shadows, and typography via tokens. Extract shared UI into `components/` for reuse instead of copy‑paste.
 82: - Accessibility and responsiveness: keep visible focus rings and ensure keyboard reachability; design mobile‑first with thoughtful breakpoints.
 83: - Theming: Choose dark/light theme to start with for ThemeProvider according to your design style (dark or light bg), then manage colors pallette with CSS variables in `client/src/index.css` instead of hard‑coding to keep global consistency;
 84: - Micro‑interactions and empty states: add motion, empty states, and icons tastefully to improve quality without distracting from content.
 85: - Navigation: Design clear and intuitive navigation structure appropriate for the app type (e.g., top/side nav for multi-page apps, breadcrumbs or contextual navigation for SPAs)'. When building dashboard-like experience, use sidebar-nav to keep all page entry easy to access.
 86: 
 87: **React component rules:**
 88: - Never call setState/navigation in render phase → wrap in `useEffect`
 89: 
 90: ---
 91: 
 92: ## Common Pitfalls
 93: 
 94: ### Infinite loading loops from unstable references
 95: **Anti-pattern:** Creating new objects/arrays in render that are used as query inputs
 96: ```tsx
 97: // ❌ Bad: New Date() creates new reference every render → infinite queries
 98: const { data } = trpc.items.getByDate.useQuery({
 99:   date: new Date(), // ← New object every render!
100: });
101: 
102: // ❌ Bad: Array/object literals in query input
103: const { data } = trpc.items.getByIds.useQuery({
104:   ids: [1, 2, 3], // ← New array reference every render!
105: });
106: ```
107: 
108: **Correct approach:** Stabilize references with useState/useMemo
109: ```tsx
110: // ✅ Good: Initialize once with useState
111: const [date] = useState(() => new Date());
112: const { data } = trpc.items.getByDate.useQuery({ date });
113: 
114: // ✅ Good: Memoize complex inputs
115: const ids = useMemo(() => [1, 2, 3], []);
116: const { data } = trpc.items.getByIds.useQuery({ ids });
117: ```
118: 
119: **Why this happens:** TRPC queries trigger when input references change. Objects/arrays created in render have new references each time, causing infinite re-fetches.
120: 
121: ### Navigation dead-ends in subpages
122: **Problem:** Creating nested routes without escape routes—no header nav, no sidebar, no back button.
123: 
124: **Solution:** Choose navigation based on app structure:
125: ```tsx
126: // For dashboard/multi-section apps: Use persistent sidebar (from shadcn/ui)
127: import { SidebarProvider, Sidebar, SidebarContent, SidebarInset } from "@/components/ui/sidebar";
128: 
129: <SidebarProvider>
130:   <Sidebar>
131:     <SidebarContent>
132:       {/* Navigation menu items - always visible */}
133:     </SidebarContent>
134:   </Sidebar>
135:   <SidebarInset>
136:     {children}  {/* Page content */}
137:   </SidebarInset>
138: </SidebarProvider>
139: 
140: // For linear flows (detail pages, wizards): Use back button
141: import { useRouter } from "wouter";
142: 
143: const router = useRouter();
144: <div>
145:   <Button variant="ghost" onClick={() => router.back()}>
146:     ← Back
147:   </Button>
148:   <ItemDetailPage />
149: </div>
150: ```
151: 
152: ### Dark mode styling without theme configuration
153: **Problem:** Using dark foreground colors without setting the theme, making text invisible on default light backgrounds.
154: 
155: **Solution:** Set `defaultTheme="dark"` in App.tsx, then update CSS variables in `index.css`:
156: ```tsx
157: // App.tsx: Set the default theme first
158: <ThemeProvider defaultTheme="dark">  {/* Applies .dark class to root */}
159:   <div className="text-foreground bg-background">
160:     Content  {/* Now uses dark theme CSS variables */}
161:   </div>
162: </ThemeProvider>
163: ```
164: 
165: ```css
166: /* index.css: Adjust color palette for dark theme */
167: .dark {
168:   --background: oklch(0.145 0 0);  /* Dark background */
169:   --foreground: oklch(0.985 0 0);  /* Light text */
170:   /* ... other variables ... */
171: }
172: ```

  1: import * as React from "react";
  2: import useEmblaCarousel, {
  3:   type UseEmblaCarouselType,
  4: } from "embla-carousel-react";
  5: import { ArrowLeft, ArrowRight } from "lucide-react";
  6: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  7: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  8: type CarouselApi = UseEmblaCarouselType[1];
  9: type UseCarouselParameters = Parameters<typeof useEmblaCarousel>;
 10: type CarouselOptions = UseCarouselParameters[0];
 11: type CarouselPlugin = UseCarouselParameters[1];
 12: type CarouselProps = {
 13:   opts?: CarouselOptions;
 14:   plugins?: CarouselPlugin;
 15:   orientation?: "horizontal" | "vertical";
 16:   setApi?: (api: CarouselApi) => void;
 17: };
 18: type CarouselContextProps = {
 19:   carouselRef: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[0];
 20:   api: ReturnType<typeof useEmblaCarousel>[1];
 21:   scrollPrev: () => void;
 22:   scrollNext: () => void;
 23:   canScrollPrev: boolean;
 24:   canScrollNext: boolean;
 25: } & CarouselProps;
 26: const CarouselContext = React.createContext<CarouselContextProps | null>(null);
 27: function useCarousel() {
 28:   const context = React.useContext(CarouselContext);
 29:   if (!context) {
 30:     throw new Error("useCarousel must be used within a <Carousel />");
 31:   }
 32:   return context;
 33: }
 34: function Carousel({
 35:   orientation = "horizontal",
 36:   opts,
 37:   setApi,
 38:   plugins,
 39:   className,
 40:   children,
 41:   ...props
 42: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & CarouselProps) {
 43:   const [carouselRef, api] = useEmblaCarousel(
 44:     {
 45:       ...opts,
 46:       axis: orientation === "horizontal" ? "x" : "y",
 47:     },
 48:     plugins
 49:   );
 50:   const [canScrollPrev, setCanScrollPrev] = React.useState(false);
 51:   const [canScrollNext, setCanScrollNext] = React.useState(false);
 52:   const onSelect = React.useCallback((api: CarouselApi) => {
 53:     if (!api) return;
 54:     setCanScrollPrev(api.canScrollPrev());
 55:     setCanScrollNext(api.canScrollNext());
 56:   }, []);
 57:   const scrollPrev = React.useCallback(() => {
 58:     api?.scrollPrev();
 59:   }, [api]);
 60:   const scrollNext = React.useCallback(() => {
 61:     api?.scrollNext();
 62:   }, [api]);
 63:   const handleKeyDown = React.useCallback(
 64:     (event: React.KeyboardEvent<HTMLDivElement>) => {
 65:       if (event.key === "ArrowLeft") {
 66:         event.preventDefault();
 67:         scrollPrev();
 68:       } else if (event.key === "ArrowRight") {
 69:         event.preventDefault();
 70:         scrollNext();
 71:       }
 72:     },
 73:     [scrollPrev, scrollNext]
 74:   );
 75:   React.useEffect(() => {
 76:     if (!api || !setApi) return;
 77:     setApi(api);
 78:   }, [api, setApi]);
 79:   React.useEffect(() => {
 80:     if (!api) return;
 81:     onSelect(api);
 82:     api.on("reInit", onSelect);
 83:     api.on("select", onSelect);
 84:     return () => {
 85:       api?.off("select", onSelect);
 86:     };
 87:   }, [api, onSelect]);
 88:   return (
 89:     <CarouselContext.Provider
 90:       value={{
 91:         carouselRef,
 92:         api: api,
 93:         opts,
 94:         orientation:
 95:           orientation || (opts?.axis === "y" ? "vertical" : "horizontal"),
 96:         scrollPrev,
 97:         scrollNext,
 98:         canScrollPrev,
 99:         canScrollNext,
100:       }}
101:     >
102:       <div
103:         onKeyDownCapture={handleKeyDown}
104:         className={cn("relative", className)}
105:         role="region"
106:         aria-roledescription="carousel"
107:         data-slot="carousel"
108:         {...props}
109:       >
110:         {children}
111:       </div>
112:     </CarouselContext.Provider>
113:   );
114: }
115: function CarouselContent({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
116:   const { carouselRef, orientation } = useCarousel();
117:   return (
118:     <div
119:       ref={carouselRef}
120:       className="overflow-hidden"
121:       data-slot="carousel-content"
122:     >
123:       <div
124:         className={cn(
125:           "flex",
126:           orientation === "horizontal" ? "-ml-4" : "-mt-4 flex-col",
127:           className
128:         )}
129:         {...props}
130:       />
131:     </div>
132:   );
133: }
134: function CarouselItem({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"div">) {
135:   const { orientation } = useCarousel();
136:   return (
137:     <div
138:       role="group"
139:       aria-roledescription="slide"
140:       data-slot="carousel-item"
141:       className={cn(
142:         "min-w-0 shrink-0 grow-0 basis-full",
143:         orientation === "horizontal" ? "pl-4" : "pt-4",
144:         className
145:       )}
146:       {...props}
147:     />
148:   );
149: }
150: function CarouselPrevious({
151:   className,
152:   variant = "outline",
153:   size = "icon",
154:   ...props
155: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Button>) {
156:   const { orientation, scrollPrev, canScrollPrev } = useCarousel();
157:   return (
158:     <Button
159:       data-slot="carousel-previous"
160:       variant={variant}
161:       size={size}
162:       className={cn(
163:         "absolute size-8 rounded-full",
164:         orientation === "horizontal"
165:           ? "top-1/2 -left-12 -translate-y-1/2"
166:           : "-top-12 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 rotate-90",
167:         className
168:       )}
169:       disabled={!canScrollPrev}
170:       onClick={scrollPrev}
171:       {...props}
172:     >
173:       <ArrowLeft />
174:       <span className="sr-only">Previous slide</span>
175:     </Button>
176:   );
177: }
178: function CarouselNext({
179:   className,
180:   variant = "outline",
181:   size = "icon",
182:   ...props
183: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Button>) {
184:   const { orientation, scrollNext, canScrollNext } = useCarousel();
185:   return (
186:     <Button
187:       data-slot="carousel-next"
188:       variant={variant}
189:       size={size}
190:       className={cn(
191:         "absolute size-8 rounded-full",
192:         orientation === "horizontal"
193:           ? "top-1/2 -right-12 -translate-y-1/2"
194:           : "-bottom-12 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 rotate-90",
195:         className
196:       )}
197:       disabled={!canScrollNext}
198:       onClick={scrollNext}
199:       {...props}
200:     >
201:       <ArrowRight />
202:       <span className="sr-only">Next slide</span>
203:     </Button>
204:   );
205: }

 58: const ChartStyle = ({ id, config }: { id: string; config: ChartConfig }) => {
 59:   const colorConfig = Object.entries(config).filter(
 60:     ([, config]) => config.theme || config.color
 61:   );
 62:   if (!colorConfig.length) {
 63:     return null;
 64:   }
 65:   return (
 66:     <style
 67:       dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{

 74:     const color =
 75:       itemConfig.theme?.[theme as keyof typeof itemConfig.theme] ||
 76:       itemConfig.color;

 78:   })
 79:   .join("\n")}
 80: }
 81: `
 82:           )

 88: const ChartTooltip = RechartsPrimitive.Tooltip;
 89: function ChartTooltipContent({
 90:   active,
 91:   payload,
 92:   className,
 93:   indicator = "dot",
 94:   hideLabel = false,
 95:   hideIndicator = false,
 96:   label,
 97:   labelFormatter,
 98:   labelClassName,
 99:   formatter,
100:   color,
101:   nameKey,
102:   labelKey,
103: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof RechartsPrimitive.Tooltip> &
104:   React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
105:     hideLabel?: boolean;
106:     hideIndicator?: boolean;
107:     indicator?: "line" | "dot" | "dashed";
108:     nameKey?: string;
109:     labelKey?: string;
110:   }) {
111:   const { config } = useChart();
112:   const tooltipLabel = React.useMemo(() => {
113:     if (hideLabel || !payload?.length) {
114:       return null;
115:     }
116:     const [item] = payload;
117:     const key = `${labelKey || item?.dataKey || item?.name || "value"}`;
118:     const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);
119:     const value =
120:       !labelKey && typeof label === "string"
121:         ? config[label as keyof typeof config]?.label || label
122:         : itemConfig?.label;
123:     if (labelFormatter) {
124:       return (
125:         <div className={cn("font-medium", labelClassName)}>
126:           {labelFormatter(value, payload)}
127:         </div>
128:       );
129:     }
130:     if (!value) {
131:       return null;
132:     }
133:     return <div className={cn("font-medium", labelClassName)}>{value}</div>;
134:   }, [
135:     label,
136:     labelFormatter,
137:     payload,
138:     hideLabel,
139:     labelClassName,
140:     config,
141:     labelKey,
142:   ]);
143:   if (!active || !payload?.length) {
144:     return null;
145:   }
146:   const nestLabel = payload.length === 1 && indicator !== "dot";
147:   return (
148:     <div
149:       className={cn(
150:         "border-border/50 bg-background grid min-w-[8rem] items-start gap-1.5 rounded-lg border px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs shadow-xl",
151:         className
152:       )}
153:     >
154:       {!nestLabel ? tooltipLabel : null}
155:       <div className="grid gap-1.5">
156:         {payload
157:           .filter(item => item.type !== "none")
158:           .map((item, index) => {
159:             const key = `${nameKey || item.name || item.dataKey || "value"}`;
160:             const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);
161:             const indicatorColor = color || item.payload.fill || item.color;
162:             return (
163:               <div
164:                 key={item.dataKey}
165:                 className={cn(
166:                   "[&>svg]:text-muted-foreground flex w-full flex-wrap items-stretch gap-2 [&>svg]:h-2.5 [&>svg]:w-2.5",
167:                   indicator === "dot" && "items-center"
168:                 )}
169:               >
170:                 {formatter && item?.value !== undefined && item.name ? (
171:                   formatter(item.value, item.name, item, index, item.payload)
172:                 ) : (
173:                   <>
174:                     {itemConfig?.icon ? (
175:                       <itemConfig.icon />
176:                     ) : (
177:                       !hideIndicator && (
178:                         <div
179:                           className={cn(
180:                             "shrink-0 rounded-[2px] border-(--color-border) bg-(--color-bg)",
181:                             {
182:                               "h-2.5 w-2.5": indicator === "dot",
183:                               "w-1": indicator === "line",
184:                               "w-0 border-[1.5px] border-dashed bg-transparent":
185:                                 indicator === "dashed",
186:                               "my-0.5": nestLabel && indicator === "dashed",
187:                             }
188:                           )}
189:                           style={
190:                             {
191:                               "--color-bg": indicatorColor,
192:                               "--color-border": indicatorColor,
193:                             } as React.CSSProperties
194:                           }
195:                         />
196:                       )
197:                     )}
198:                     <div
199:                       className={cn(
200:                         "flex flex-1 justify-between leading-none",
201:                         nestLabel ? "items-end" : "items-center"
202:                       )}
203:                     >
204:                       <div className="grid gap-1.5">
205:                         {nestLabel ? tooltipLabel : null}
206:                         <span className="text-muted-foreground">
207:                           {itemConfig?.label || item.name}
208:                         </span>
209:                       </div>
210:                       {item.value && (
211:                         <span className="text-foreground font-mono font-medium tabular-nums">
212:                           {item.value.toLocaleString()}
213:                         </span>
214:                       )}
215:                     </div>
216:                   </>
217:                 )}
218:               </div>
219:             );
220:           })}
221:       </div>
222:     </div>
223:   );

225: const ChartLegend = RechartsPrimitive.Legend;
226: function ChartLegendContent({
227:   className,
228:   hideIcon = false,
229:   payload,
230:   verticalAlign = "bottom",
231:   nameKey,
232: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> &
233:   Pick<RechartsPrimitive.LegendProps, "payload" | "verticalAlign"> & {
234:     hideIcon?: boolean;
235:     nameKey?: string;
236:   }) {
237:   const { config } = useChart();
238:   if (!payload?.length) {
239:     return null;
240:   }
241:   return (
242:     <div
243:       className={cn(
244:         "flex items-center justify-center gap-4",
245:         verticalAlign === "top" ? "pb-3" : "pt-3",
246:         className
247:       )}
248:     >
249:       {payload
250:         .filter(item => item.type !== "none")
251:         .map(item => {
252:           const key = `${nameKey || item.dataKey || "value"}`;
253:           const itemConfig = getPayloadConfigFromPayload(config, item, key);
254:           return (
255:             <div
256:               key={item.value}
257:               className={cn(
258:                 "[&>svg]:text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1.5 [&>svg]:h-3 [&>svg]:w-3"
259:               )}
260:             >
261:               {itemConfig?.icon && !hideIcon ? (
262:                 <itemConfig.icon />
263:               ) : (
264:                 <div
265:                   className="h-2 w-2 shrink-0 rounded-[2px]"
266:                   style={{
267:                     backgroundColor: item.color,
268:                   }}
269:                 />
270:               )}
271:               {itemConfig?.label}
272:             </div>
273:           );
274:         })}
275:     </div>
276:   );
277: }
278: function getPayloadConfigFromPayload(
279:   config: ChartConfig,
280:   payload: unknown,
281:   key: string
282: ) {
283:   if (typeof payload !== "object" || payload === null) {
284:     return undefined;
285:   }
286:   const payloadPayload =
287:     "payload" in payload &&
288:     typeof payload.payload === "object" &&
289:     payload.payload !== null
290:       ? payload.payload
291:       : undefined;
292:   let configLabelKey: string = key;
293:   if (
294:     key in payload &&
295:     typeof payload[key as keyof typeof payload] === "string"
296:   ) {
297:     configLabelKey = payload[key as keyof typeof payload] as string;
298:   } else if (
299:     payloadPayload &&
300:     key in payloadPayload &&
301:     typeof payloadPayload[key as keyof typeof payloadPayload] === "string"
302:   ) {
303:     configLabelKey = payloadPayload[
304:       key as keyof typeof payloadPayload
305:     ] as string;
306:   }
307:   return configLabelKey in config
308:     ? config[configLabelKey]
309:     : config[key as keyof typeof config];
310: }

  1: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
  2: import * as DialogPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-dialog";
  3: import { XIcon } from "lucide-react";
  4: import * as React from "react";
  5: const DialogCompositionContext = React.createContext<{
  6:   isComposing: () => boolean;
  7:   setComposing: (composing: boolean) => void;
  8:   justEndedComposing: () => boolean;
  9:   markCompositionEnd: () => void;
 10: }>({
 11:   isComposing: () => false,
 12:   setComposing: () => {},
 13:   justEndedComposing: () => false,
 14:   markCompositionEnd: () => {},
 15: });
 16: export const useDialogComposition = () =>
 17:   React.useContext(DialogCompositionContext);
 18: function Dialog({
 19:   ...props
 20: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Root>) {
 21:   const composingRef = React.useRef(false);
 22:   const justEndedRef = React.useRef(false);
 23:   const endTimerRef = React.useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);
 24:   const contextValue = React.useMemo(
 25:     () => ({
 26:       isComposing: () => composingRef.current,
 27:       setComposing: (composing: boolean) => {
 28:         composingRef.current = composing;
 29:       },
 30:       justEndedComposing: () => justEndedRef.current,
 31:       markCompositionEnd: () => {
 32:         justEndedRef.current = true;
 33:         if (endTimerRef.current) {
 34:           clearTimeout(endTimerRef.current);
 35:         }
 36:         endTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
 37:           justEndedRef.current = false;
 38:         }, 150);
 39:       },
 40:     }),
 41:     []
 42:   );
 43:   return (
 44:     <DialogCompositionContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
 45:       <DialogPrimitive.Root data-slot="dialog" {...props} />
 46:     </DialogCompositionContext.Provider>
 47:   );
 48: }
 49: function DialogTrigger({
 50:   ...props
 51: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Trigger>) {
 52:   return <DialogPrimitive.Trigger data-slot="dialog-trigger" {...props} />;
 53: }
 54: function DialogPortal({
 55:   ...props
 56: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Portal>) {
 57:   return <DialogPrimitive.Portal data-slot="dialog-portal" {...props} />;
 58: }
 59: function DialogClose({
 60:   ...props
 61: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Close>) {
 62:   return <DialogPrimitive.Close data-slot="dialog-close" {...props} />;
 63: }
 64: function DialogOverlay({
 65:   className,
 66:   ...props
 67: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Overlay>) {
 68:   return (
 69:     <DialogPrimitive.Overlay
 70:       data-slot="dialog-overlay"
 71:       className={cn(
 72:         "data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/50",
 73:         className
 74:       )}
 75:       {...props}
 76:     />
 77:   );
 78: }
 79: DialogOverlay.displayName = "DialogOverlay";
 80: function DialogContent({
 81:   className,
 82:   children,
 83:   showCloseButton = true,
 84:   onEscapeKeyDown,
 85:   ...props
 86: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof DialogPrimitive.Content> & {
 87:   showCloseButton?: boolean;
 88: }) {
 89:   const { isComposing } = useDialogComposition();
 90:   const handleEscapeKeyDown = React.useCallback(
 91:     (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
 92:       const isCurrentlyComposing = (e as any).isComposing || isComposing();
 93:       if (isCurrentlyComposing) {
 94:         e.preventDefault();
 95:         return;
 96:       }
 97:       onEscapeKeyDown?.(e);
 98:     },
 99:     [isComposing, onEscapeKeyDown]
100:   );
101:   return (
102:     <DialogPortal data-slot="dialog-portal">
103:       <DialogOverlay />
104:       <DialogPrimitive.Content
105:         data-slot="dialog-content"
106:         className={cn(
107:           "bg-background data-[state=open]:animate-in data-[state=closed]:animate-out data-[state=closed]:fade-out-0 data-[state=open]:fade-in-0 data-[state=closed]:zoom-out-95 data-[state=open]:zoom-in-95 fixed top-[50%] left-[50%] z-50 grid w-full max-w-[calc(100%-2rem)] translate-x-[-50%] translate-y-[-50%] gap-4 rounded-lg border p-6 shadow-lg duration-200 sm:max-w-lg",
108:           className
109:         )}
110:         onEscapeKeyDown={handleEscapeKeyDown}
111:         {...props}
112:       >
113:         {children}
114:         {showCloseButton && (
115:           <DialogPrimitive.Close
116:             data-slot="dialog-close"
117:             className="ring-offset-background focus:ring-ring data-[state=open]:bg-accent data-[state=open]:text-muted-foreground absolute top-4 right-4 rounded-xs opacity-70 transition-opacity hover:opacity-100 focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 focus:outline-hidden disabled:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:pointer-events-none [&_svg]:shrink-0 [&_svg:not([class*='size-'])]:size-4"
118:           >
119:             <XIcon />
120:             <span className="sr-only">Close</span>
121:           </DialogPrimitive.Close>
122:         )}
123:       </DialogPrimitive.Content>
124:     </DialogPortal>
125:   );
126: }

128:   return (
129:     <div

156:         className

161:       {children && (
162:         <span
163:           className="bg-background text-muted-foreground relative mx-auto block w-fit px-2"

172: function FieldError({
173:   className,
174:   children,
175:   errors,
176:   ...props
177: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
178:   errors?: Array<{ message?: string } | undefined>;
179: }) {
180:   const content = useMemo(() => {
181:     if (children) {
182:       return children;
183:     }
184:     if (!errors) {
185:       return null;
186:     }
187:     if (errors?.length === 1 && errors[0]?.message) {
188:       return errors[0].message;
189:     }
190:     return (
191:       <ul className="ml-4 flex list-disc flex-col gap-1">
192:         {errors.map(
193:           (error, index) =>
194:             error?.message && <li key={index}>{error.message}</li>
195:         )}
196:       </ul>
197:     );
198:   }, [children, errors]);
199:   if (!content) {
200:     return null;
201:   }
202:   return (
203:     <div
204:       role="alert"
205:       data-slot="field-error"
206:       className={cn("text-destructive text-sm font-normal", className)}
207:       {...props}
208:     >
209:       {content}
210:     </div>
211:   );
212: }

  1: "use client";
  2: import * as React from "react";
  3: import * as LabelPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-label";
  4: import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot";
  5: import {
  6:   Controller,
  7:   FormProvider,
  8:   useFormContext,
  9:   useFormState,
 10:   type ControllerProps,
 11:   type FieldPath,
 12:   type FieldValues,
 13: } from "react-hook-form";
 14: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 15: import { Label } from "@/components/ui/label";
 16: const Form = FormProvider;
 17: type FormFieldContextValue<
 18:   TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
 19:   TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
 20: > = {
 21:   name: TName;
 22: };
 23: const FormFieldContext = React.createContext<FormFieldContextValue>(
 24:   {} as FormFieldContextValue
 25: );
 26: const FormField = <
 27:   TFieldValues extends FieldValues = FieldValues,
 28:   TName extends FieldPath<TFieldValues> = FieldPath<TFieldValues>,
 29: >({
 30:   ...props
 31: }: ControllerProps<TFieldValues, TName>) => {
 32:   return (
 33:     <FormFieldContext.Provider value={{ name: props.name }}>
 34:       <Controller {...props} />
 35:     </FormFieldContext.Provider>
 36:   );
 37: };
 38: const useFormField = () => {
 39:   const fieldContext = React.useContext(FormFieldContext);
 40:   const itemContext = React.useContext(FormItemContext);
 41:   const { getFieldState } = useFormContext();
 42:   const formState = useFormState({ name: fieldContext.name });
 43:   const fieldState = getFieldState(fieldContext.name, formState);
 44:   if (!fieldContext) {
 45:     throw new Error("useFormField should be used within <FormField>");
 46:   }
 47:   const { id } = itemContext;
 48:   return {
 49:     id,
 50:     name: fieldContext.name,
 51:     formItemId: `${id}-form-item`,
 52:     formDescriptionId: `${id}-form-item-description`,
 53:     formMessageId: `${id}-form-item-message`,
 54:     ...fieldState,
 55:   };
 56: };

 58:   id: string;
 59: };
 60: const FormItemContext = React.createContext<FormItemContextValue>(
 61:   {} as FormItemContextValue
 62: );

 65:   return (
 66:     <FormItemContext.Provider value={{ id }}>
 67:       <div
 68:         data-slot="form-item"

 74: }
 75: function FormLabel({
 76:   className,
 77:   ...props
 78: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof LabelPrimitive.Root>) {
 79:   const { error, formItemId } = useFormField();
 80:   return (
 81:     <Label
 82:       data-slot="form-label"
 83:       data-error={!!error}
 84:       className={cn("data-[error=true]:text-destructive", className)}
 85:       htmlFor={formItemId}
 86:       {...props}
 87:     />
 88:   );
 89: }
 90: function FormControl({ ...props }: React.ComponentProps<typeof Slot>) {
 91:   const { error, formItemId, formDescriptionId, formMessageId } =
 92:     useFormField();
 93:   return (
 94:     <Slot
 95:       data-slot="form-control"
 96:       id={formItemId}
 97:       aria-describedby={
 98:         !error
 99:           ? `${formDescriptionId}`
100:           : `${formDescriptionId} ${formMessageId}`
101:       }
102:       aria-invalid={!!error}
103:       {...props}
104:     />
105:   );
106: }
107: function FormDescription({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
108:   const { formDescriptionId } = useFormField();
109:   return (
110:     <p
111:       data-slot="form-description"
112:       id={formDescriptionId}
113:       className={cn("text-muted-foreground text-sm", className)}
114:       {...props}
115:     />
116:   );
117: }
118: function FormMessage({ className, ...props }: React.ComponentProps<"p">) {
119:   const { error, formMessageId } = useFormField();
120:   const body = error ? String(error?.message ?? "") : props.children;
121:   if (!body) {
122:     return null;
123:   }
124:   return (
125:     <p
126:       data-slot="form-message"
127:       id={formMessageId}
128:       className={cn("text-destructive text-sm", className)}
129:       {...props}
130:     >
131:       {body}
132:     </p>
133:   );
134: }

 1: import { useDialogComposition } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
 2: import { useComposition } from "@/hooks/useComposition";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: import * as React from "react";
 5: function Input({
 6:   className,
 7:   type,
 8:   onKeyDown,
 9:   onCompositionStart,
10:   onCompositionEnd,
11:   ...props
12: }: React.ComponentProps<"input">) {
13:   const dialogComposition = useDialogComposition();
14:   const {
15:     onCompositionStart: handleCompositionStart,
16:     onCompositionEnd: handleCompositionEnd,
17:     onKeyDown: handleKeyDown,
18:   } = useComposition<HTMLInputElement>({
19:     onKeyDown: (e) => {
20:       const isComposing = (e.nativeEvent as any).isComposing || dialogComposition.justEndedComposing();
21:       if (e.key === "Enter" && isComposing) {
22:         return;
23:       }
24:       onKeyDown?.(e);
25:     },
26:     onCompositionStart: e => {
27:       dialogComposition.setComposing(true);
28:       onCompositionStart?.(e);
29:     },
30:     onCompositionEnd: e => {
31:       dialogComposition.markCompositionEnd();
32:       setTimeout(() => {
33:         dialogComposition.setComposing(false);
34:       }, 100);
35:       onCompositionEnd?.(e);
36:     },
37:   });
38:   return (
39:     <input
40:       type={type}
41:       data-slot="input"
42:       className={cn(
43:         "file:text-foreground placeholder:text-muted-foreground selection:bg-primary selection:text-primary-foreground dark:bg-input/30 border-input h-9 w-full min-w-0 rounded-md border bg-transparent px-3 py-1 text-base shadow-xs transition-[color,box-shadow] outline-none file:inline-flex file:h-7 file:border-0 file:bg-transparent file:text-sm file:font-medium disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 md:text-sm",
44:         "focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 focus-visible:ring-[3px]",
45:         "aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive",
46:         className
47:       )}
48:       onCompositionStart={handleCompositionStart}
49:       onCompositionEnd={handleCompositionEnd}
50:       onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
51:       {...props}
52:     />
53:   );
54: }
55: export { Input };

File: manus-archive-master/templates/event-template/client/src/components/ui/sidebar.tsx
================
  1: "use client";
  2: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  3: import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
  4: import { Separator } from "@/components/ui/separator";
  5: import {
  6:   Sheet,
  7:   SheetContent,
  8:   SheetDescription,
  9:   SheetHeader,
 10:   SheetTitle,
 11: } from "@/components/ui/sheet";
 12: import { Skeleton } from "@/components/ui/skeleton";
 13: import {
 14:   Tooltip,
 15:   TooltipContent,
 16:   TooltipProvider,
 17:   TooltipTrigger,
 18: } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
 19: import { useIsMobile } from "@/hooks/useMobile";
 20: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 21: import { Slot } from "@radix-ui/react-slot";
 22: import { cva, VariantProps } from "class-variance-authority";
 23: import { PanelLeftIcon } from "lucide-react";
 24: import * as React from "react";
 25: const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME = "sidebar_state";
 26: const SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE = 60 * 60 * 24 * 7;
 27: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH = "16rem";
 28: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE = "18rem";
 29: const SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON = "3rem";
 30: const SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT = "b";
 31: type SidebarContextProps = {
 32:   state: "expanded" | "collapsed";
 33:   open: boolean;
 34:   setOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
 35:   openMobile: boolean;
 36:   setOpenMobile: (open: boolean) => void;
 37:   isMobile: boolean;
 38:   toggleSidebar: () => void;
 39: };
 40: const SidebarContext = React.createContext<SidebarContextProps | null>(null);
 41: function useSidebar() {
 42:   const context = React.useContext(SidebarContext);
 43:   if (!context) {
 44:     throw new Error("useSidebar must be used within a SidebarProvider.");
 45:   }
 46:   return context;
 47: }
 48: function SidebarProvider({
 49:   defaultOpen = true,
 50:   open: openProp,
 51:   onOpenChange: setOpenProp,
 52:   className,
 53:   style,
 54:   children,
 55:   ...props
 56: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
 57:   defaultOpen?: boolean;
 58:   open?: boolean;
 59:   onOpenChange?: (open: boolean) => void;
 60: }) {
 61:   const isMobile = useIsMobile();
 62:   const [openMobile, setOpenMobile] = React.useState(false);
 63:   const [_open, _setOpen] = React.useState(defaultOpen);
 64:   const open = openProp ?? _open;
 65:   const setOpen = React.useCallback(
 66:     (value: boolean | ((value: boolean) => boolean)) => {
 67:       const openState = typeof value === "function" ? value(open) : value;
 68:       if (setOpenProp) {
 69:         setOpenProp(openState);
 70:       } else {
 71:         _setOpen(openState);
 72:       }
 73:       document.cookie = `${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_NAME}=${openState}; path=/; max-age=${SIDEBAR_COOKIE_MAX_AGE}`;
 74:     },
 75:     [setOpenProp, open]
 76:   );
 77:   const toggleSidebar = React.useCallback(() => {
 78:     return isMobile ? setOpenMobile(open => !open) : setOpen(open => !open);
 79:   }, [isMobile, setOpen, setOpenMobile]);
 80:   React.useEffect(() => {
 81:     const handleKeyDown = (event: KeyboardEvent) => {
 82:       if (
 83:         event.key === SIDEBAR_KEYBOARD_SHORTCUT &&
 84:         (event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey)
 85:       ) {
 86:         event.preventDefault();
 87:         toggleSidebar();
 88:       }
 89:     };
 90:     window.addEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
 91:     return () => window.removeEventListener("keydown", handleKeyDown);
 92:   }, [toggleSidebar]);
 93:   const state = open ? "expanded" : "collapsed";
 94:   const contextValue = React.useMemo<SidebarContextProps>(
 95:     () => ({
 96:       state,
 97:       open,
 98:       setOpen,
 99:       isMobile,
100:       openMobile,
101:       setOpenMobile,
102:       toggleSidebar,
103:     }),
104:     [state, open, setOpen, isMobile, openMobile, setOpenMobile, toggleSidebar]
105:   );
106:   return (
107:     <SidebarContext.Provider value={contextValue}>
108:       <TooltipProvider delayDuration={0}>
109:         <div
110:           data-slot="sidebar-wrapper"
111:           style={
112:             {
113:               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH,
114:               "--sidebar-width-icon": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_ICON,
115:               ...style,
116:             } as React.CSSProperties
117:           }
118:           className={cn(
119:             "group/sidebar-wrapper has-data-[variant=inset]:bg-sidebar flex min-h-svh w-full",
120:             className
121:           )}
122:           {...props}
123:         >
124:           {children}
125:         </div>
126:       </TooltipProvider>
127:     </SidebarContext.Provider>
128:   );
129: }
130: function Sidebar({
131:   side = "left",
132:   variant = "sidebar",
133:   collapsible = "offcanvas",
134:   disableTransition = false,
135:   className,
136:   children,
137:   ...props
138: }: React.ComponentProps<"div"> & {
139:   side?: "left" | "right";
140:   variant?: "sidebar" | "floating" | "inset";
141:   collapsible?: "offcanvas" | "icon" | "none";
142:   disableTransition?: boolean;
143: }) {
144:   const { isMobile, state, openMobile, setOpenMobile } = useSidebar();
145:   if (collapsible === "none") {
146:     return (
147:       <div
148:         data-slot="sidebar"
149:         className={cn(
150:           "bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground flex h-full w-(--sidebar-width) flex-col",
151:           className
152:         )}
153:         {...props}
154:       >
155:         {children}
156:       </div>
157:     );
158:   }
159:   if (isMobile) {
160:     return (
161:       <Sheet open={openMobile} onOpenChange={setOpenMobile} {...props}>
162:         <SheetContent
163:           data-sidebar="sidebar"
164:           data-slot="sidebar"
165:           data-mobile="true"
166:           className="bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground w-(--sidebar-width) p-0 [&>button]:hidden"
167:           style={
168:             {
169:               "--sidebar-width": SIDEBAR_WIDTH_MOBILE,
170:             } as React.CSSProperties
171:           }
172:           side={side}
173:         >
174:           <SheetHeader className="sr-only">
175:             <SheetTitle>Sidebar</SheetTitle>
176:             <SheetDescription>Displays the mobile sidebar.</SheetDescription>
177:           </SheetHeader>
178:           <div className="flex h-full w-full flex-col">{children}</div>
179:         </SheetContent>
180:       </Sheet>
181:     );
182:   }
183:   return (
184:     <div
185:       className="group peer text-sidebar-foreground hidden md:block"
186:       data-state={state}
187:       data-collapsible={state === "collapsed" ? collapsible : ""}
188:       data-variant={variant}
189:       data-side={side}
190:       data-slot="sidebar"
191:     >
192:       {}
193:       <div
194:         data-slot="sidebar-gap"
195:         className={cn(
196:           "relative w-(--sidebar-width) bg-transparent",
197:           disableTransition
198:             ? "transition-none"
199:             : "transition-[width] duration-200 ease-linear",
200:           "group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:w-0",
201:           "group-data-[side=right]:rotate-180",
202:           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
203:             ? "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+(--spacing(4)))]"
204:             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-(--sidebar-width-icon)"
205:         )}
206:       />
207:       <div
208:         data-slot="sidebar-container"
209:         className={cn(
210:           "fixed inset-y-0 z-10 hidden h-svh w-(--sidebar-width) md:flex",
211:           disableTransition
212:             ? "transition-none"
213:             : "transition-[left,right,width] duration-200 ease-linear",
214:           side === "left"
215:             ? "left-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:left-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]"
216:             : "right-0 group-data-[collapsible=offcanvas]:right-[calc(var(--sidebar-width)*-1)]",
217:           variant === "floating" || variant === "inset"
218:             ? "p-2 group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-[calc(var(--sidebar-width-icon)+(--spacing(4))+2px)]"
219:             : "group-data-[collapsible=icon]:w-(--sidebar-width-icon) group-data-[side=left]:border-r group-data-[side=right]:border-l",
220:           className
221:         )}
222:         {...props}
223:       >
224:         <div
225:           data-sidebar="sidebar"
226:           data-slot="sidebar-inner"
227:           className="bg-sidebar group-data-[variant=floating]:border-sidebar-border flex h-full w-full flex-col group-data-[variant=floating]:rounded-lg group-data-[variant=floating]:border group-data-[variant=floating]:shadow-sm"
228:         >
229:           {children}
230:         </div>
231:       </div>
232:     </div>
233:   );
234: }

 1: import * as React from "react";
 2: import * as SliderPrimitive from "@radix-ui/react-slider";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: function Slider({
 5:   className,
 6:   defaultValue,
 7:   value,
 8:   min = 0,
 9:   max = 100,
10:   ...props
11: }: React.ComponentProps<typeof SliderPrimitive.Root>) {
12:   const _values = React.useMemo(
13:     () =>
14:       Array.isArray(value)
15:         ? value
16:         : Array.isArray(defaultValue)
17:           ? defaultValue
18:           : [min, max],
19:     [value, defaultValue, min, max]
20:   );
21:   return (
22:     <SliderPrimitive.Root
23:       data-slot="slider"
24:       defaultValue={defaultValue}
25:       value={value}
26:       min={min}
27:       max={max}

File: manus-archive-master/templates/event-template/client/src/components/ui/textarea.tsx

 1: import { useDialogComposition } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
 2: import { useComposition } from "@/hooks/useComposition";
 3: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 4: import * as React from "react";
 5: function Textarea({
 6:   className,
 7:   onKeyDown,
 8:   onCompositionStart,
 9:   onCompositionEnd,
10:   ...props
11: }: React.ComponentProps<"textarea">) {
12:   const dialogComposition = useDialogComposition();
13:   const {
14:     onCompositionStart: handleCompositionStart,
15:     onCompositionEnd: handleCompositionEnd,
16:     onKeyDown: handleKeyDown,
17:   } = useComposition<HTMLTextAreaElement>({
18:     onKeyDown: (e) => {
19:       const isComposing = (e.nativeEvent as any).isComposing || dialogComposition.justEndedComposing();
20:       if (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey && isComposing) {
21:         return;
22:       }
23:       onKeyDown?.(e);
24:     },
25:     onCompositionStart: e => {
26:       dialogComposition.setComposing(true);
27:       onCompositionStart?.(e);
28:     },
29:     onCompositionEnd: e => {
30:       dialogComposition.markCompositionEnd();
31:       setTimeout(() => {
32:         dialogComposition.setComposing(false);
33:       }, 100);
34:       onCompositionEnd?.(e);
35:     },
36:   });
37:   return (
38:     <textarea
39:       data-slot="textarea"
40:       className={cn(
41:         "border-input placeholder:text-muted-foreground focus-visible:border-ring focus-visible:ring-ring/50 aria-invalid:ring-destructive/20 dark:aria-invalid:ring-destructive/40 aria-invalid:border-destructive dark:bg-input/30 flex field-sizing-content min-h-16 w-full rounded-md border bg-transparent px-3 py-2 text-base shadow-xs transition-[color,box-shadow] outline-none focus-visible:ring-[3px] disabled:cursor-not-allowed disabled:opacity-50 md:text-sm",
42:         className
43:       )}
44:       onCompositionStart={handleCompositionStart}
45:       onCompositionEnd={handleCompositionEnd}
46:       onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
47:       {...props}
48:     />
49:   );
50: }
51: export { Textarea };

File: manus-archive-master/templates/event-template/client/src/components/ErrorBoundary.tsx
================
 1: import { cn } from "@/lib/utils";
 2: import { AlertTriangle, RotateCcw } from "lucide-react";
 3: import { Component, ReactNode } from "react";
 4: interface Props {
 5:   children: ReactNode;
 6: }
 7: interface State {
 8:   hasError: boolean;
 9:   error: Error | null;
10: }
11: class ErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {
12:   constructor(props: Props) {
13:     super(props);
14:     this.state = { hasError: false, error: null };
15:   }
16:   static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): State {
17:     return { hasError: true, error };
18:   }
19:   render() {
20:     if (this.state.hasError) {
21:       return (
22:         <div className="flex items-center justify-center min-h-screen p-8 bg-background">
23:           <div className="flex flex-col items-center w-full max-w-2xl p-8">
24:             <AlertTriangle
25:               size={48}
26:               className="text-destructive mb-6 flex-shrink-0"
27:             />
28:             <h2 className="text-xl mb-4">An unexpected error occurred.</h2>
29:             <div className="p-4 w-full rounded bg-muted overflow-auto mb-6">
30:               <pre className="text-sm text-muted-foreground whitespace-break-spaces">
31:                 {this.state.error?.stack}
32:               </pre>
33:             </div>
34:             <button
35:               onClick={() => window.location.reload()}
36:               className={cn(
37:                 "flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg",
38:                 "bg-primary text-primary-foreground",
39:                 "hover:opacity-90 cursor-pointer"
40:               )}
41:             >
42:               <RotateCcw size={16} />
43:               Reload Page
44:             </button>
45:           </div>
46:         </div>
47:       );
48:     }
49:     return this.props.children;
50:   }
51: }
52: export default ErrorBoundary;

  1: import EventCard from "./EventCard";
  2: import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from "@/components/ui/tabs";
  3: interface Event {
  4:   title: string;
  5:   description: string;
  6:   time: string;
  7:   location: string;
  8:   type: string;
  9:   featured?: boolean;
 10: }
 11: interface DayData {
 12:   date: string;
 13:   events: Event[];

File: manus-archive-master/templates/event-template/client/src/components/LeftNavigation.tsx
================
  1: import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from "react";
  2: import { Heart } from "lucide-react";
  3: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
  4: interface NavItem {
  5:   name: string;
  6:   href: string;
  7: }
  8: const NavBar = () => {
  9:   const [activeSection, setActiveSection] = useState("");
 10:   const [isScrolled, setIsScrolled] = useState(false);
 11:   const [isVisible, setIsVisible] = useState(true);
 12:   const lastScrollY = useRef(0);
 13:   const navItems: NavItem[] = [
 14:     { name: "Events", href: "#events" },
 15:     { name: "Wedding Party", href: "#wedding-party" },
 16:     { name: "Location", href: "#location" },
 17:     { name: "RSVP", href: "#rsvp" },
 18:   ];
 19:   useEffect(() => {
 20:     const handleScroll = () => {
 21:       const currentScrollY = window.scrollY;
 22:       if (currentScrollY > lastScrollY.current && currentScrollY > 80) {
 23:         setIsVisible(false);
 24:       } else {
 25:         setIsVisible(true);
 26:       }
 27:       setIsScrolled(false);
 28:       const sections = navItems.map(item => item.href.replace('#', ''));
 29:       const scrollPosition = currentScrollY + 100; // Offset for header
 30:       for (let i = sections.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
 31:         const element = document.getElementById(sections[i]);
 32:         if (element && element.offsetTop <= scrollPosition) {
 33:           setActiveSection(sections[i]);
 34:           break;
 35:         }
 36:       }
 37:       // Update lastScrollY after all other state updates
 38:       lastScrollY.current = currentScrollY;
 39:     };
 40:     window.addEventListener('scroll', handleScroll);
 41:     handleScroll();
 42:     return () => window.removeEventListener('scroll', handleScroll);
 43:   }, []);
 44:   const handleNavClick = (href: string) => {
 45:     const element = document.querySelector(href);
 46:     if (element) {
 47:       element.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
 48:     }
 49:   };
 50:   return (
 51:     <header className={`fixed top-0 left-0 right-0 z-40 w-full transition-all duration-300 ease-in-out ${
 52:       isVisible ? 'translate-y-0' : '-translate-y-full'
 53:     } ${
 54:       isScrolled
 55:         ? 'bg-background/98 backdrop-blur-md border-b border-border shadow-lg'
 56:         : 'bg-background/95 backdrop-blur-sm border-b border-border'
 57:     }`}>
 58:       <div className="mx-auto px-6 max-w-full">
 59:         <div className={`flex items-center justify-between transition-all duration-300 ${
 60:           isScrolled ? 'h-14' : 'h-16'
 61:         }`}>
 62:           {}
 63:           <div className="flex items-center space-x-3">
 64:             <div className={`bg-gradient-to-r from-gold to-gold-light rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center transition-all duration-300 ${
 65:               isScrolled ? 'w-9 h-9' : 'w-10 h-10'
 66:             }`}>
 67:               <Heart className={`text-white transition-all duration-300 ${
 68:                 isScrolled ? 'w-4 h-4' : 'w-5 h-5'
 69:               }`} />
 70:             </div>
 71:             <p className={`font-medium text-muted-foreground transition-all duration-300 ${
 72:               isScrolled ? 'text-xs' : 'text-sm'
 73:             }`}>S&M</p>
 74:           </div>
 75:           {}
 76:           <nav className="hidden md:flex">
 77:             <ul className={`flex items-center transition-all duration-300 ${
 78:               isScrolled ? 'space-x-4' : 'space-x-8'
 79:             }`}>
 80:               {navItems.map((item) => {
 81:                 const sectionId = item.href.replace('#', '');
 82:                 const isActive = activeSection === sectionId;
 83:                 return (
 84:                   <li key={item.name}>
 85:                     <button
 86:                       onClick={() => handleNavClick(item.href)}
 87:                       className={`transition-all duration-300 ${
 88:                         isScrolled ? 'px-2 py-1' : 'px-3 py-2'
 89:                       } ${
 90:                         isActive
 91:                           ? 'text-gold font-medium transform scale-105'
 92:                           : 'text-muted-foreground hover:text-gold'
 93:                       }`}
 94:                     >
 95:                       <span className={`whitespace-nowrap transition-all duration-300 ${
 96:                         isScrolled ? 'text-xs' : 'text-sm'
 97:                       }`}>
 98:                         {item.name}
 99:                       </span>
100:                     </button>
101:                   </li>
102:                 );
103:               })}
104:             </ul>
105:           </nav>
106:           {}
107:           <div className="flex items-center">
108:             <Button
109:               variant="outline"
110:               size="sm"
111:               className="border-gold text-gold hover:bg-gold hover:text-white"
112:               title="RSVP Now"
113:             >
114:               RSVP
115:             </Button>
116:           </div>
117:         </div>
118:       </div>
119:     </header>
120:   );
121: };
122: export default NavBar;

 1: import { useEffect, useState } from "react";
 2: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";
 3: import { APP_LOGO, APP_TITLE } from "@/const";
 4: import {
 5:   Dialog,
 6:   DialogContent,
 7:   DialogDescription,
 8:   DialogFooter,
 9:   DialogTitle,
10: } from "@/components/ui/dialog";
11: interface ManusDialogProps {
12:   title?: string;
13:   logo?: string;
14:   open?: boolean;
15:   onLogin: () => void;
16:   onOpenChange?: (open: boolean) => void;
17:   onClose?: () => void;
18: }
19: export function ManusDialog({
20:   title = APP_TITLE,
21:   logo = APP_LOGO,
22:   open = false,
23:   onLogin,
24:   onOpenChange,
25:   onClose,
26: }: ManusDialogProps) {
27:   const [internalOpen, setInternalOpen] = useState(open);
28:   useEffect(() => {
29:     if (!onOpenChange) {
30:       setInternalOpen(open);
31:     }
32:   }, [open, onOpenChange]);
33:   const handleOpenChange = (nextOpen: boolean) => {
34:     if (onOpenChange) {
35:       onOpenChange(nextOpen);
36:     } else {
37:       setInternalOpen(nextOpen);
38:     }
39:     if (!nextOpen) {
40:       onClose?.();
41:     }
42:   };
43:   return (
44:     <Dialog
45:       open={onOpenChange ? open : internalOpen}
46:       onOpenChange={handleOpenChange}
47:     >
48:       <DialogContent className="py-5 bg-[#f8f8f7] rounded-[20px] w-[400px] shadow-[0px_4px_11px_0px_rgba(0,0,0,0.08)] border border-[rgba(0,0,0,0.08)] backdrop-blur-2xl p-0 gap-0 text-center">
49:         <div className="flex flex-col items-center gap-2 p-5 pt-12">
50:           <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-white rounded-xl border border-[rgba(0,0,0,0.08)] flex items-center justify-center">
51:             <img src={logo} alt="App icon" className="w-10 h-10 rounded-md" />
52:           </div>
53:           {}
54:           <DialogTitle className="text-xl font-semibold text-[#34322d] leading-[26px] tracking-[-0.44px]">
55:             {title}
56:           </DialogTitle>
57:           <DialogDescription className="text-sm text-[#858481] leading-5 tracking-[-0.154px]">
58:             Please login with Manus to continue
59:           </DialogDescription>
60:         </div>
61:         <DialogFooter className="px-5 py-5">
62:           {}
63:           <Button
64:             onClick={onLogin}
65:             className="w-full h-10 bg-[#1a1a19] hover:bg-[#1a1a19]/90 text-white rounded-[10px] text-sm font-medium leading-5 tracking-[-0.154px]"
66:           >
67:             Login with Manus
68:           </Button>
69:         </DialogFooter>
70:       </DialogContent>
71:     </Dialog>
72:   );
73: }

File: manus-archive-master/templates/event-template/client/src/contexts/ThemeContext.tsx
================
 1: import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from "react";
 2: type Theme = "light" | "dark";
 3: interface ThemeContextType {
 4:   theme: Theme;
 5:   toggleTheme?: () => void;
 6:   switchable: boolean;
 7: }
 8: const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextType | undefined>(undefined);
 9: interface ThemeProviderProps {
10:   children: React.ReactNode;
11:   defaultTheme?: Theme;
12:   switchable?: boolean;
13: }
14: export function ThemeProvider({
15:   children,
16:   defaultTheme = "light",
17:   switchable = false,
18: }: ThemeProviderProps) {
19:   const [theme, setTheme] = useState<Theme>(() => {
20:     if (switchable) {
21:       const stored = localStorage.getItem("theme");
22:       return (stored as Theme) || defaultTheme;
23:     }
24:     return defaultTheme;
25:   });
26:   useEffect(() => {
27:     const root = document.documentElement;
28:     if (theme === "dark") {
29:       root.classList.add("dark");
30:     } else {
31:       root.classList.remove("dark");
32:     }
33:     if (switchable) {
34:       localStorage.setItem("theme", theme);
35:     }
36:   }, [theme, switchable]);
37:   const toggleTheme = switchable
38:     ? () => {
39:         setTheme(prev => (prev === "light" ? "dark" : "light"));
40:       }
41:     : undefined;
42:   return (
43:     <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, toggleTheme, switchable }}>
44:       {children}
45:     </ThemeContext.Provider>
46:   );
47: }
48: export function useTheme() {
49:   const context = useContext(ThemeContext);
50:   if (!context) {
51:     throw new Error("useTheme must be used within ThemeProvider");
52:   }
53:   return context;
54: }

File: manus-archive-master/templates/event-template/client/src/hooks/useComposition.ts
================
 1: import { useRef } from "react";
 2: import { usePersistFn } from "./usePersistFn";
 3: export interface UseCompositionReturn<
 4:   T extends HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement,
 5: > {
 6:   onCompositionStart: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
 7:   onCompositionEnd: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
 8:   onKeyDown: React.KeyboardEventHandler<T>;
 9:   isComposing: () => boolean;
10: }
11: export interface UseCompositionOptions<
12:   T extends HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement,
13: > {
14:   onKeyDown?: React.KeyboardEventHandler<T>;
15:   onCompositionStart?: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
16:   onCompositionEnd?: React.CompositionEventHandler<T>;
17: }
18: type TimerResponse = ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>;
19: export function useComposition<
20:   T extends HTMLInputElement | HTMLTextAreaElement = HTMLInputElement,
21: >(options: UseCompositionOptions<T> = {}): UseCompositionReturn<T> {
22:   const {
23:     onKeyDown: originalOnKeyDown,
24:     onCompositionStart: originalOnCompositionStart,
25:     onCompositionEnd: originalOnCompositionEnd,
26:   } = options;
27:   const c = useRef(false);
28:   const timer = useRef<TimerResponse | null>(null);
29:   const timer2 = useRef<TimerResponse | null>(null);
30:   const onCompositionStart = usePersistFn((e: React.CompositionEvent<T>) => {
31:     if (timer.current) {
32:       clearTimeout(timer.current);
33:       timer.current = null;
34:     }
35:     if (timer2.current) {
36:       clearTimeout(timer2.current);
37:       timer2.current = null;
38:     }
39:     c.current = true;
40:     originalOnCompositionStart?.(e);
41:   });
42:   const onCompositionEnd = usePersistFn((e: React.CompositionEvent<T>) => {
43:     timer.current = setTimeout(() => {
44:       timer2.current = setTimeout(() => {
45:         c.current = false;
46:       });
47:     });
48:     originalOnCompositionEnd?.(e);
49:   });
50:   const onKeyDown = usePersistFn((e: React.KeyboardEvent<T>) => {
51:     if (
52:       c.current &&
53:       (e.key === "Escape" || (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey))
54:     ) {
55:       e.stopPropagation();
56:       return;
57:     }
58:     originalOnKeyDown?.(e);
59:   });
60:   const isComposing = usePersistFn(() => {
61:     return c.current;
62:   });
63:   return {
64:     onCompositionStart,
65:     onCompositionEnd,
66:     onKeyDown,
67:     isComposing,
68:   };
69: }

File: manus-archive-master/templates/event-template/client/src/hooks/useMobile.tsx
================
 1: import * as React from "react";
 2: const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768;
 3: export function useIsMobile() {
 4:   const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(
 5:     undefined
 6:   );
 7:   React.useEffect(() => {
 8:     const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`);
 9:     const onChange = () => {
10:       setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
11:     };
12:     mql.addEventListener("change", onChange);
13:     setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
14:     return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange);
15:   }, []);
16:   return !!isMobile;
17: }

================
File: manus-archive-master/templates/event-template/client/src/hooks/usePersistFn.ts
================
 1: import { useRef } from "react";
 2: type noop = (...args: any[]) => any;
 3: export function usePersistFn<T extends noop>(fn: T) {
 4:   const fnRef = useRef<T>(fn);
 5:   fnRef.current = fn;
 6:   const persistFn = useRef<T>(null);
 7:   if (!persistFn.current) {
 8:     persistFn.current = function (this: unknown, ...args) {
 9:       return fnRef.current!.apply(this, args);
10:     } as T;
11:   }
12:   return persistFn.current!;
13: }

5: }

 1: import { Toaster } from "@/components/ui/sonner";
 2: import { TooltipProvider } from "@/components/ui/tooltip";
 3: import NotFound from "@/pages/NotFound";
 4: import { Route, Switch } from "wouter";
 5: import ErrorBoundary from "./components/ErrorBoundary";
 6: import { ThemeProvider } from "./contexts/ThemeContext";
 7: import Home from "./pages/Home";
 8: function Router() {
 9:   return (
10:     <Switch>
11:       <Route path={"/"} component={Home} />
12:       <Route path={"/404"} component={NotFound} />
13:       {}
14:       <Route component={NotFound} />
15:     </Switch>
16:   );
17: }
18: function App() {
19:   return (
20:     <ErrorBoundary>
21:       <ThemeProvider
22:         defaultTheme="light"
23:       >
24:         <TooltipProvider>
25:           <Toaster />
26:           <Router />
27:         </TooltipProvider>
28:       </ThemeProvider>
29:     </ErrorBoundary>
30:   );
31: }
32: export default App;

 1: export { COOKIE_NAME, ONE_YEAR_MS } from "@shared/const";
 2: export const APP_TITLE = import.meta.env.VITE_APP_TITLE || "App";
 3: export const APP_LOGO =
 4:   import.meta.env.VITE_APP_LOGO ||
 5:   "https://placehold.co/128x128/E1E7EF/1F2937?text=App";
 6: export const getLoginUrl = () => {
 7:   const oauthPortalUrl = import.meta.env.VITE_OAUTH_PORTAL_URL;
 8:   const appId = import.meta.env.VITE_APP_ID;
 9:   const redirectUri = `${window.location.origin}/api/oauth/callback`;
10:   const state = btoa(redirectUri);
11:   const url = new URL(`${oauthPortalUrl}/app-auth`);
12:   url.searchParams.set("appId", appId);
13:   url.searchParams.set("redirectUri", redirectUri);
14:   url.searchParams.set("state", state);
15:   url.searchParams.set("type", "signIn");
16:   return url.toString();
17: };

 7: async function startServer() {
 8:   const app = express();
 9:   const server = createServer(app);
10:   const staticPath =
11:     process.env.NODE_ENV === "production"
12:       ? path.resolve(__dirname, "public")

17:   });
18:   const port = process.env.PORT || 3000;

22: }
